But, <u>in contrast</u>, it is only in modern times that Galileo has become a problem child for historians of science.（B4L32）
  近义搭配：
  **compared <u>with/ to</u>……** 与……相对比（L41）
  **<u>in/ by</u> comparison <u>with/ to</u>……**
  **<u>in/ by</u> contrast <u>with/ to</u>……**
  ✎ It’s as if they were, in some sense, cosmic beings <u>in</u> violent and lovely <u>contrast with</u> us suburban creatures.（B4L5）
  **A as against B is as C against D** A与B相比较，就如同C和D相比较一样
  ✎ The military power of the US, <u>as against</u> that of DPRK, <u>is as</u> the strength of an elephant <u>against</u> that of a mouse. 美国的军事力量与朝鲜的相比的话，就好比大象的力量与老鼠的相比一样。
+ **comforts** n.[pl.] 使人感觉舒适的事物
  ✎ hotels with all the <u>modern comforts</u> 配备所有现代化舒适设施的酒店
  ✎ After the trip, it was nice getting back to a few <u>home comforts</u>. 旅行结束后，回到家里几处舒适的环境中感觉很好。
+ **stretch one’s legs** 舒活筋骨
  ┏ 去散步（L19、L23）
  ┗ **take a <u>walk/ stroll</u>**
  ┗ **have a <u>walk/ stroll</u>**
  ┗ **go for a <u>walk/ stroll</u>**
  ✎ He usually <u>takes a</u> short <u>walk</u> in the evenings and is always home by seven o’clock.（L19）
  ✎ The idea never appealed to me very much, but one day, after a heavy shower, I happened to be walking in my garden when I noticed a huge number of snails <u>taking a stroll</u> on some of my prize plants.（L23）
  ✎ — What do you want to do after breakfast?
  — Why don’t we <u>take a walk</u> down to the river?（《走遍美国》）
  ✎ Phoebe: Hey, is Chandler here?
  Joey: No, no he <u>went for a walk</u>.（《老友记》）
+ **meet** 结识，结交（主动行为），~~遇见~~
  ✎ One wants to <u>meet</u> like-minded collectors, ……（L59）
+ **assuming (that) ……** 以为；假定，假如
  ① 以为
  ✎ <u>Assuming that</u> his family had been killed during an air raid, Hans settled down in a village fifty miles away where he had remained ever since.（L36）
  ② 假定，假如
  ✎ 你将用半小时到那里——当然假定路上车不多的话。
  You’ll get there in half an hour — <u>assuming</u>, of course, <u>that</u> the traffic is not heavy.
+ **transport [英]/ transportation [美]** [U] 交通方式；泛指交通工具
  **public <u>transport/ transportation</u>** 公共交通工具
  ✎ A lot of people object to mobile phones, especially when they are used in public places like restaurants or on <u>public transport</u>.（L47）

#### 👾 “最高级”的表达
1. **否定词 + 比较级 = 最高级**
  ✎ <u>Nothing</u> could have been <u>more</u> annoying.（B2L54）
  ✎ <u>No</u> creature has received <u>more</u> praise and abuse than the common garden snail.（L23）
  ✎ There is <u>no quicker</u> method of disposing of patients than by giving them what they are asking for.（B4L28）
2. ┏ **nothing can be compared with……** 没有任何事物能与……相比（L41）
   ┗ **<u>no one/ nobody</u> can be compared with……** 没有任何人能与……相比
  ✎ <u>Nothing can be compared</u>, he maintains, <u>with</u> the first cockcrow, the twittering of birds at dawn, the sight of the rising sun glinting on the trees and pastures.（L41）
3. ┏ **nothing can match sth.** 没有任何东西能与之相匹敌
   ┗ **<u>no one/ nobody</u> can match sb.**
  ✎ But <u>nothing can match</u> them for speed and comfort.（本文）
4. **<u>no one/ nobody/ nothing</u> <u>equals/ matches</u> sb.** 
  ✎ <u>Nobody equals/ matches</u> him in strength. 在力量上，没人能与他相匹敌。
5. **have no equal** 没有人能与之相匹敌
  ✎ In English she <u>has no equal</u> in her class. 在英语方面班里没有人能与她相匹敌。
6. **<u>be/ stand</u> head and shoulders above sb.** 明显超过他人，鹤立鸡群（通常指人）（习语）
  ✎ In computer programming, Susan <u>is head and shoulders above</u> the rest of us. 在计算机编程方面，苏珊比其他人强得多。
  Answer: Susan is much better than we are in this subject.（听力真题）

+ **relatively** <u>few/ easy/ new/ minor/ ……</u> 比较少/简单/新/次要
  ✎ Cave exploration, or pot-holing, as it has come to be known, is a <u>relatively new</u> sport.（L42）
+ **be prepared to do = be <u>willing/ ready</u> to do** 乐意，愿意
  ✎ Why people <u>are prepared to</u> tolerate a four-hour journey each day for the dubious privilege of living in the country is beyond me.（L41）
+ **sacrifice…… for……** 为了（某个目的-后者）而牺牲/献出（某个宝贵的东西-前者）
  ✎ Such is human nature, that a great many people are often willing to <u>sacrifice</u> higher pay <u>for</u> the privilege of becoming white-collar workers.（L4）
> 仿写第1段末句
  没有多少人愿意为了钱而牺牲掉自己作为人的尊严。
  Relatively few people are prepared to sacrifice their human dignity for money.
+ **have the reputation of being……** 有……的名声（无褒贬）
  ✎ She <u>has the reputation of being</u> a good doctor. 她以是个好医生而闻名。
  ✎ Peter <u>has the reputation of being</u> the worst boy in the class. 彼得以是班上最差的男孩而著称。
+ **hardened** a. 老练的，老资格的，见怪不怪的，麻木不仁的（L11）
  英文释义：someone who is hardened has had a lot of difficult or unpleasant experiences and is no longer much affected by such things
  ✎ The <u>hardened</u> professional smuggler, on the other hand, is never troubled by such feelings, even if he has five hundred gold watches hidden in his suitcase.（L11）
+ **have the disadvantage of……** 有……的劣势/不利之处/弊端
  ✎ He <u>has the disadvantage of</u> being unable to drive a car. 他的劣势是不会开车。
  反义搭配：
  **have the advantage of……** 有……的优势/长处
  ✎ Though she <u>has the twin advantages of</u> wealth and beauty, she doesn’t live a happy life. 虽然她拥有财富和美貌的双重优势，但她并没有过上幸福的生活。
+ **exhilarating** a. 令人极其兴奋和高兴的（书面语）
  ✎ There is nothing more <u>exhilarating</u> than to be shot at without result. 没有什么比被枪杀而没有被打死更令人兴奋的了。（丘吉尔）
+ **devise** v. 设计出，想出，构思出（L26）
  ✎ They <u>devise</u> hundreds of competitions which will enable us to win huge sums of money.（L26）
+ **settle**
  + v. 舒适地坐到……
    ✎ <u>settle back</u> in a deep armchair（本文）
    ✎ We <u>settled</u> in front of the television for the evening. 我们舒舒服服地坐在电视机前度过了一个晚上。（不及物）
    ✎ Jessica <u>settled herself</u> on the sofa with a small sigh of relief. 杰西卡舒了一口气，让自己坐在了沙发上。（及物）
  + 驻扎在某地
    ✎ Six hundred years ago, Sir John Hawkwood arrived in Italy with a band of soldiers and <u>settled</u> near Florence.（L14）
  + **settled down** 定居下来
    ✎ Assuming that his family had been killed during an air raid, Hans <u>settled down</u> in a village fifty miles away where he had remained ever since.（L36）
    ✎ He had often dreamed of retiring in England and had planned to <u>settle down</u> in the country.（B2L38）
  + 解决问题，解决争端，解决纠纷
    ✎ The two men quarrelled bitterly and it was clear that the argument could only <u>be settled</u> by a fight.（L21）
+ **escapist** n. 遁世逍遥者，逃避现实生活一心享受的人
+ **sip** 小口地抿
+ **service** n. BrE （汽车，火车，轮船，飞机等的）班次，~~服务~~
英文释义：a regular journey made by a bus, train, boat, plane etc to a particular place at a particular time
  ✎ the 8:15 <u>service</u> to Cambridge 八点十五分到剑桥的班次/班机/班车
+ **refinement** [C] 使事物变得更好的东西，改进，改良
  ✎ With several <u>refinements</u> your essay would be excellent. 只要稍加改进，你的文章就会变得很优秀。
+ **occupy** vt. 占据（时间，空间等）
  ✎ A little later, a man came along with a biscuit which <u>occupied</u> the whole boot of his car.（L26）
  ✎ Mainframe computers were very large indeed, often <u>occupying</u> whole air-conditioned rooms, employing full-time technicians and run on specially-written software.（L51）
  **occupied** a. 忙的，有事做的
  **keep sb. occupied** 使某人有事可做，不至于太无聊
  ✎ We need something to <u>keep the children occupied</u>. 我们需要一些东西来让孩子们有事做。
+ **breathtaking** a. 令人惊叹的
  **breathtakingly** ad.
  ✎ The West Lake is <u>breathtakingly</u> beautiful! 西湖有着令人惊叹的美！
  **take a…… breath** ……呼吸
  ✎ He <u>took a deep breath</u> to compose himself. 他深吸一口气，让自己镇定下来。
+ **landscape**
  n1. scenery of an area of land（陆上的）风景，景色
  n2. picture showing a view of the countryside 野外风景画
+ **prevent <u>sb./sth.</u> from doing** 防止/阻止某人/某事物，使其无法做某事
  ✎ 在新社会，每个孩子都能接受良好的教育。
  In the new society, there is nothing to <u>prevent</u> a child <u>from receiving</u> good education.
  ✎ 她既有天赋又这么勤奋，一定能实现自己的梦想。
  She is so talented and diligent that there is nothing to prevent her from fulfilling her dream.
  （参考：Despite its immensity, it is both simple and elegant, <u>fulfilling its designer’s dream</u> to create ‘an enormous object drawn as faintly as possible’. 实现梦想（L17））
> 仿写倒数第2句
  无论在前进的道路上(on our road ahead)遇到(encounter)什么样的困难，有一件事是肯定的：只要(So long as)我们坚持(persist)就一定能克服它(manage to overcome it)。
  Whatever difficulty we may encounter on our road ahead, one thing is certain: we will manage to overcome it so long as we persist.
+ **recover from……** 从……中恢复（L43）
  **recover sth.**（及物）
  ① 恢复了…… 同义词：**restore, regain**
  ② 重新获得，找回，赚回，补偿
  ✎ But the claim made by a local authority to <u>recover</u> the cost of salvaging a sunken pie dish must surely be unique.（L43）
+ **arduous** a. 艰苦的，费力的（L35）
  ✎ Justice is part of the complex machinery of the law. Those who seek it undertake an <u>arduous</u> journey and can never be sure that they will find it.（L35）

---

## **Lesson 45 - The power of the press**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>In democratic countries any efforts to restrict the freedom of the press are rightly condemned. However, this freedom can easily be abused. Stories about people often attract far more public attention than political events. Though we may enjoy reading about the lives of others, it is extremely doubtful whether we would equally enjoy reading about ourselves. Acting on the contention that facts are sacred, reporters can cause untold suffering to individuals by publishing details about their private lives. Newspapers exert such tremendous influence that they can not only bring about major changes to the lives of ordinary people but can even overthrow a government.

The story of a poor family that acquired fame and fortune overnight, dramatically illustrates the power of the press. The family lived in Aberdeen, a small town of 23,000 inhabitants in South Dakota. As the parents had five children, life was a perpetual struggle against poverty. They were expecting their sixth child and were faced with even more pressing economic problems. If they had only had one more child, the fact would have passed unnoticed. They would have continued to struggle against economic odds and would have lived in obscurity. But they suddenly became the parents of quintuplets, four girls and a boy, an event which radically changed their lives. The day after the birth of the five children, an aeroplane arrived in Aberdeen bringing sixty reporters and photographers.

The rise to fame was swift. Television cameras and newspapers carried the news to everyone in the country. Newspapers and magazines offered the family huge sums for the exclusive rights to publish stories and photographs. Gifts poured in not only from unknown people, but from baby food and soap manufacturers who wished to advertise their products. The old farmhouse the family lived in was to be replaced by a new $500,000 home. Reporters kept pressing for interviews so lawyers had to be employed to act as spokesmen for the family at press conferences. While the five babies were still quietly sleeping in oxygen tents in a hospital nursery, their parents were paying the price for fame. It would never again be possible for them to lead normal lives. They had become the victims of commercialization, for their names had acquired a market value. Instead of being five new family members, these children had immediately become a commodity.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **democratic** a. 民主的
  ✎ a <u>democratic</u> <u>country/ government/ society</u> 一个民主国家/政府/社会
  ✎ the <u>democratic</u> process 民主进程
  词根：**dem(o)**: people 人民；**crat**: ruler 统治者；**cracy**: rule 统治
  同根词：
  ◇ **democrat** 民主主义者，民主党人；**democracy** 民主，民主政体
  相关词：
  ◇ **demography** n. 人口统计，人口普查，人口学（**graphy**: write 写字）
  ◇ **epidemic** n. 流行病；流行病的爆发（**epi**: among 在……中间）
  ◇ **autocrat** n. 独裁者；**autocratic** a. 独裁的；**autocracy** 独裁，独裁政体（**auto**: self 自己的）
  ◇ **bureaucrat** （政府里的）官僚（贬）；**bureaucratic** 官僚的，官僚作风的，官僚主义的；**bureaucracy** 官僚主义，官僚制度，官僚作风（**bureau**: 政府的部局处科）
+ **restrict** v. 限制，局限
  ✎ The long skirt <u>restricted</u> her movements. 长裙限制了她的行动。（具象）
  ✎ The government passed a law to <u>restrict</u> the sale of guns. 政府通过了一项法律以限制枪支的销售。（抽象）
  **restrict…… to……** 把……限制在……范畴之内
  ✎ Access to the club <u>is restricted to</u> members only. 俱乐部仅限会员进入。
  ✎ I <u>restrict</u> myself <u>to</u> a glass of wine per day. 我限制自己每天只喝一杯葡萄酒。
  **limit…… to……** 把……限制在……范畴之内
  ✎ The air strikes <u>are limited to</u> military targets. 空袭仅限于军事目标。
  **confine…… to……** 把……限制在……范畴之内
  ✎ ……, for collectors <u>are</u> not <u>confined to</u> any one country.（L59）
+ **perpetual** a. 永恒的，长久的；没完没了的
  ✎ A <u>perpetual</u> mist hung over the valley. 山谷上空永远笼罩着薄雾。
  ✎ He soon grew tired of her <u>perpetual</u> demands for money. 他很快就厌烦了她无休无止的要钱。
  同义替换：
  **eternal**
  ✎ eternal <u>love/ life/ optimist</u> 永恒的爱/生命/乐观主义者
  ✎ the <u>eternal</u> arguments between mother and son 母子之间的没完没了的争执
  **everlasting**
  ✎ <u>everlasting</u> <u>fame/ glory/ life</u> 永远的名誉/荣耀/生命
  ✎ I’m tired of his <u>everlasting</u> complaints. 我烦透了他没完没了的抱怨。
  近义词：
  ┏ **immortal** 不朽的，流芳百世的（L17）
  ✎ Plato believed that the soul is <u>immortal</u>. 柏拉图相信灵魂是不朽的。
  ✎ the <u>immortal</u> Shakespeare 不朽的莎士比亚
  ✎ Emily Bronte’s <u>immortal</u> love story 艾米莉·勃朗特不朽的爱情故事
  ┗ **mortal** 会死的，终有一死的；致命的
  ✎ All human beings are <u>mortal</u>. 人皆终有一死。
  ✎ a <u>mortal</u> wound 一处致命的外伤
  ┏ **permanent** 长期的，固定的（L25）
  ✎ a <u>permanent</u> job 一份固定的工作
  ✎ my <u>permanent</u> address 我的固定住址
  ┗ **temporary** 临时的，暂时的
  ✎ a <u>temporary</u> job 一份临时的工作
  ✎ a <u>temporary</u> measure 一个临时措施
  ✎ <u>temporary</u> relief from pain 暂时缓和疼痛
+ **obscurity** n. 默默无闻
  **obscure** a. 默默无闻的，不起眼的；难以让人理解的（L36）
  ✎ Readers happily accepted the fact that an <u>obscure</u> maidservant was really the hero’s mother.（L36）
  多用于搭配中 ↓ 
  英 | 汉 | 英 | 汉
  ---- | ---- | ---- | ---
  **live in obscurity** | 过着默默无闻的生活 | **live in comfort** | 过着舒适的生活
  **live in peace** | 过着宁静的生活 | **live in fear** | 过着惶恐的生活
  **live in poverty** | 过着贫困的生活 | **live in luxury** | 过着奢侈的生活
  **live in happiness** | 过着幸福的生活 | **live in misery** | 过着悲惨的生活
+ **commodity** n.[C] 商品（书面语）
  ✎ agricultural <u>commodities</u> 农产品，农作物
  ✎ Coal is becoming a rare <u>commodity</u>. 煤炭正在成为一种稀缺的商品。
  **commodity prices** 物价
  ✎ <u>Commodity prices</u> fell sharply. 物价骤降。
  表示**商品**的词：
  **goods**（必须带s）
  ✎ <u>industrial/ agricultural</u> <u>goods</u> 工业商品/农产品
  **wares** n. 货物，商品（多指摆摊售卖的商品，而非商店）（是泛指，所以必须带s，较文言）（L28）
  ✎ craftspeople selling their <u>wares</u> 正出售他们货物的手工艺者
  ✎ Small boats loaded with <u>wares</u> sped to the great liner as she was entering the harbour.（L28）
  **merchandise** n.[U]（**merchant** 大商人，较文言）
  ✎ a wide selection of <u>merchandise</u> 多种选择的商品
  ✎ These tokens can be exchanged for <u>merchandise</u> in any of our stores. 这些代币可以在我们的任何商店兑换商品。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **any** 任何，任一
  其后通常跟单数名词或不可数名词，此处的efforts习惯复数，所以保留s
+ **the press/ the Press** 新闻界，报界，舆论界（L5、L31）
  ✎ This exhibition received a great deal of attention in <u>the press</u>, for though the pictures were supposed to be the work of famous artists, they had in fact been painted by Dickie.（L31）
  **(the) freedom of the press** 新闻自由
  **(the) freedom of <u>speech/ expression/ thought/ choice</u>** 言论自由/表达自由/思想自由/选择自由
  **(the) <u>press/ academic/ political/ religious</u> freedom** 新闻自由/学术自由/政治自由/宗教信仰自由
+ **rightly** ad. for a good reason 应该（L41）
  ✎ They could be saved so much misery and expense if they chose to live in the city where they <u>rightly</u> belong.（L41）
+ **condemn A <u>for/ as</u> B** 因为B而谴责A / 把A谴责为是B（大家一致地批评）（L16、L37）
  ✎ The movie <u>was condemned for</u> its sexism. 这部电影因为性别歧视而受到谴责。
  ✎ The terrorist attack <u>was condemned as</u> an act of barbarism and cowardice. 这次恐怖袭击被谴责为是野蛮和懦弱的行径。
> 仿写第1句
  在民主国家，任何限制言论自由的企图都应该受谴责。
  In democratic countries any efforts to restrict the freedom of speech are rightly condemned.
  在文明社会，任何歧视妇女的行径(act)都应该受谴责。
  In civilized society any act of discrimination against women is rightly condemned.
+ **abuse** ① 辱骂；② 虐待；③ 滥用
+ ┏ **attract attention** 吸引注意
  ┗ **receive attention** 受到关注
  ✎ This exhibition <u>received</u> a great deal of <u>attention</u> in the press, ……（L31）
  **<u>public/ media/ press</u> attention** 公众/媒体/新闻界的关注
  ✎ Her case attracted a great deal of <u>media attention</u>. 她的案件引起了媒体的广泛关注。
+ ┏ “ **far/ much/ even/ still/ yet/ ……** ”加强比较级的语气
  ┗ “ **slightly/ a little/ a bit/ ……** ”降低比较级的语气
  ✎ These days, people who do manual work often receive <u>far more</u> money than people who work in offices.（L4）
  ✎ To compensate for his unpleasant experiences in hospital, the man drank <u>a little more</u> than was good for him.（L29）
+ **it is doubtful <u>if/ whether/ (that)</u> ……** 是否……，这是非常可疑的
  ✎ <u>It is doubtful if</u> he will survive. 他能否活下来值得怀疑。
  ✎ <u>It’s doubtful whether</u> the car will last another year. 这辆车能否再使用一年值得怀疑。
  ✎ <u>It is doubtful (that)</u> the missing airmen will ever be found. 失踪的飞行员是否会被找到值得怀疑。
+ ……, it is extremely doubtful whether we **would** equally enjoy reading about ourselves **if we read about ourselves**. 虚拟语气（原文补全）
  if从句的虚拟未必会把从句写出来，常常将其省略，而暗含在上下文逻辑中，注意识别。
  ✎ To ignore this <u>would</u> be a mistake. 忽视这一点将是一个错误。
  ✎ A picnic <u>would</u> not be any fun without you. 没有你，野餐不会有任何乐趣。
  ✎ Your wife <u>would</u> not be pleased to hear you say that. 你的妻子听到你这么说是会不高兴的。
  ✎ It <u>would</u> be a shame to stay indoors on such a beautiful day. 在这么美好的一天，呆在家里真是太可惜了。
> 仿写第4句
  尽管我们可能喜欢对别人恶作剧(play jokes on……)，但是我们是否喜欢别人对我们恶作剧是极其可疑的。
  Though we may enjoy playing jokes on others, it is extremely doubtful whether we would equally enjoy others playing jokes on ourselves.
+ **act on……** 依照……行事，因为……行事
  英文释义：take action in accordance with or as a result of sth 
  ✎ She is <u>acting on</u> the advice of her lawyers. 她正在按照律师的建议行事。
  ✎ Police say they <u>acted on</u> information received. 警方表示，他们根据收到的信息采取了行动。
  ✎ <u>Acting on</u> a sudden impulse, I collected several dozen, put them in a paper bag, and took them to Robert.（L23）
+ **contention** n.(fml.) 观点，论点
  **contend** v.（某人）坚称、坚持认为
+ **untold** a. 难以估量的，数不尽的，罄竹难书的 = **immeasurable** 不可估量的
  ✎ <u>untold</u> <u>suffering/ misery/ damage/ etc.</u> 无尽的痛苦/苦难/损失等
> 仿写第5句
  父母亲依照子女应该顺从(be obedient to……)长辈(one’s elders)这一观点干涉(interfere in……)成年子女的婚烟，可能给他们的成年子女(adult offspring)造成不尽的痛苦。
  Acting on the contention that children should be obedient to their elders, parents can cause untold suffering to their adult offspring by interfering in their marriages.
+ ┏ **major** 重大的，巨大的，重要的
  ┗ **minor** 微小的，微不足道的
+ **exert…… on……** 施加某种力量于……上（L26）
  ✎ …… , for advertising <u>exerts</u> a subtle influence <u>on</u> us.（L26）
  ✎ My wife <u>exerts</u> a lot of pressure <u>on</u> me to make more money. 我妻子给我施加了很大的压力，让我赚更多的钱。
  【◐】The influence of newspapers is so great that……
  【✔】**…… exert such tremendous influence that……** ……施加如此大的影响，以至于……
> 仿写第一段末句
  宗教有如此大的影响，它们不但会给普通人的精神面貌(spiritual outlook)带来重大变化，甚至还可能决定世界的命运。
  Religions exert such tremendous influence that they can not only bring about major changes to the spiritual outlook of ordinary people but can even determine the destiny of the world.
+ **acquire fame and fortune overnight** 迅速成名获利（指人）
  ✎ With the success of their first record, they <u>acquired fame and fortune overnight</u>. 随着他们第一张唱片的成功，他们迅速成名获利了。
  **rise to fame swiftly** 迅速成名（指人）（L21）
  ✎ Mendoza <u>rose to fame swiftly</u> after a boxing match when he was only fourteen years old.（L21）
  ✎ The <u>rise to fame</u> was <u>swift</u>.（本文）
  **make a name for oneself** 成名，出名（指人）（L14）
  ✎ He soon <u>made a name for himself</u> and came to be known to the Italians as Giovanni Acuto.（L14）
  **make (the) headlines**（指事）
  **hit the headlines**（指事）
  ┏ 9-11恐怖袭击迅速成为世界新闻。
  ┗ The 9/11 terrorist attack <u>made (the) headlines</u> around the world.
  ┗ The 9/11 terrorist attack <u>hit the headlines</u> around the world.
  **<u>be/ become</u> a household <u>name/ word</u>** 是/成为了一个家喻户晓的字（指人、事物都可）
  ✎ Coca Cola <u>is a household name</u> around the world. 可口可乐是全世界家喻户晓的名字。（指事物）
  ✎ Microsoft has <u>become a household word</u>. 微软已经成为一个家喻户晓的词。（指事物）
  ✎ She <u>became a household name</u> in the 1960s. 她在20世纪60年代成为家喻户晓的人物。（指人）
  ✎ Cindy married one of her publishers and <u>became a household word</u>. 辛迪嫁给了她的一位出版商，成为了家喻户晓的人物。（指人）
+ **illustrate** vt. (用例子、图表等) 说明，阐明
  英文释义：to make the meaning of sth clearer by using examples, pictures, etc.
  ✎ To <u>illustrate</u> my point, let me tell you a little story. 为了阐明我的观点，让我给你讲一个小故事。
  ✎ The lecturer <u>illustrated</u> his point with a diagram on the blackboard. 演讲者用黑板上的图表阐明了他的观点。
  **<u>amply/ clearly/ dramatically/ graphically/ vividly</u> illustrate……**
  充分地/清楚地/戏剧性地/生动地/生动地说明……
  ✎ One example may <u>amply illustrate</u> this point. 一个例子可以充分说明这一点。
  ✎ The example of the United States <u>graphically illustrates</u> this point. 美国的例子生动地阐明了这个观点。
> 仿写第2段首句
  一个原本默默无闻的(obscure)洗发水(shampoo)迅速变得家喻户晓的例子戏剧化地说明了广告宣传的力量。
  The example of an obscure shampoo that became a household name overnight, dramatically illustrates the power of advertising.
+ of 引出某地人数
  ✎ a town <u>of</u> 11,000 inhabitants 一个有11000居民的城镇
  ✎ a city <u>of</u> six million inhabitants 一座拥有600万居民的城市
+ 【✔】As the parents had five children, life was a perpetual struggle against poverty.（原文）
  【◐】As the parents had five children, <u>they perpetually struggled against poverty</u>.（中式写法：人称主语，喜欢用动词。人称主语过多，句式结构单调；动词不如名词正式）
> 仿写第2段第3句
  基督徒的生活就是永远和自我的搏斗。
  The life of a Christian <u>is a perpetual struggle against</u> self.
  炒股(speculation in stocks)就是永远和恐惧与贪婪的搏斗。
  Speculation in stocks <u>is a perpetual struggle against</u> fear and greed.
+ **be expecting (a baby)** 怀孕的含蓄表达
  怀孕的其他表达；
  **be pregnant**（较直白）
  **conceive (a baby)**（较医学）
  **be in a family way**（较含蓄）
  **be knitting a tiny garment** 正在织一件小衣服（**knit** 针织，编织；**garment** 成衣）（较含蓄）
  怀孕的其他句子：
  ◇ When <u>is</u> your baby <u>due</u>? 你的孩子什么时候出生？
  ◇ She <u>gave birth to</u> twins. 她生了一对双胞胎。（**give birth to** 生孩子）
  ◇ She <u>abort</u>ed after 2 months. 两个月后她流产了。
  ◇ She <u>is on maternity leave</u>. 她正在休产假。（**maternity** 母亲身份；**leave** 假期）
+ ┏ **be faced with……** 面临（某个棘手的问题）
  ┗ **be confronted with……**
  ✎ ……, for then man <u>was faced with</u> a real need to understand something about the seasons.（L38）
  ✎ ……, for it is impossible to foretell the exact nature of the difficulties which will <u>confront</u> the pot-holer.（L42-主动）
  ✎ ……, and no father <u>is confronted with</u> his inability to ‘buy’ an education for his child.（B4L33-被动）

+ **pressing** a. 紧急的，急迫的
  **= urgent**
  **pressing <u>problem/ matter/ need/ etc.</u>** 紧急的问题/事务/需求等
  ✎ a <u>pressing need</u> for housing 对住房的迫切需求
  ✎ Poverty is a more <u>pressing problem</u> than pollution. 贫困是一个比污染更紧迫的问题。
+ If they <u>had</u> ^助动词^ only <u>had</u> ^使役动词^ one more child, the fact <u>would have passed</u> <u>unnoticed</u> ^主语补足语^.（原文）
  **If + S. + had done, S. + <u>would/ should/ could/ might</u> + have done**
  与过去事实相反的“if”型的虚拟语气（详见L17笔记）
+ **unnoticed** a. 无人注意的 without being noticed（通常作主语补足语）
  ✎ I tried to slip up the stairs <u>unnoticed</u>. 我试图趁没人注意溜上楼去。
  **<u>go/ pass</u> unnoticed** 不为人知地过去了（固定搭配）
  ✎ The event <u>went unnoticed</u>. 这件事悄无声息地过去了。
  ✎ Her death <u>passed unnoticed</u>. 她的死没有引起人们的注意。
  ✎ The Ombudsman’s prompt action at once put an end to an unpleasant practice which might have <u>gone unnoticed</u>.（L53）
  ✎ 我不能让这种暴行(brutality)不了了之。
  I cannot let this brutality <u>go/ pass unnoticed</u>.
  ✎ 要不是(but for)这封感谢信(letter of thanks)，这件善举可能就不为人知地过去了。
  But for the letter of thanks, the act of kindness might have <u>gone/ passed unnoticed</u>.

+ **odds** n. 困难（difficulties，常用于固定搭配）；可能性
  **<u>struggle/ fight/ battle</u> against the odds** 与困难作斗争
  **<u>beat/ overcome</u> the odds** 击败/克服困难
  **against (all) the odds** 克服（重重）困难
  ✎ The hospital’s director has been <u>battling against the odds</u> to improve patient care. 医院院长一直在与困难作斗争，以改善患者护理。
  ✎ The South Africans <u>overcame the odds</u> to beat Australia. 南非队克服重重困难击败了澳大利亚队。
  ✎ <u>Against all the odds</u> she achieved her dream of becoming a ballerina. 尽管面对极大的困难，她还是实现了当芭蕾舞演员的梦想。
+ **radically <u>change/ alter</u>……** 彻底改变……
  **radical** a. 彻底的
  ✎ Computers have <u>radically changed</u> our lives. 计算机彻底改变了我们的生活。
  ✎ Relativity and quantum mechanics have <u>radically altered</u> our picture of nature. 相对论和量子力学已经从根本上改变了我们对大自然的看法。
  ✎ <u>radical changes</u> in education 教育方面的彻底的变化
> 仿写第2段倒数第2句
  他突然间中了一千万美元的大奖(win the lottery of ……)，几乎是他年收入的100倍(100 times the amount of his annual income)，这件事彻底改变了他的生活。
  He suddenly won the lottery of ten million dollars, nearly 100 times the amount of his annual income, an event which radically changed his life.
+ The day after …… 
  **一段时间 + before/ after** 之前之后多久（before, after 作介词）
  ✎ <u>Four days</u> <u>after setting out</u>, while the Titanic was sailing across the icy waters of the North Atlantic, a huge iceberg was suddenly spotted by a lookout.（L10）
  ✎ A man who had broken his right leg was taken to hospital <u>a few weeks</u> <u>before Christmas</u>.（L29）
+ **carry** v. 刊登，播出（新闻报道等）
  英文释义：to publish or broadcast a news story
  ✎ All the papers <u>carried</u> the story the next day. 第二天，所有的报纸都刊登了这件事。
> 仿写第3段第2句
  当北京赢得了2008年奥林匹克运动会主办权的时候，电视摄像机和报纸把这一消息传遍了全世界。
  When Beijing won to right to host the 2008 Olympic Games, Television cameras and newspapers carried the news to everyone in the world.
+ **exclusive** a. 独家的，独享的（**-clu-**：关闭）
  英文释义：available or belonging only to particular people, and not shared
  **inclusive** a. 包含的，包括的
  **exclusive <u>access/ rights/ use</u>** 独家访问权/权利/使用权
  ✎ They have <u>exclusive rights</u> to market the drug in Africa. 他们拥有在非洲销售这种药物的独家权利。
  ✎ The road is for the <u>exclusive use</u> of residents. 这条路仅供居民使用。
  **exclusive <u>report/ coverage/ interview</u>** 独家报道/报道/采访
  ✎ Tune in to our <u>exclusive coverage</u> of Wimbledon. 请调台收看我们对温布尔登的独家报道。
  **be exclusive to……** 是……所独享的
  ✎ This offer <u>is exclusive to</u> readers of The Sun. 此优惠仅适用于《太阳报》的读者。
+ **pour in** 涌入（in 作副词）（**pour** 倒水）
  ✎ Letters of complaints <u>poured in</u>. 投诉信纷至沓来。
  ✎ Donations <u>poured in</u> for the earthquake victims in China. 捐赠品源源不断地涌向中国地震灾民。
  **pour <u>into/ out of</u>……** 涌入/涌出
  ✎ Crowds <u>poured into/ out of</u> the stadium. 人群涌入/涌出了体育场。
+ **advertise** a product 宣传产品
  **promote** a product 推销产品
  **develop** a product 开发产品
  **launch** a product 推出新产品
+ **be + to do** 即将……（表示将来时）（L40）
+ **press (sb.) for sth.** 迫切要求，一再敦促
  ✎ Reporters <u>pressed (him) for</u> an explanation. 记者们迫切要求（他）作出解释。
  ✎ I <u>pressed (him) for</u> his consent to our marriage. 我催促（他）同意我们的婚事。
  **be pressed for sth.** 缺乏……
  **be pressed for <u>time/ money/ cash/ space</u>** 缺乏时间/钱/现金/空间
+ ┏ **<u>act as/ serve as/ function as/ be used as</u>……** 当做……来使用（事物作主语）（L3）
  ✎ The box <u>acts as</u> a seat. 这个盒子充当座位。
  ┗ **act as……** 临时担任某种工作（本身不是做相关工作的）
  ✎ My brother speaks French — he can <u>acts as</u> interpreter. 我弟弟会说法语，他可以临时充当翻译。（职位前可不加冠词）
  ✎ Alfred the Great <u>acted as</u> his own spy, visiting Danish camps disguised as a minstrel.（B4L9）
+ **oxygen tent** n. 氧气帐，氧幕
  英文释义：a clear covering put over the head and upper body of an ill person to provide oxygen to help them breathe
+ **nursery** n. 医院的婴儿室
  英文释义：a room in a hospital where babies that have just been born are looked after
+ **pay the price for sth.** 为……付出代价
  ✎ Being recognized wherever you go is <u>the price</u> you <u>pay for</u> being famous. 无论走到哪里都会被认出来，是你为出名而付出的代价。
  ✎ Pollution is <u>the price</u> we <u>pay for</u> an overpopulated,over industrialized planet.（L47）
  相关搭配：
  ┏ **be a small price to pay for……** 对于……来说算不了什么（L15）
  ┗ **be a high price to pay for……** 对于……来说不值得/代价太高
  ✎ Giving up his job <u>was a small price to pay for</u> his children’s happiness. 辞掉他的工作，对于孩子的幸福来说算不了什么。
  ✎ Loneliness <u>is a high price to pay for</u> independence in your old age. 晚年要想独立，恐怕要付出孤独这一高昂的代价。
+ **<u>lead/ live</u> a…… life** 过着……样的生活（L9）
  ✎ They can be friendly and affectionate towards humans, but they <u>lead mysterious lives</u> of their own as well.（L9）
+ **<u>be/ become</u> the victim of……** 变成……的受害者/牺牲品
  ✎ Only when he saw that the man was actually telephoning the police did he realize that they had all <u>been the victims of</u> a hoax.（L40）
  ✎ They had become <u>the victims of</u> commercialization, for their names had acquired a market value.（本文）
  ✎ A man without an education, many of us believe, <u>is an unfortunate victim of</u> adverse circumstances, deprived of one of the greatest twentieth-century opportunities.（B4L33）
+ **commercialization** n. 商业化
  **commercialize[美]/ commercialise[英]** vt.
  [usually passive] to be more concerned with making money from sth. than about its quality, used to show disapproval 使商业化（贬义）
  ✎ Christmas has become so <u>commercialized</u>. 圣诞节变得如此商业化了。
+ **market value** n.  市场价值
  英文释义：the value of a product, building etc. based on the price that people are willing to pay for it, rather than the cost of producing it or building it
+ **instead of…… , ……** 本该……，却……
  ✎ <u>Instead of</u> becoming a doctor, however, he became a successful writer of detective stories.（L24）

---

## **Lesson 46 - Do it yourself**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>So great is our passion for doing things for ourselves, that we are becoming increasingly less dependent on specialized labour. No one can plead ignorance of a subject any longer, for there are countless do-it-yourself publications. Armed with the right tools and materials, newlyweds gaily embark on the task of decorating their own homes. Men, particularly, spend hours of their leisure time installing their own fireplaces, laying out their own gardens; building garages and making furniture. Some really keen enthusiasts go so far as to build their own computers. Shops cater for the do-it-yourself craze not only by running special advisory services for novices, but by offering consumers bits and pieces which they can assemble at home. Such things provide an excellent outlet for pent up creative energy, but unfortunately not all of us are born handymen.

Some wives tend to believe that their husbands are infinitely resourceful and can fix anything. Even men who can hardly drive a nail in straight are supposed to be born electricians, carpenters, plumbers and mechanics. When lights fuse, furniture gets rickety, pipes get clogged, or vacuum cleaners fail to operate, some women assume that their husbands will somehow put things right. The worst thing about the do-it-yourself game is that sometimes even men live under the delusion that they can do anything, even when they have repeatedly been proved wrong. It is a question of pride as much as anything else.

Last spring my wife suggested that I call in a man to look at our lawn mower. It had broken down the previous summer, and though I promised to repair it, I had never got round to it. I would not hear of the suggestion and said that I would fix it myself. One Saturday afternoon, I hauled the machine into the garden and had a close look at it. As far as I could see, it needed only a minor adjustment: a turn of a screw here, a little tightening up there, a drop of oil and it would be as good as new. Inevitably the repair job was not quite so simple. The mower firmly refused to mow, so I decided to dismantle it. The garden was soon littered with chunks of metal which had once made up a lawn mower. But I was extremely pleased with myself. I had traced the cause of the trouble. One of the links in the chain that drives the wheels had snapped. After buying a new chain I was faced with the insurmountable task of putting the confusing jigsaw puzzle together again. I was not surprised to find that the machine still refused to work after I had reassembled it, for the simple reason that I was left with several curiously shaped bits of metal which did not seem to fit anywhere. I gave up in despair. The weeks passed and the grass grew. When my wife nagged me to do something about it, I told her that either I would have to buy a new mower or let the grass grow. Needless to say our house is now surrounded by a jungle. Buried somewhere in deep grass there is a rusting lawn mower which I have promised to repair one day.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **plead**（L39）
  / | 一般过去式 | 过去分词 
  ---- | ---- | ---- 
  第1种 | pleaded | pleaded
  第2种 | pled | pled
  
  + ① vt. 以某事作为借口
    ✎ <u>plead</u> <u>ignorance/ illness/ a headache/ tiredness/ insanity</u> 以无知/得病/头疼/疲劳/精神失常为借口
    ✎ Ellie <u>pleaded</u> <u>tiredness</u> and went to bed very early. 艾莉以疲倦为借口，很早就上床睡觉了。
    ✎ He could not <u>plead</u> ignorance as his excuse; he should have known what was happening in his department.（05年六级真题）
    (A) plead; (B) resort; (C) petition; (D) reproach
  + ② vi. 恳求，请求
    **plead for sth.** 恳求得到某物
    ✎ He knelt in front of the king, <u>pleading for</u> mercy. 他跪在国王面前恳求得到宽恕。
    **plead with sb. to do sth.** 恳求某人去做某事
    ✎ I <u>pleaded with</u> him <u>to</u> stay, but he turned his back on me. 我恳求他留下来，但他拒绝了我。（**turn one’s back on sb.** 拒绝某人）
+ **ignorance** n. 无知，不知道（略贬义：应该知道却不知道）
  ✎ <u>Ignorance</u> is bliss. 无知是福。/难得糊涂。（谚语）
  **ignorant** a.
  **be ignorant of……** 不知道……
  ✎ Darwin had a phrase to describe those <u>ignorant of</u> evolution: they “look at an organic being as a savage looks at a ship, as at something wholly beyond his comprehension.”（阅读真题）
  达尔文用一句话来形容那些对进化一无所知的人：他们“看待有机体，就像野蛮人看待一艘船，就像看待完全超出他理解能力的东西一样。”
  **ignore** v. 不理睬，漠视（有意为之）（L31）
  近义词：
  **neglect** 忽视（无意为之）
  ✎ When I saw Jane, I stopped and smiled, but she <u>ignored</u> me and walked on.
  (A) refused; (B) ignored; (C) denied; (D) missed（1987考研英语27题）
  ✎ The joys of travel, having long <u>neglected</u> the disabled, are opening up to virtually anyone who has the means.（means 钱）
  (A) omitted 省略，删除; (B) missed; (C) neglected; (D) discarded 抛弃（六级真题）
+ **newlyweds** n. 新婚夫妇（L7）
  ┏ **fiancé** n. 未婚夫
  ┗ **fiancée** 未婚妻
  ┏ **husband-to-be** 未婚夫（准丈夫）
  ┗ **bride-to-be** 未婚妻（准新娘）
  ┏ **groom/ bridegroom** 新郎
  ┗ **bride** 新娘
  ┏ **bridesmaid** 女傧相；**maid of honor** 伴娘
  ┗ **groomsman** 男傧相；**best man** 伴郎
+ **novice** n. 新手，初学者
  近义词：**beginner, learner**（L33）
  ✎ The woman immediately behind the two cars happened to be a <u>learner</u>.
  + 词根：**-nov-**: new
    **novel** a. 新颖的 ✎ a <u>novel</u> idea 新奇的想法
    **novelty** n. 新鲜事物；新颖性 ✎ The car was a <u>novelty</u> in 1900. 这辆车在1900年还是个新奇的东西。
    **innovate** vi. 革新，创新 ✎ <u>innovate</u> in technique 技术创新
    **innovation** n. 革新，创新
    **renovate** v. 整修；翻新
    **renovation** n. 整修；翻新 ✎ The Imperial Palace is under <u>renovation</u>. 故宫正在翻修之中。
+ ┏ **consumer** n. 消费者，顾客（买东西买服务都可）
  ┗ **consume** v. 消费；消耗
  ┗ **consumption** n. 消费；消耗
  ┏ **customer** 顾客（通常指**买东西**而非买服务）
  ┗ **client** 客户，顾客，主顾（通常指**买服务**而非买东西）
  **patron/ regular** 老顾客，老主顾
  **subscriber** 订购者，订阅者（**subscribe** 订购，订阅）
  **bargain hunter** 淘便宜货的人（**bargain** 便宜货）（L34）
+ **creative** a. 创造性的，有创造力的
  **creativity** n. 创造性，创造力
  **inventive** a. 有创意的；善于创新的（**invent** vt. 发明）
  ┏ **imaginative** a. 富于想象力的
  ┗ **imaginary** a. 虚构的；想象中的
  **original** a. 新颖的；有原创性的；最初的
  **inspired** a. 有灵感的；受到启发的（常指艺术创作）（**inspiration** n. 灵感）
  ┏ **resourceful** a. 足智多谋的
  ┗ **full of ideas** 充满点子；足智多谋的
  ✎ She is a very <u>imaginative</u> student. She’s always talking about travelling to outer space.
  (A) imaginary; (B) imaginative; (C) imaginable; (D) imagining
+ **clog** v. （粘稠的东西）堵塞住……
  **clog sth. (up) with……** (后者) 把 (前者) 堵住（堵得死死的）
  ✎ The pipe <u>was clogged (up) with mud</u>. 管道被泥巴堵住（堵死）了。
  近义词（不强调是粘稠的东西）：
  **jam, block, obstruct** 阻塞，挡住
  ✎ A crowd of people <u>jammed/ blocked/ obstructed</u> the road. 有一群人挡住了道路。
  相关词：
  **thwart** 阻挠
  ✎ Harry knew that nothing could <u>thwart</u> his plans. 哈利知道没有什么能阻挠他的计划了。
  **hamper, hinder, impede** vt. 妨碍
  ✎ Higher interest rates could <u>hamper/ hinder/ impede</u> economic growth. 更高的利率可能会阻碍经济增长。
+ **delusion** n. 错觉
  **<u>be/ live</u> under the <u>illusion/ delusion</u> that……** 某人有某种错觉
  ✎ Even he still <u>lives under the illusion that</u> country life is somehow superior to town life.（L41）
  ✎ The worst thing about the do-it-yourself game is that sometimes even men <u>live under the delusion that</u> they can do anything, even when they have repeatedly been proved wrong.（本文）
  形近词：
  **allusion** 影射；暗指（**allude** v. 影射；暗指 **allude to**）
  **allusion to**
  ✎ He resents any <u>allusion to</u> his baldness. 他讨厌任何对他秃头的影射。
  相关词：
  **hallucination** 幻觉
  ✎ The high fever gave her <u>hallucinations</u>. 高烧使她产生了幻觉。
  **mirage** 海市蜃楼
+ **adjustment** n. 调节，调整（多表示微调）
  **make adjustments to……** 对……做一些调节/调整
  ✎ The room was full of dancers, all <u>making</u> last-minute <u>adjustments to</u> their costumes. 房间里挤满了舞者，他们都在做上台前最后的服装上的调整。
  **adjust** v. 调节，调整（多表示微调）
  **adjust (A) to B** 调整(A)以适应B
  ✎ You can <u>adjust</u> the belt <u>to</u> the size you want. 你可以把皮带调整到你想要的尺寸。（及物）
  ✎ Some animals <u>adjust</u> (themselves) <u>to</u> their environment by instinct. 有些动物本能地调整(自己)以适应环境。（不及物）
  **adapt** 调节；改编（通常表示幅度大的调整）
  **adapt (A) to B** 调整(A)以适应B
  ✎ Novels <u>are</u> often <u>adapted to</u> the stage. 小说经常被改编成舞台剧。
  ✎ She couldn’t <u>adapt</u> (herself) <u>to</u> eating fish every day. 她无法适应每天吃鱼。
  **adaptation** n. 调整，调节；改编版本
  **amend** 修订，修正（多指文字、措辞上的修改）
  ✎ <u>amend</u> a <u>bill/ rule/ law/ document</u> 修订一份法案/规章/法律/文件
  **amendment** n. 修订；修订案
+ **nag** n. 数落，唠叨
  **nag (at) sb.** 数落某人
  ✎ His wife <u>nagged (at)</u> him all day long. 他妻子成天数落他。
  **bitch at sb.**（口语，不尊重）
  ✎ Stop <u>bitching at</u> me!
  **<u>complain /moan /grouch</u> about sth.** 对某事发牢骚/抱怨
  **chatter** 喋喋不休地说
  **murmur** 轻声耳语
  **mumble** 喃喃自语，小声嘟囔（L29）
  ✎ He was still <u>mumbling</u> something about hospitals at the end of the party when he slipped on a piece of ice and broke his left leg.（L29）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ ┏ So great is our passion for doing things for ourselves, that we are becoming increasingly less dependent on specialized labour.（原文 - 副词so放到句首，表示强调，引起部分倒装）
  ┗ Our passion for doing things for ourselves <u>is so great</u> that……（正常语序 - 无法强调“so great”；头重脚轻）
+ **passion** n. 强烈情感，激情，热情
  **passion for** 对……的热情
  ✎ his passion <u>for</u> table tennis 他对乒乓球的热忱
  ✎ his passion <u>for</u> the girl 他对这个女孩的热情
  **passionate** a. 充满激情的
  名词搭配 | 译 | 形容词 | 译 
  ---- | ---- | ---- | ---- 
  enthusiasm for…… | 对于……的热情 | enthusiastic | a. 热情的
  zest for…… | ~ | zestful | a. ~
  zeal for…… | ~ | zealous | a. ~
  ardo(u)r for…… | ~ | ardent | a. ~ 

+ **do sth. for oneself** 亲自做某事，~~为自己做某事~~（L29）
  ✎ The following example of ‘sick humor’ will enable you to judge <u>for yourself</u>.（L29）
  近义搭配：
  **oneself** 自己亲自（辨：**by oneself** 独自一个人做）
  ✎ I made these curtains <u>myself</u>. 这些窗帘是我自己做的。
  **in person** 亲自
  ✎ You have to sign for it <u>in person</u>. 你必须亲自签收。
  **personally** 亲自
  ✎ The President wrote to us <u>personally</u> to thank us for our hard work. 总统亲自写信给我们，感谢我们的辛勤工作。
+ **increasingly**: more and more
  **be becoming increasingly + a.** 正在变得越来越……（固定句型）
  ✎ It <u>is</u> also <u>becoming increasingly difficult</u> to deal with the problem of traffic in towns.（考研阅读）
  ✎ As a result of all these factors, governments <u>are becoming increasingly dependent</u> on biologists and social scientists for planning the appropriate programs and putting them into effect.（2000考研-英译汉）
  因为所有这些因素，政府正在变得越来越依赖生物学家和社会科学家来规划恰当的方案并将其付诸实施。
  ✎ 有机食品正在变得越来越流行。
  Organic food <u>is becoming increasingly popular</u>.
  ✎ 人们正在变得越来越了解(aware)国家和国际间的问题。
  People <u>are becoming increasingly aware</u> of national and international issues.
+ ┏ **be dependent on……** 依赖于……
  ┗ **be independent of……** 不依赖于……（L9）
  ✎ We are becoming increasingly <u>independent of</u> specialized labor.
> 仿写首句
  我母亲住得这么远以至于我们很少(hardly ever)见到她。
  So far away does my mother live that we hardly ever see her.
  我们对因特网的热情是如此的高涨以至于我们对电视越来越没有兴趣了。
  So great is our passion for the Internet that we are becoming increasingly less interested in the television.
+ ┏ No one can plead ignorance of a subject any longer, for there are countless do-it-yourself publications.（原文）
  ┗ To plead ignorance of a subject is no longer a <u>legitimate/ justifiable</u> excuse.（原文改写）
  **legitimate, justifiable** 合情合理的
+ **<u>countless, numerous</u>** 数不胜数的，无数的，特别多的（通常修饰可数名词复数）
  ✎ There are <u>countless</u> people who, ever since their early years, have learned to associate snails with food.（L23）
  ✎ There are <u>numerous</u> people, who……（L23-课后题12）
+ **do-it-yourself** publications（短语+连字符 → 复合形容词）
  **take-home** pay 税后工资
  a **can’t-be-put-down** book 一本令人爱不释手的书
  a **wait-and-see** policy 一项观望的政策
  a **good-for-nothing** man 一个一无是处的男人
+ **Armed with** the right tools and materials, newlyweds gaily embark on the task of decorating their own homes.（原文-非谓语动词作方式状语）
  ✎ <u>Armed with</u> a torch, the vicar went up into the clock tower to see what was going on.（L2）
+ **right** tools 合适的，~~正确的~~
+ **materials** [pl.] 材料，素材
  ✎ <u>reading/ writing/ building</u> <u>materials</u> 阅读材料/写作素材/建材
+ **gaily** ad. 兴高采烈地，开心地 = **cheerfully, happily, joyfully**
  **gay** a. 高兴的，开心的；同性恋的（**homosexual** 同性恋的）
  【✔】He is <u>gay</u>.
  【✘】He is a <u>gay</u>.
  **lesbian** 女同性恋的
  **bisexual** 双性恋的
  **heterosexual, straight** 异性恋的
+ **embark on……** ② 开始（某个工作或任务）；① 上船，上飞机，上火车等（本义）（L28）
  ✎ We <u>embarked on</u> the ship for Shanghai. 我们登船启程赴上海。
  同义替换：
  **start on sth.**
  **set about sth.**
  反义搭配：
  **disembark from……** 下船，下飞机，下火车等（通常不翻译成“结束任务”）
  ✎ Passengers began to <u>disembark from</u> the ferry. 乘客们开始从渡船上下船登岸。（**ferry** 渡轮，渡口）
+ **particularly** ad. 尤其，特别
  同义替换：
  **especially, in particular**
+ **leisure time** 业余时间
+ **lay out……**
  ① 把……摊开/摆放开
  ✎ While they were <u>laying</u> it <u>out</u> on the decks.（L28课后题-1b）
  ✎ <u>Lay out</u> the map on the table and let’s have a look.
  ② 布置 = **arrange**
  ✎ Diamond necklaces and rings had <u>been</u> beautifully <u>arranged</u> on a background of black velvet.（L6）
  ✎ The gardens <u>were laid out</u> with lawns and flower beds. 花园里布置了草坪和花坛。
+ **so…… as to do** 如此……以至于……
+ **far** 程度，~~距离远~~
  ✎ I can only trust him so <u>far</u>. 我信任他只能信任到这个程度。
  ✎  — I got a surprise for you.
  — Yeah? I got one for you too. I’ve watched you do business for years, but I thought there was a limit to how sick you could…… How could you, Linus? How could you do what you did to me and to her? How could you <u>go that far</u>? What the hell makes you think you have the right? 到这样的程度
  — Habit.（《情归巴黎 Sabrina》 (1995)）
  ✎ <u>as/ so</u> far as I know 据我所知
  ✎ <u>as/ so</u> far as I can remember 据我能够回忆起来的
  ✎ <u>as/ so</u> far as I can see 依我看
+ **build** 组装 = **assemble**
+ **cater for……** 迎合……
  ✎ Schools often fail to <u>cater for</u> the needs of gifted children. 学校往往无法满足天才儿童的需求。
  ✎ It is a resort that clearly <u>caters for</u> the well-off. 这是一个明显迎合富人的度假胜地。
+ **craze** 狂热，热潮 = **fad, mania**
  **crazy** 疯狂的
+ **run** 开设、提供某种课程或服务
  ✎ The college <u>runs</u> summer courses. 这所学院开设暑期课程。
+ ser**vices** for no**vices**（learner, beginner）（尾韵）
  ✎ the in<u>stitute</u> for the de<u>stitute</u>（poor）平民学院
  ✎ H<u>aste</u> makes w<u>aste</u>. 欲速则不达（谚语）
  ✎ Man pro<u>poses</u>, God dis<u>poses</u>. 谋事在人，成事在天。
  ✎ Genius is one percent in<u>spiration</u> and ninety-nine percent per<u>spiration</u>.（sweat） — Thomas Edison
  天才就是百分之一的灵感加上百分之一的汗水。 — 托马斯·爱迪生
+ **outlet** n. （精力、强烈情感等的）发泄的途径；排水孔，排气孔（outlets 折扣经销店）
  英文释义：means of releasing energy, strong feelings, etc.
  **outlet for……**
  ✎ Children need an <u>outlet for</u> their energy. 孩子们需要一个发泄精力的途径。
+ **pent-up** a. （情感、精力等）被压抑的，郁积的
  英文释义：pent-up feelings or energy have not been expressed or used for a long time
  ✎ He needs an <u>outlet for</u> all that <u>pent-up</u> anger. 他需要一个发泄长期被压抑的愤怒的途径。
+ **not 与 all, every, everything, everyone, both连用多表示部分否定**
  ✎ <u>All</u> that glitters is <u>not</u> gold. 闪光的不都是金子。（莎士比亚《威尼斯商人》）
  ✎ <u>Every</u> machine here is <u>not</u> produced in our plant. 这里的机器并非每一台都是我们工厂生产的。
  ✎ <u>Both</u> of the substances do <u>not</u> dissolve in water. 这两种物质并不都能溶于水。
+ ┏ **born + n.**（表示出生时的状态）
  ┗ **die + n.**（表示死亡时的状态）
  ✎ He was born <u>an idiot</u>. 他生来就是个傻子。
  ✎ He was born <u>idiotic</u>. ~
  ✎ He died <u>a beggar</u>. 他死的时候是个乞丐。
  ✎ He died <u>poor</u>. 他在贫困中死去了。
+ **tend to do** 往往，常常，倾向于做某事（辨：**intend to do** 打算做某事）
  ✎ Women <u>tend to</u> live longer than men. 女性寿命往往比男性更长。
  **have a tendency to do** 往往，常常，倾向于
  ✎ Women <u>have a tendency to</u> live longer than men.
+ **drive** v. 钉，钉进去
  ✎ <u>drive</u> the posts into the ground 把木桩钉到地里
+ **straight** 笔直地，直直地；立即，立刻，不耽搁
  ✎ She had told him to come <u>straight</u> in if ever she failed to open the door and to leave the bread on the kitchen table.（L13）
  ✎ M: We thought we’d all go out for lunch today. Can you be ready to leave at one o’clock?
  W: I have to pick up my car and do a couple of other errands. So I’ll just come <u>straight</u> to the restaurant.
  Q: What will the woman do?
  Answer: Meet her friends at the restaurant.（托福听力真题）
+ **be supposed to <u>do/ be sth.</u>** 被认为做某事/是某事物
+ **born** a. 天生的
  ✎ He is a <u>born</u> <u>leader/ musician</u>. 他是一个天生的领袖/音乐家。
  同义替换：
  **gifted, talented**
  ✎ Picasso was one of the most <u>gifted/ talented</u> artists. 毕加索是最有天赋的艺术家之一。
  ┏ **have a gift for sth.** 在某方面有天赋/才华
  ┗ **have an aptitude for sth.**（**aptitude** 天赋）
  ✎ <u>have a gift/ an aptitude for</u> <u>languages/ painting/ music/ dancing/ etc.</u> 有语言/绘画/音乐/舞蹈等天赋
+ **rickety** 摇摇晃晃的（尤指木制家具、楼梯等） = **shaky**
+ **assume** v. 假定（贬义，通常指没有证据，暗示是错的、不合理的）
+ **somehow**
  + ① ad1. 以某种方式 in some way, or by some means, although you do not know how
    ✎ Don’t worry, we’ll get the money back <u>somehow</u>. 别担心，我们会设法把钱要回来的。
  + ② ad2. 不知怎么搞地，出于未知的原因 for a reason that you do not know or understand（L1）
    ✎ <u>Somehow</u>, I don’t feel I can trust him. 不知怎么的，我觉得我不能相信他。
    ✎ ……, this one must have been in the possession of a private collector and <u>somehow</u> managed to escape.（L1）
    ✎ And I couldn’t remember what it felt like when I could not walk down the street without holding her hand. I mean she was the same woman I fell in love with, she hadn’t changed. But <u>somehow</u> everything’s different. We’d lost something along the way.（《遗愿清单》）
+ ┏ **put…… <u>right/ in order</u>** 使……恢复正常（习语）
  ┗ **put…… out of order** 使……出故障
  ✎ As the floods had <u>put</u> the telephone <u>out of order</u>, we could not find out how they were managing.（L56）
+ **a question of……** ……的问题
  ✎ She is so diligent and talented that her success is only <u>a question of</u> time. 她如此勤奋和有天赋，以至于她的成功只是时间问题。
  ✎ There would definitely be some job losses; it was just <u>a question of</u> how many. 肯定会有一些人失业；只是人数多少的问题。
  同义替换：
  **a matter of……**
  ✎ <u>a matter of</u> time 时间问题
  ✎ <u>a matter of</u> life <u>and/ or</u> death 关乎生死的问题
  ✎ <u>a matter of</u> personal taste 个人品味的问题
  ✎ I can’t take the money. It is <u>a matter of</u> principle. 我不能接受这笔钱。这是一个原则问题。
+ **as…… as anything (else)** [英] [口] 非常大、多等（加强语气）
  ✎ It’s <u>as</u> easy <u>as anything (else)</u> 这件事情很容易
  ✎ He’s <u>as</u> fat <u>as anything (else)</u> 他特别胖
+ **call <u>sb. 🗘 in</u>** 叫某人来帮忙
  英文释义：to ask sb. to come and help you with a difficult situation
  ✎ Your father is very sick. You’d better <u>call in</u> a doctor at once. 你爸爸病得很重。你最好马上请医生来帮忙。
+ **look at……**（look v.）检查……，~~看……~~ = **examine……**
  **have a look at……**（look n.）
  **have a close look at……** 仔细地检查……
+ **get <u>round/ around</u> to <u>sth. /doing sth.</u>** 有时间（找到时间）做某事（to作介词，后接名词或动名词）（round [英]；around [美]）
  ✎ W: I’m having trouble slicing the bread with this knife.（**slice** n. 薄薄的一片；v. 切成片）
  M: Oh. Sorry about that. I haven’t <u>gotten around to</u> sharpening it yet.
  Q: What can be inferred about the knife?
  Answer: It’s dull.（老托福听力片段）
+ **not hear of sth.** 不同意某事，~~没听见/没听说过某事~~
  ✎ I wanted to pay but she <u>wouldn’t hear of</u> it. 我想付钱，但她不肯。
  ┏ I would not hear of the suggestion and……（原文）
  ┗ I would not hear of the suggestion <u>that I **call** in a man to look at our lawn mower</u>.（展开成同位语从句）
+ ┏ …… and had a close look at it.（原文）
  ┗ …… and examined it carefully（同义表达）
+ as far as I can see 在我看来
+ **as good as……**（L2）
  ① 几乎，差不多，像……一样 = **almost, nearly**
  ✎ The injured man is <u>as good as</u> dead. 这个病人奄奄一息。
  ✎ Everything is <u>as good as</u> settled. 每件事都差不多解决了。
  ② 像……一样好
  ✎ Thirteen is not <u>as good as</u> one, but it’s better than nothing.（L2）
+ The **mower** firmly refused to **mow**, ……
  用词重复，增强对比。
  ┏ The <u>waiter</u> refused to <u>wait on</u> us. 服务员拒绝为我们服务。
  ┗ The waiter refused to serve us.
  ✎ If we see the <u>unutterable</u>, it is unwise to try to <u>utter</u> it, ……（B4L24）
  ✎ We only <u>help</u> those who really need <u>help</u>. 我们只帮助那些真正需要帮助的人。
+ ┏ ……, so I decided to <u>dismantle it</u>.（原文）
  ┗ ……, so I decided to <u>take it apart</u>.（同义替换）
+ **chunk** n. 大块（牛肉、面包等）
+ **be <u>littered/ cluttered</u> with……** 杂乱地堆满了……（L28？，L39）
  ✎ The floor <u>was littered/ cluttered with</u> broken glass. 地板上堆满了碎玻璃。
  ✎ Even though the road <u>was littered with</u> boulders and pitted with holes, Bruce was not in the least perturbed.（L39）
  **litter, clutter** v. 堆满
  ✎ Broken glass <u>littered/ cluttered</u> the floor. 碎玻璃堆满了地板。
  ✎ There is always hope that in its labyrinth of musty, dark, disordered rooms a real rarity will be found amongst the piles of assorted junk that <u>litter</u> the floors.（L34）
+ **be pleased with……** 对……很开心/满意
  ✎ Robert <u>was</u> delighted to see me and equally <u>pleased with</u> my little gift.（L23）
  ✎ I <u>felt</u> especially <u>pleased with</u> my wonderful bargain — until I got back to the ship.（L28）
+ **trace** 找到（尤指循着蛛丝马迹找到元凶/根源） = **track down**
  ✎ The president vowed to <u>trace/ track down</u> those responsible for the bombing. 总统发誓要找到为爆炸事件负责的人。
+ ┏ **be faced with……** 面临（某个棘手的问题）（L38，L45）
  ┗ **be confronted with……**
  ✎ China <u>is faced/ confronted with</u> the problem of overpopulation. 中国面临着人口过剩的问题。
+ **insurmountable** a. 不能克服的，难以应付的
+ ┏ **for the simple reason that……** 只不过是因为……（较后者更正式）
  ┗ **simply because……**
  ✎ People who work in offices are frequently referred to as ‘white-collar workers’ <u>for the simple reason that</u> they usually wear a collar and tie to go to work.（L4）
+ **leave sb. with sth.** 把某物留给某人
+ **shaped** 某种形状的
  ✎ curiously <u>shaped</u> 奇形怪状的
  ✎ <u>Oddly shaped</u> forms that are suspended form the ceiling and move in response to a gust of wind are quite familiar to everybody. 奇形怪状的（L18）
+ **fit** 装进去 = **go**
  ✎ The key won’t <u>fit/ go</u> in the lock. 钥匙插不进锁里。
+ **in despair** 绝望地（despair 作名词）（L7）
  ✎ He killed himself <u>in despair</u>. 他绝望地自杀了。/他在绝望中自杀了。（自译）
  ✎ With this faith, we will be able to hew out of <u>the mountain of despair</u> a stone of hope. 有了这个信仰，我们就能从绝望的大山中砍下一块希望的石头。（马丁路德金演讲《我有一个梦想》）
  **despair of <u>n./ doing</u>** 对某事/对做某事很绝望（despair 作动词）
  ✎ The teachers began to <u>despair of</u> him. 老师们已经开始对他绝望了。
  ✎ Mike <u>despaired of</u> ever seeing her again. 麦克对再次见到女孩已经绝望了。
+ **pass**（时间的）流逝 = **<u>go by/ elapse</u>**
  ◇ The weeks <u>passed</u> and the grass <u>grew</u>.（原文）都是单音节，音韵和谐。
  ✎ An <u>idle</u> youth, a <u>needy</u> age. 少壮不努力，老大徒伤悲。（谚语）
+ ┏ **Needless to say……** 不用说也能知道……（L36）
  ┗ **As you can imagine, ……**  正如你能想象到的那样
+ **be surrounded by** 被……所包围

---

## **Lesson 47 - Too high a price?**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Pollution is the price we pay for an overpopulated, overindustrialized planet. When you come to think about it, there are only four ways you can deal with rubbish: dump it, burn it, turn it into something you can use again, attempt to produce less of it. We keep trying all four methods, but the sheer volume of rubbish we produce worldwide threatens to overwhelm us.

Rubbish, however, is only part of the problem of polluting our planet. The need to produce ever-increasing quantities of cheap food leads to a different kind of pollution. Industrialized farming methods produce cheap meat products: beef, pork and chicken. The use of pesticides and fertilizers produces cheap grain and vegetables. The price we pay for cheap food may be already too high: Mad Cow Disease (BSE) in cattle, salmonella in chicken and eggs, and listeria in dairy products. And if you think you’ll abandon meat and become a vegetarian, you have the choice of very expensive organically-grown vegetables or a steady diet of pesticides every time you think you’re eating fresh salads and vegetables, or just having an innocent glass of water!

However, there is an even more insidious kind of pollution that particularly affects urban areas and invades our daily lives, and that is noise. Burglar alarms going off at any time of the day or night serve only to annoy passers-by and actually assist burglars to burgle. Car alarms constantly scream at us in the street and are a source of profound irritation. A recent survey of the effects of noise revealed (surprisingly?) that dogs barking incessantly in the night rated the highest form of noise pollution on a scale ranging from 1 to 7. The survey revealed a large number of sources of noise that we really dislike. Lawn mowers whining on a summer’s day, late-night parties in apartment blocks, noisy neighbours, vehicles of all kinds, especially large container trucks thundering through quiet village, planes and helicopters flying overhead, large radios carried round in public places and played at maximum volume. New technology has also made its own contribution to noise. A lot of people object to mobile phones, especially when they are used in public places like restaurants or on public transport. Loud conversations on mobile phones invade our thoughts or interrupt the pleasure of meeting friends for a quiet chat. The noise pollution survey revealed a rather surprising and possibly amusing old-fashioned source of noise. It turned out to be snoring! Men were found to be the worst offenders. It was revealed that 20% of men in their mid-thirties snore. This figure rises to a staggering 60% of men in their sixties. Against these figures, it was found that only 5% of women snore regularly, while the rest are constantly woken or kept awake by their trumpeting partners. Whatever the source of noise, one thing is certain: silence, it seems, has become a golden memory.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **overpopulated** a. 人口过多的
  + **over** 过分……
    **overworked** 工作负担太重的
    **overdressed** 着装过分正式的
    **overestimated** 被高估的（**overestimate** v. 高估）
    **overcrowded** 过分拥挤的
    **overcooked** 烹饪过火的
    **over-industrialized** 过分工业化的
    **overpopulated** 人口过剩的（**overpopulation** 人口过剩）
    ✎ China is faced with the problem of <u>overpopulation</u>. 中国面临着人口过剩的问题。
  + **populate** v. （人口）生活于，居住于
    ┏ <u>densely/ thickly populated</u> regions 人口稠密地区
    ┗ <u>sparsely/ thinly populated</u> regions 人口稀疏地区
+ **overwhelm** v. 大水淹没某地（本义）
  ✎ The village **was overwhelmed by** floods. 村子被洪水淹没了。
  派生义：
  ◇ **be overwhelmed <u>with/ by</u>** <u>grief/ despair/ excitement/ ……</u> 沉浸在悲痛/绝望/兴奋中
  ◇ **be overwhelmed by** 到处充满了人/事物
  ✎ In June the town **is overwhelmed by** tourists. 在6月，该城到处都是游客。
  其他派生义举例：
  ✎ I <u>feel</u> a little bit <u>overwhelmed by</u> work. 我觉得我有点忙不过来了。
  ✎ Her beauty completely <u>overwhelmed</u> him. 她的美貌让他神魂颠倒。
  ✎ Government troops have <u>overwhelmed</u> the rebels. 政府军已经击溃了叛军。
  同根词：
  **overwhelming** a. 压倒性的，势不可挡的
  ✎ an <u>overwhelming</u> victory 压倒性的胜利
  ✎ the <u>overwhelming</u> majority 绝大多数（固定搭配）
+ **insidious** a. 潜在的，潜伏的，暗中为害的
  ✎ an <u>insidious</u> disease 一个潜伏性的疾病
  ✎ <u>insidious</u> jealousy 按藏于心的妒忌
  + 词根 **-sid- / -sed-** : sit
    **as<u>sid</u>uous, <u>sed</u>ulous** 勤奋的，勤劳的（通常指伏案工作，如学生、科学家、作家等，不指体力工作者）
    **<u>sed</u>ative** 镇静剂；**<u>sed</u>iment** 沉淀物
    **pre<u>sid</u>e** v. 主持（会议）；掌管（机构）；**pre<u>sid</u>ent** 总统，主席，院长
    **re<u>sid</u>e** 居住在；定居于；**re<u>sid</u>ence** 住宅，住所
    **sub<u>sid</u>e** 平息，减弱；**sub<u>sid</u>iary** 附属的；辅助的；次要的
    ✎ I wanna hold you till I die, till we both break down and cry. I wanna hold you till the fear in me <u>subsides</u>.（**break down and cry** 抑制不住感情而哭了出来（习语））（Rod Stewart《Sometimes When We Touch》）
+ **profound** a. 深刻的，深远的；极度的
  **= deep**
  ✎ a <u>profound</u> <u>effect/ influence/ impact</u> 深远的影响
  ✎ a <u>profound</u> poem 深奥的诗
  ✎ a <u>profound</u> question 有深度的问题
  ✎ <u>profound</u> sadness 极度的悲伤
  ✎ <u>profound</u> irritation 极度的烦躁
+ **maximum** a. 最大的
  ✎ <u>maximum</u> <u>amount + [U]/ number + [C]</u> 最大量
  ✎ <u>maximum</u> temperature 最高温度
  ✎ <u>maximum</u> voltage 最高电压
  **maximize** vt. 使最大化
  ✎ to <u>maximize</u> profits 使利润最大化
  ✎ to <u>maximize</u> windows 使窗口最大化（指电脑程序窗口）
  **maximization** n. ……的最大化
  ✎ the <u>maximization</u> of profits 利润的最大化
  反义词：
  **minimum** a. 最小的
  ✎ <u>minimum</u> wage 最低工资
  **minimize** vt. 使最小化
  ✎ to <u>minimize</u> the civilian casualties 使平民的伤亡最小化/尽量减少平民伤亡
  **minimization** n. ……的最小化
+ **mobile** 英 /ˈməʊbaɪl/; 美 /ˈmoʊbl/ a. 可移动的
  ✎ <u>mobile</u> home 可移动式住宅
  ✎ <u>mobile</u> library 可移动式图书馆
  ✎ <u>mobile</u> phone 可移动式电话，手机（美：<u>cell/ cellular</u> phone）
  + **ile**发音的英美区别
    **host<u>ile</u>** a. 有敌意的，不友好的
    **doc<u>ile</u>** a. 温顺的
    **fert<u>ile</u>** a. 肥沃的
    **frag<u>ile</u>** a. 易碎的
    **fut<u>ile</u>** a. 徒劳的
    **infant<u>ile</u>** a. 婴儿的；幼稚的
    **juven<u>ile</u>** 青少年（的）（法律用语）
    **miss<u>ile</u>** 导弹（的）
    **ag<u>ile</u>** a. 敏捷的
    **rept<u>ile</u>** n. 爬行动物

+ **snore** v. 打呼噜，打鼾
  相近词辨析：
  **sneeze** 打喷嚏；**sniff** 吸鼻子（闻东西；抽泣）；**gasp** 喘气（尤指由于惊讶或疼痛）
  **sigh** 叹气；**yawn** 打哈欠
  **blow one’s nose** 擤鼻涕
  **clear one’s throat** 清嗓子
  **break wind** 放屁 ；**fart** 放屁（书面语）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **环境污染相关常用句型**
  表达严重性：
  ◇ Environmental pollution **is becoming increasingly serious**.（参考L46）
  ◇ Environmental pollution **is a serious <u>problem/ issue</u>**.
  ◇ Environmental pollution **is a global <u>problem/ issue</u>**.
  ◇ Environmental pollution **is an issue that crosses the national boundaries**.（**boundary** 边界；边境）
  表达关注度：
  ◇ We should **pay attention to the issue of** environmental pollution.
  ◇ We should **show concern for** environmental pollution.
  ◇ We should **attach more <u>importance/ significance</u> to the issue of** environmental pollution.
  ◇ We should **make efforts to tackle the problem of** environmental pollution.
+ **be the price sb. pay for……** 某物是某人为……而付出的代价
  ✎ 沙尘暴(dust storm)是我们为过度砍伐(tree felling)付出的代价。
  Dust storms <u>are the price we pay for</u> excessive tree felling.
  ✎ 这次事故是他为疏忽(negligence)付出的代价。
  The accident <u>is the price he pays for</u> his negligence.
  ┏ **be a small price to pay for sth.** 对于……来说算不了什么（L15）
  ✎ 损失点钱对于提高地位来说算不了什么。
  The loss of money <u>is a small price to pay for</u> the rise in status.
  ┗ **be a high price to pay for sth.** 对于……来说不值得/代价太高
  ✎ 为了成功牺牲健康不值得。
  The sacrifice of health <u>is a high price to pay for</u> success.
+ **come to do** 开始做某事
  ✎ Future historians will be in a unique position when they <u>come to</u> record the history of our own times.（L38）
+ 表达**列举**的重要句型
  **① there are…… <u>ways/ kinds/ sorts/ types/ categories/ classes/ ……</u>**
  ✎ <u>There are</u> three <u>categories of</u> accommodation: economical, standard and deluxe. 住宿分为三类：经济型、标准型和豪华型。
  **② fall into…… categories** 分……种类
  ✎ Shakespeare’s plays <u>fall into</u> three <u>categories</u>: tragedies such as Hamlet, comedies such as The Merchant of Venice and histories such as Henry IV.（history [U] 历史；[C] 历史剧）
  **③ be divided into…… classes** 被分成……类（B4L46）
  ✎ Broadly speaking, human beings may <u>be divided into</u> three <u>classes</u>: those who are toiled to death, those who are worried to death,and those who are bored to death.（B4L46）
+ ┏ **deal with** rubbish 处理
  ┗ **dispose of** <u>rubbish/ garbage</u>（同义替换）
  ┗ <u>rubbish/ garbage</u> <u>disposal</u> 垃圾处理（名词搭配）
+ ┏ turn it into something you can use again（原文）
  ┗ <u>recycle</u> it（同义表达）
+ **sheer** a. 纯粹的；语气词-强调数量之大
  **the sheer volume of sth.** 巨量的/海量的某物
  **the sheer size of sth.** 巨大的某物（面积、体积等）
  ✎ <u>The sheer size of</u> the country makes communications difficult. 该国巨大的面积，使得交通有些困难/不便。
+ **threaten to do** ① 威胁说…… (人作主语)；② 有……的危险 (事物作主语)（L40）
  ✎ They <u>threatened to</u> kill him if he didn’t obey. 他们威胁说，如果他不服从，就杀了他。
  ✎ Mining operations <u>threaten to</u> destroy our environment. 采矿活动有毁掉我们的环境的危险。
  主语不同，含义不同：
  **promise to do** ① 承诺/答应做某事 (人作主语)；② 有……的可能 (事物作主语) 
  ✎ He <u>promised to</u> call me every week. 他答应每周给我打电话。
  ✎ It <u>promises to</u> be warm today. 今天可能会很暖和。
+ **part of**（L35）
  **当“part of”之前没有形容词修饰时，通常不加不定冠词“a”**
  ✎ Justice is <u>part of</u> the complex machinery of the law.（L35）
  ✎ This idyllic pastoral scene is only <u>part of</u> the picture.（L41）
  ✎ Memory loss is <u>a **normal** part of</u> the aging process. 记忆力的丧失是衰老过程中一个很正常的部分。（aging 衰老，老化）

+ **ever-doing结构** a. 不断……的（L38）
  the **ever-changing** world 不断变化的世界
  the **ever-growing** knowledge  不断增长的知识
  the **ever-developing** economy  不断发展的经济
  the **ever-expanding** market 不断扩张的市场
  the **ever-deepening** reform 不断深化的改革
  the **ever-dwindling** resources 不断缩减的资源（**dwindle** vi.(fml.) 缩减，慢慢变少）
  **ever-increasing** 不断增加的
  ✎ 满足人们不断增长的物质和文化生活需求的需要
  the need to satisfy people’s <u>ever-increasing</u> demands for material and cultural life
+ **lead to** 通往、到达；导致
  ✎ Hundreds of steps <u>lead to</u> the high wall which surrounds the president’s palace.（L5）
  ✎ This <u>led to</u> yet another angry argument.（L33）
+ **farming** 养殖，~~耕种，种植~~
  pig farming 养猪；cattle farming 养牛；chicken farming 养鸡；poultry farming 家禽养殖；livestock farming 家畜养殖
  **farm** v.
  farmed fish 养殖鱼；farmed shrimp 养殖虾
+ **produce** cheap meat **products**
  用同词根/同源的词，以押韵
  ✎ assist <u>burglars</u> to <u>burgle</u>（本文）
  ✎ <u>live</u> a…… <u>life</u>
  ✎ <u>sing</u> a <u>song</u>
  ✎ <u>breathe</u> one’s last <u>breath</u> 咽下最后一口气（气绝身亡）
  ✎ <u>die</u> a glorious <u>death</u>  死得光荣
+ **chicken** [C] 小鸡；[U] 鸡肉
  【✔】eat <u>chicken</u> 吃鸡肉
  【✘】eat <u>chicken**s**</u> 吃小鸡
  类似单词：
  **lamb**  [C] 小羊羔；[U] 羔羊肉
  **turkey** [C] 火鸡；[U] 火鸡肉
  **duck** [C] 鸭子；[U] 鸭子肉
  **lobster**  [C] 龙虾；[U] 龙虾肉
  **……**
+ **the price sb. pay for……** 某人为……而付出的代价
  ✎ Pollution is <u>the price we pay for</u> an overpopulated, over-industrialized planet.（本文）
  **at…… price**
  price表示代价，常与介词at搭配
  ✎ The precious information came <u>at a price</u>. 这份宝贵的信息是付出代价的。
  ✎ The precious information came <u>at a heavy price</u>. 这份宝贵的信息付出了极大的代价。
  ✎ She is determined to have a child <u>at any price</u>. 她决心不惜一切代价要一个孩子。
  **at the expense of……** 以损害……为代价
  ✎ Military strength is often achieved <u>at the expense of</u> a country’s economic health. 军事实力的取得往往是以损害一个国家的经济健康为代价的。
  ✎ The Roosevelt Administration believed that rebuilding the nation’s soil was in the national interest and was not simply a plan to help farmers <u>at the expense of</u> other citizens.（六级阅读真题片段）
  罗斯福政府认为，重建国家的土壤符合国家利益，而不仅仅是以损害其他公民为代价帮助农民的计划。（**in…… interest** 为了……的利益）
+ **BSE** 疯牛病（bovine spongiform encephalopathy）
  其他疾病名称缩写：
  **AIDS** 艾滋病（Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome）
+ **cattle** [pl.] 牛（可数名词，本身即复数）
  【✘】a <u>cattle</u>
  【✔】two <u>cattle</u>
  同类型词：**people, police**
+ **dairy** 牛奶公司；乳品店
  ✎ <u>dairy</u> products 奶制品；<u>dairy</u> cattle 奶牛
  形近词：
  **diary** 日记 ✎ keep a <u>diary</u> 记日记
  形近词举例（字母相同，但排列顺序不同）：
  ┏ **angle** 角，角度
  ┗ **angel** 天使
  ┏ **altitude** 海拔高度
  ┗ **latitude** 纬度（**longitude** 经度）
  ┏ **aboard** 在船上，在飞机上
  ┗ **abroad** 在国外，到国外
> 仿写第2段第5句
  我们为人口过多付出的代价可能已经太高了：失业现象，各种各样的污染，以及越来越多的(ever-increasing)犯罪。
  The price we pay for overpopulation may be already too high: unemployment, pollution of all kinds, and the ever-increasing crime.
+ **have the choice of A or B** 在A和B之间选一个
+ **organically-grown** 有机栽培的
  ✎ <u>organically-grown</u> vegetables  有机栽培的蔬菜
  ✎ <u>organically-grown</u> produce 有机栽培的农作物（**product** 产品）
  相关词：
  **environment-friendly** 环保的，对环境无害的
  ✎ <u>environment-friendly</u> products 环保产品
+ **steady** 稳定的，持续不断的
  ✎ a <u>steady</u> <u>job/ income</u> 一份稳定的工作/收入
  ✎ a <u>steady</u> relationship 一段稳定的关系
  ✎ a <u>steady</u> <u>boyfriend/ girlfriend</u> 关系稳定的男/女朋友
  ✎ a <u>steady</u> <u>decline/ increase</u> 稳定的下降/上升
+ **every time (when) ……** 每一次，每当（既可以看作连词，引导时间状语从句；也可看作名词，作状语，其后是省略when的定语从句）
  **= whenever……**
  **= no matter when……**
+ **innocent** a. 无害的，无毒的 = **harmless, innocuous**
> 仿写第2段末句
  如果你想放弃开车，那么你可以两者选一：或者是慢得出奇(extraordinarily slow)的公共汽车，或者是过分拥挤(over-crowded)的地铁。
  If you think you’ll abandon the car, you have the choice of the extraordinarily slow buses or the over-crowded subway.

> 仿写第3段首句
  有一种更为隐蔽有害的侵略，它尤其影响人们的思维模式(mode of thought)并侵犯当地的传统，那就是文化侵略。
  There is an even more insidious kind of aggression that particularly affects people’s mode of thought and invades local tradition, and that is cultural aggression.

+ **go off** 发出巨大的、刺耳的声音（如警报声、枪炮声、闹铃声）
  ✎ The alarm clock <u>went off</u>. 闹钟响了。
  ✎ The gun <u>went off</u> accidentally. 枪走火了。
  ✎ The bomb <u>went off</u> at midnight. 炸弹在午夜爆炸了。
  近义词：
  **ring**（门铃、电话等）响
  ✎ The <u>phone/ doorbell</u> <u>rang</u>.
  **strike** （钟表打点报时）响
  ✎ The clock was <u>striking</u> the hours.（L2）
  ✎ The clock began to <u>strike</u> twelve. 钟开始敲十二点的钟声。
  **blare** 汽车鸣笛声
  ✎ The silence was suddenly broken when a large car, with its headlights on and its horn <u>blaring</u>, roared down the arcade.（L6）
  **roar, thunder** 巨大的、低沉的轰鸣声
  ✎ large container trucks <u>thundering</u> through quiet village（本文）
  **whine**（机器运转的）轰鸣声
  ✎ Lawn mowers <u>whining</u> on a summer’s day（本文）
+ **serve to do** 发挥某个作用，有某个效果
  ✎ His death <u>serves to</u> remind us how dangerous using drugs can be. 他的死的作用是提醒我们吸毒是多么危险。
  **serve as……** 发挥作为某物的作用，当作某物来用（要用主动）（L25）
  ✎ She <u>serves as</u> an impressive reminder of the great ships of past.（L25）
+ **a source of** ……的来源
  ✎ ……, but uncles and aunts are always <u>a source of</u> extra income.（L15）
+ **survey, poll, opinion poll** 民意调查
  **census** 人口普查
  ✎ the Fifth National <u>Census</u> 第五次全国人口普查
  **investigation** 调查（无场合限制）
  ✎ the <u>investigation</u> of the <u>case/ market/ ……</u> 案件调查/市场调研
+ **rate** 被评定为是，被划分为是
  ✎ The essay <u>rates</u> a low grade. 这篇文章被评定为低等级。
  **on scale** 在……等级
  ✎ The earthquake measured 8.0 <u>on</u> the Richter <u>scale</u>. 这次地震震级为里氏8.0级。
  ✎ The students rates the teachers <u>on</u> a <u>scale</u> of 1 to 5. 学生们用1到5分对老师进行评分。
+ ┏ **range from A to B** 从A到B范围内
  ┗ **range between A and B**
  ┏ The team contained ten players whose ages <u>ranged from 10 to 16</u>.
  ┗ The team contained ten players whose ages <u>ranged between 10 and 16</u>.
+ **block**（有专门用途的）大楼
  ✎ apartment <u>block</u> 公寓楼
  ✎ office <u>block</u> 办公楼
+ **object to + n.** 反对某物
  **oppose + n.** 反对某物
  **protest (against) + n.** 示威，抗议
  **boycott + n.** 抵制某物
  反义搭配：
  **<u>support/ back</u> + n.** 支持某物
  **be behind + n.** 支持某人
  **stand by + n.** 支持某人（**stand by** 袖手旁观）
  **<u>advocate/ endorse</u> + n.** 公开支持/鼓吹
+ ┏ **public transport [英]** [U] 公共交通工具
  ┗ **public transportation [美]** [U] 
  = buses, trains etc.
+ **on + n.** 使用某设备/乐器等
  ✎ She is <u>on</u> the <u>phone/ computer</u>. 她正在打电话/用电脑。
  ✎ She is playing a piece of music <u>on</u> the piano. 她正在用钢琴演奏一支乐曲。
+ mobile phone[英] = <u>cell/ cellular</u> phone [美]
+ mid-thirties 三十五岁左右，三十五六岁
  early thirties 三十出头，三十一二岁
  late thirties 近四十岁，三十八九岁
+ ┏ **<u>rise/ increase/ jump/ soar/ rocket/ spiral</u> to……** 上升到……（L8）
  ┗ **<u>fall/ drop/ plunge/ dive/ plummet</u> to……** 下降到……（后三者多表示骤降、暴跌）
+ **against……** 与……相比，~~与……对抗~~
  同义搭配：
  **compared <u>to/ with</u>……**
  **<u>in/ by</u> comparison <u>to/ with</u>……**
  **<u>in/ by</u> contrast <u>to/ with</u>……**
  相关搭配：
  **A as against B is as C against D**  A与B相比较，就如同C和D相比较一样（L44）
  ✎ The military power of the US, <u>as against</u> that of DPRK, <u>is as</u> the strength of an elephant <u>against</u> that of a mouse. 美国的军事力量与朝鲜的相比的话，就好比大象的力量与老鼠的相比一样。
+ **whatever引导让步状语从句时，常省略be动词。**
  ┏ <u>Whatever the source of noise</u>, one thing is certain:……（原文-省略）
  ┗ <u>Whatever the source of noise (is)</u>, one thing is certain……（原文补全）
  ✎ After all, <u>whatever her faults (are)</u>, she is your mother. 毕竟，无论她有什么过失，她都是你的母亲。
  ✎ The country is always beautiful <u>whatever the season (is)</u>. 无论什么季节，这个国家总是如此美丽。
+ **golden** 金子般的
  ✎ a <u>golden</u> memory  金子般的回忆
  ✎ a <u>golden</u> opportunity 一个宝贵的机会（固定搭配）

---

## **Lesson 48 - The silent village**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>In this much-travelled world, there are still thousands of places which are inaccessible to tourists. We always assume that villagers in remote places are friendly and hospitable. But people who are cut off not only from foreign tourists, but even from their own countrymen can be hostile to travellers. Visits to really remote villages are seldom enjoyable — as my wife and I discovered during a tour through the Balkans.

We had spent several days in a small town and visited a number of old churches in the vicinity. These attracted many visitors, for they were not only of great architectural interest, but contained a large number of beautifully preserved frescoes as well. On the day before our departure, several bus loads of tourists descended on the town. This was more than we could bear, so we decided to spend our last day exploring the countryside. Taking a path which led out of the town, we crossed a few fields until we came to a dense wood. We expected the path to end abruptly, but we found that it traced its way through the trees. We tramped through the wood for over two hours until we arrived at a deep stream. We could see that the path continued on the other side, but we had no idea how we could get across the stream. Suddenly my wife spotted a boat moored to the bank. In it there was a boatman fast asleep. We gently woke him up and asked him to ferry us to the other side. Though he was reluctant to do so at first, we eventually persuaded him to take us.

The path led to a tiny village perched on the steep sides of a mountain. The place consisted of a straggling unmade road which was lined on either side by small houses. Even under a clear blue sky, the village looked forbidding, as all the houses were built of grey mud bricks. The village seemed deserted, the only sign of life being an ugly-looking black goat on a short length of rope tied to a tree in a field nearby. Sitting down on a dilapidated wooden fence near the field, we opened a couple of tins of sardines and had a picnic lunch. All at once, I noticed that my wife seemed to be filled with alarm. Looking up I saw that we were surrounded by children in rags who were looking at us silently as we ate. We offered them food and spoke to them kindly, but they remained motionless. I concluded that they were simply shy of strangers. When we later walked down the main street of the village, we were followed by a silent procession of children. The village which had seemed deserted, immediately came to life. Faces appeared at windows. Men in shirt sleeves stood outside their houses and glared at us. Old women in black shawls peered at us from doorways. The most frightening thing of all was that not a sound could be heard. There was no doubt that we were unwelcome visitors. We needed no further warning. Turning back down the main street, we quickened our pace and made our way rapidly towards the stream where we hoped the boatman was waiting.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
张道真说，语法简单，词法难？
+ **inaccessible** a. 无法到达的
  ✎ The country consists mainly of dense jungles and <u>inaccessible</u> mountain ranges. 该国主要由茂密的丛林和无法到达的山脉组成。
  **inaccessible to** 对……来说无法到达
  ✎ The bathroom is situated at the top of a flight of stairs, making it <u>inaccessible to</u> the disabled. 浴室位于一段楼梯的顶部，使得残疾人无法到达。
  反义词：
  **accessible** a. 可到达的
  ✎ The village is isolated and <u>accessible</u> only by helicopter. 这个村庄与世隔绝，只能乘直升机到达。
  **(be) accessible to** 对……来说可以到达（作表语加be动词）
  ✎ All parts of the museum <u>are accessible to</u> wheelchairs. 博物馆的所有地方，轮椅都可以到达。
  + **access**
    ◇ n1.（接近或进入某地的）方法，通道
    **access to……**
    ✎ The only <u>access to</u> the farmhouse is across the fields. 通往农舍的唯一通道是穿过田野。
    ◇ n2.（使用某物或接近某人的）机会或权利
    **have access to……**
    ✎ Students must <u>have access to</u> a good library. 学生必须能够使用一个好的图书馆。
    ✎ Only high officials <u>have access to</u> the president. 只有高级官员才能接触到总统。
+ **hospitable** a. 好客的（L34）
  **be hospitable <u>to/ towards</u> sb.** 对某人很热情/好客
  ✎ The local people <u>are</u> very <u>hospitable to</u> strangers. 当地人对陌生人非常热情好客。
  **hospitality** n. 好客
  ✎ Thank you for your kind <u>hospitality</u>. 谢谢你的盛情款待。
  ✎ The Chinese are noted for their <u>hospitality</u>. 中国人因好客而著称。
  反义词：
  **inhospitable** a. 不好客的
  **unfriendly** a. 不友好的
  **unwelcoming** a. 不热情的
  **forbidding** a. 令人望而生畏的；冷冰冰的
  ✎ a <u>forbidding</u> <u>place/ appearance</u> 一个令人望而生畏的地方/一副拒人于千里之外的模样
  ✎ The more expensive kind of antique shop where rare objects are beautifully displayed in glass cases to keep them free from dust is usually a <u>forbidding place</u>.（L34）
+ **hostile** 英 /ˈhɒstaɪl/; 美 /ˈhɑːstl/ a. 很不友好的，有敌意的
  ✎ <u>hostile</u> attitude 敌对态度
  ✎ a <u>hostile</u> <u>response/ reaction/ crowd/ review/ reception/ ……</u>
  很不友好的回应/反应/人群/评论/接待/……
  **be hostile <u>to/ towards</u>……** 对……很不友好（作表语）
  ✎ But people who are cut off not only from foreign tourists, but even from their own countrymen can <u>be hostile to</u> travellers.（本文）
  近义搭配：
  **be antagonistic <u>to/ towards</u>……** (fml.) 对……非常不友好
  ✎ He<u>’s always antagonistic towards</u> new ideas. 他总是对新思想怀有敌意。
  + 发音的英美区别（见L47）
+ **vicinity** n. 附近地区
  **in the vicinity (of sth.)** 在（……的）附近
  ✎ There is no hospital <u>in the vicinity</u>. 这附近没有医院。
  ✎ There are several hotels <u>in the immediate vicinity of</u> the station. 车站附近有几家旅馆。（immediate 修饰，表示很近）
  ✎ We had spent several days in a small town and visited a number of old churches <u>in the vicinity</u>.（本文）
  ✎ Everyone knows that if he shouts <u>in the vicinity of</u> a wall or a mountainside, an echo will come back.（B4L7）
  近义搭配：
  **in the neighbourhood (of sth.)** 在（……的）附近
  ✎ Is there a good Chinese restaurant <u>in the neighbourhood</u>? 这附近有好的中餐馆吗？
  ✎ Houses <u>in the neighborhood of</u> Paris are extremely expensive. 巴黎附近的房子非常昂贵。
  ✎ Hans returned to his family home, but the house had been bombed and no one <u>in the neighbourhood</u> knew what had become of the inhabitants.（L36）
  + **在……附近**（L6，L34）
    a famous arcade + (以下5行) 在皮卡迪利大姐的附近
    ↳ **near** Piccadilly
    ↳ **close to** Piccadilly
    ↳ **around** Piccadilly
    ↳ **off** Piccadilly
    ↳ **in the <u>neighborhood/ vicinity</u> of** Piccadilly
  + **距离近**的表达（L34）
    **only a short bus ride away** 坐公交车就能到（bus ride 公交车的车程）
    **within walking distance** 走着就能到
    **within driving distance** 开车能到
    **within commuting distance** 乘车往返可以到（commute 乘车往返，通勤）
    **only a stone’s throw away** 仅仅一箭之遥
+ **abruptly** ad. ① 出乎意料地；② 粗鲁无礼地
  ✎ The interview ended <u>abruptly</u>. 这次采访/面试突然结束了。
  ✎ ‘Good night, then,’ she said <u>abruptly</u>. “那么，晚安，”她粗鲁地说。
  **abrupt**
  + a1. 突如其来的，意外的
    英文释义：sudden and unexpected, often in an unpleasant way
    ✎ an <u>abrupt</u> <u>ending/ change/ departure</u> 一个突然的结束/变化/离去
    **come to an abrupt <u>end/ halt</u>** 突然/出乎意料地结束/停下了
    ✎ The bus <u>came to an abrupt halt</u>. 公交车突然停了。
    ✎ Our friendship <u>came to an abrupt end</u>. 我们的友谊戛然而止。
    **bring sth. to an abrupt <u>end/ halt</u>** 使某事出乎意料地结束/停止
    ✎ The accident <u>brought</u> his career <u>to an abrupt end</u>. 那次事故使他的职业生涯突然结束了。
  + a2. 粗鲁无礼的，无耐心的
    英文释义：seeming rude and unfriendly, esp. because you do not waste time in friendly conversation
    ✎ an <u>abrupt</u> manner 粗鲁的举止
    ✎ She was very <u>abrupt</u> with me in our meeting. 在我们见面的时候，她对我很粗鲁。
+ **tramp**
  + v. 缓慢而步履沉重地行走（尤指长途跋涉）
    英文释义：to walk somewhere slowly and with heavy steps
    ✎ He <u>tramped</u> the streets looking for work. 他在街上长途跋涉找工作。（vt.）
    **tramp <u>through/ across/ around</u>……** 步履沉重地穿过/横穿/在附近……（vi.） 
    ✎ We <u>tramped through</u> the wood for over two hours until we arrived at a deep stream.（本文）
  + n. 长途跋涉；流浪汉
    ✎ go for a solitary <u>tramp</u> in the country 去乡下独自长途跋涉
    ✎ We had a long <u>tramp</u> home. 我们是经过长途跋涉回家的。/ 我们走了很长一段路才回家。
    ✎ But real <u>tramps</u> are not beggars.（L27）
+ **dilapidated** a. 破旧的，年久失修的
  英文释义：(of furniture and buildings) old and in very bad condition
  ✎ a <u>dilapidated</u> <u>chair/ bed</u> 一把/张破旧的椅子/床
  ✎ We stayed in an old, <u>dilapidated</u> hotel with a leaky roof. 我们住在一家破旧不堪、屋顶漏水的宾馆里。（**leak** v. 漏）
  近义词：
  **battered** a. 破旧不堪的
  英文释义：old, used a lot, and in bad condition
  ✎ a <u>battered</u> old suitcase 一个破旧的箱子
  ✎ a <u>battered</u> old car 一辆破旧的车
  ✎ While the <u>battered</u> car was moving away, Roy stopped his bus and telephoned the police.（B2L35）
  **rickety** a. 摇摇晃晃快散架的（L46）
  英文释义：a rickety structure or piece of furniture is in very bad condition, and likely to break easily
  ✎ a <u>rickety</u> old wooden chair 一把摇摇晃晃的旧木椅子
  ✎ When lights fuse, furniture gets <u>rickety</u>, pipes get clogged, or vacuum cleaners fail to operate, some women assume that their husbands will somehow put things right.（L46）
+ **rag** n. 破布，碎布片
  **in rags** 穿着破烂衣服
  ✎ a tramp dressed <u>in rags</u> 一个穿着破烂衣服的流浪汉
  ✎ Children <u>in rags</u> begged money from the tourists. 穿着破烂衣服的孩子们向游客乞讨。
  **from rags to riches** 白手起家（固定搭配）
  ✎ He likes to tell people of his rise <u>from rags to riches</u>. 他喜欢跟人讲他从赤贫到富裕的过程。
  + **衣服、服装**（L13）：
    **costume** 戏服，化妆服，道具服
    **overalls/ coveralls**  工作服，工装裤（蓝领、工人）
    **uniform** 制服（警察、护士、学生所着装的统一的制服）
    ✎ school <u>uniform</u> 校服 ✎ military <u>uniform</u> 军装
    **sportswear** 运动服（所有由“wear”构成的单词都是不可数）
    **leisure wear** 休闲装
    **underclothes** [pl.] 内衣
    **underwear** [U] 内衣
    **suit** 西服套装
    **shroud** 寿衣；裹尸布
+ **procession** n.（人或车）队伍
  英文释义：a line of people or vehicles that move along slowly, especially as part of a ceremony
  ✎ a <u>funeral/ wedding/ carnival</u> <u>procession</u> 一个送葬/婚礼/狂欢节的队伍
  **march in procession** 列队前进（固定搭配）
  ✎ Groups of unemployed people from all over the country <u>marched in procession</u> to the capital. 来自全国各地的失业者列队向首都前进。
  ✎ There seemed to be an endless <u>procession</u> of boyfriends knocking on her door. 似乎有络绎不绝的男朋友在列队敲她的门。（比喻义）
  相关词：
  **parade** n.（节日或庆典）游行的队伍；阅兵式；列队展示或表演
  ✎ a <u>victory/ carnival</u> <u>parade</u> 一场凯旋/狂欢节游行
  ✎ a military <u>parade</u> 一场阅兵式
  ✎ a fashion <u>parade</u> 一场时装表演
  ✎ a <u>parade</u> of players before a football match 足球赛前队员列队入场
  ✎ She had a constant <u>parade</u> of young men coming to visit her. 经常有一连串的小伙子找她。（比喻义）
  **column** n. (人或事物的)队伍 a long moving line of people or things 
  ✎ a <u>column</u> of soldiers 一队士兵
  ✎ a <u>column</u> of refugees 一队难民
  ✎ Who has not stood in awe at the sight of a spider pouncing on a fly, or a <u>column</u> of ants triumphantly bearing home an enormous dead beetle?（L54）
+ **peer** v.（因看不清而）仔细看，费力看
  **peered at** 仔细地/费力地看某物
  ✎ Mary <u>peered at</u> her watch.
  ✎ He <u>peered</u> closely <u>at</u> the photograph. 他仔细地看了看照片。
  ✎ Old women in black shawls <u>peered at</u> us from doorways.（本文）
  近义搭配：
  **squint at……** 眯起眼睛来看……（L22）
  **squint one’s eyes** 某人眯起眼睛（多用于光线太暗的情境）
  ✎ Stop <u>squinting at</u> the screen — put your glasses on. 别眯着眼睛看屏幕了——戴上眼镜吧。
  ✎ Then, <u>squinting his eyes</u>, he said: ‘The light is dim. Read the letter to me.’（L22）
