Our own warm atmosphere and the heat generated by the telescope would make it impossible to detect objects as small as planets. Even a telescope in orbit round the earth, like the very successful Hubble telescope, would not be suitable because of the dust particles in our solar system. A telescope would have to be as far away as the planet Jupiter to look for life in outer space, because the dust becomes thinner the further we travel towards the outer edges of our own solar system. Once we detected a planet, we would have to find a way of blotting out the light from its star, so that we would be able to ‘see’ the planet properly and analyse its atmosphere. In the first instance, we would be looking for plant life, rather than ‘little green men’. The life forms most likely to develop on a planet would be bacteria. It is bacteria that have generated the oxygen we breathe on earth. For most of the earth’s history they have been the only form of life on our planet. As Earth-dwellers, we always cherish the hope that we will be visited by little green men and that we will be able to communicate with them. But this hope is always in the realms of science fiction. If we were able to discover lowly forms of life like bacteria on another planet, it would completely change our view of ourselves. As Daniel Goldin of NASA observed, ‘Finding life elsewhere would change everything. No human endeavour or thought would be unchanged by it.’</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **astronomy** n. 天文学
  字根 **astr/ aster = star**（L37）
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onomy 天文学
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onomical 天文学的；天文数字的
  ◇ <u>astr</u>ology 占星术
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onautics 航天学（nau = ship；cs 表示某种学问）
  ◇ <u>astr</u>onaut 宇航员
  ◇ dis<u>aster</u> 大灾难；灾星，扫把星（dis 表示不好的，有灾的）
  ◇ <u>aster</u>oid 小行星
  ◇ <u>aster</u>isk 星号（*）
  字根 **stell = star**
  ◇ <u>stell</u>ar 星的；恒星的 ✎ <u>stellar</u> light 星光 ✎ <u>stellar</u> system 星系
  ◇ inter<u>stell</u>ar 星际的（inter-: between）✎ <u>interstellar</u> travel 星际旅行
  ◇ con<u>stell</u>ation 星座；一系列（相关的想法、事物）；一群（相关的人）✎ a <u>constellation</u> of famous scientists and artists 一群著名的科学家和艺术家
+ **solar** a. 太阳的
  ✎ <u>solar</u> energy 太阳能
  ✎ <u>solar</u> system 太阳系
  ✎ <u>solar</u> radiation 太阳辐射
  ✎ <u>solar</u> calendar 阳历
  ✎ a <u>partial/ total</u> <u>solar</u> eclipse 日偏/全食
  **lunar** a. 月球的；月亮的
  ✎ <u>lunar</u> calendar 阴历
  ✎ a <u>partial/ total</u> <u>lunar</u> eclipse 月偏/全食
+ **Venus** n. 金星（美神维纳斯）
  **Mercury** 水星；水银（小写）（商贸之神墨丘利）
  **Mars** 火星（战神马尔斯）
  **Jupiter** 木星（众神之王朱庇特）
  **Saturn** 土星（农神萨图恩）
  **Uranus** 天王星（天空之神乌拉诺斯）
  **Neptune** 海王星（海神尼普顿）
  **Puto** 冥王星（冥王普路托）
+ **bacteria** n.[pl.] 细菌
  单数 | 复数 | 词义 
  ---- | ---- | ---- 
  bacteri<u>um</u> | bacteri<u>a</u> | 细菌
  dat<u>um</u> | dat<u>a</u> | 数据
  medi<u>um</u> | medi<u>a</u> | 媒体；媒介
  strat<u>um</u> | strat<u>a</u> | 岩层；社会阶层
  curricul<u>um</u> | curricul<u>a</u> | 课程
  
+ **realm** n. 王国；范围，领域
  ✎ the <u>realm</u> of <u>literature/ science</u> 文学/科学界/领域
  ✎ the <u>political/ military</u> <u>realm</u> 政治/军事界/领域
  ┏ the <u>realm</u> of necessity 必然王国（哲学概念）
  ┗ the <u>realm</u> of freedom 自由王国（哲学概念）
  ✎ The history of mankind is one of continuous development from <u>the realm of necessity</u> to <u>the realm of freedom</u>. 人类的历史是从必然王国向自由王国不断发展的历史。——毛泽东
  近义词：
  **domain** （贵族的）领土；范围，领域
  ✎ the political <u>domain</u> 政治界/领域
  ✎ the <u>domain</u> of natural science 自然科学领域
  **field/ area/ world/ sphere** 范围，领域（比上面两个更通俗）
  ✎ the <u>field</u> of politics 政治界/领域
  ✎ the <u>world</u> of art 艺术界/领域
  ✎ the <u>area</u> of education 教育界/领域
  ✎ the diplomatic <u>sphere</u> 外交界/领域
  ✎ the ideological <u>sphere</u> 思想界/领域（**ideology** 思想（体系）；意识形态）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **真正宾语较长，且有宾语补足语时，可将形式宾语放至原宾语位置，将真正宾语放至宾语补足语后面。**
+ **detect** v. 发现，觉察 to discover or notice sth, especially sth that is not easy to see, hear, etc.
  ✎ The tests are designed to detect the <u>disease</u> early. 这些测试旨在及早发现疾病。
  ✎ an instrument that can detect small <u>amounts</u> of radiation 能探测微量辐射的仪器
+ **the Milky Way = the Galaxy** 银河（**galaxy** 星系；人才荟萃）
+ **in relative terms** 相对来说 compared with other, similar things（习语）
  ✎ Students have less money <u>in relative terms</u>, but spend more on books. 学生的钱相对较少，但花在书本上的钱更多。
+ **prove (to be) + <u>a./n.</u>** 被证明是……（L1）
  ✎ The search <u>proved</u> difficult, for the puma was often observed at one place in the morning and at another place twenty miles away in the evening.（L1）
+ **hard enough** 足够困难（enough 修饰形容词后副词时，通常后置）
+ **life** [U] 作泛指或抽象含义；[C] 具体某人某物的生命
+ **infinitely** ad.（尤其与比较级连用）……得多 very much — used esp. when comparing things
  ✎ Your English is <u>infinitely</u> better than my German. 你的英语比我的德语好得多。
  ✎ Travel is <u>infinitely</u> more comfortable now than it used to be. 现在旅行比以前舒服得多了。
  同义表达：
  **<u>far/ much/ even/ still/ yet</u> + 比较级** ……得多（用 infinitely 更正式）（L4）
+ **support** v.（提供合适的条件以）维持生命，使活下去 to provide the right conditions, such as enough food and water, for life
  ✎ The land is so poor here that it cannot <u>support</u> any crops. 这里的土地是如此得贫瘠，以至于无法种植任何庄稼。
  ✎ Because of pollution, this lake is now too acid to <u>support</u> fish. 由于污染，这个湖现在太酸了，无法养鱼。

**it takes…… (for……) to do sth.** 做某事需要/花费……（L42）
  ✎ <u>It took</u> a few minutes <u>for</u> his eyes <u>to</u> adjust to the dark. 他的眼睛花了几分钟时间来适应黑暗。
  ✎ <u>It</u> can <u>take</u> as long as eight days <u>to</u> rig up rope ladders and <u>to</u> establish supply bases before a descent can be made into a very deep cave.（L42）
+ **that is (to say)** 也就是说，确切地说 or more exactly（常用于引出同位语）
  （下列例句中，划虚线文字为同位语）
  ✎ The fare is reduced for <span style="border-bottom: dashed">children</span>, <u>that is</u> <span style="border-bottom: dashed">anyone under 15 years old</span>. 儿童的费用有所降低，即15岁以下的任何人。
  ✎ One solution would be <span style="border-bottom: dashed">to change the shape of the screen</span>, <u>that is</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">to make it wider</span>.  一种解决方案是改变屏幕的形状，也就是使其更宽。
  ✎ Languages are taught <span style="border-bottom: dashed">by the direct method</span>, <u>that is to say</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">without using the student’s own language</span>. 语言教学采用直接教学法，也就是说，不使用学生自己的语言。
  ✎ <span style="border-bottom: dashed">I loved him</span> — <u>that is</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">I thought I did</span>. 我当时爱他，确切来说，是我认为我当时爱他。
  ✎ <span style="border-bottom: dashed">I’ll meet you in the city</span>, <u>that is</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">will if the trains are running</span>. 我会在城里跟你见面，也就是说，如果火车还正常行驶的话。
  ✎ One authority on spiders made a census of the spiders in a grass field in the south of England, and he estimated that there were <span style="border-bottom: dashed">more than 2,250,000 in one acre</span>, <u>that is</u> <span style="border-bottom: dashed">something like 6,000,000 spiders of different kinds on a football pitch</span>.（B4L2）
  同义表达：
  **i.e.** 也就是说，换句话说，即
  ✎ The film is only open to <span style="border-bottom: dashed">adults</span>, <u>i.e.</u> <span style="border-bottom: dashed">people over 18</span>. 这部电影只对成年人开放，即18岁以上的人。
  ✎ The hotel is closed <span style="border-bottom: dashed">during low season</span>, <u>i.e.</u> <span style="border-bottom: dashed">from October to March</span>. 酒店在淡季（即10月至3月）关闭。
  ✎ The price must be <span style="border-bottom: dashed">more realistic</span>, <u>i.e.</u> <span style="border-bottom: dashed">lower</span>. 价格必须更现实，即更低。
  **to be exact** 精确地说（通常后置）
  ✎ She has worked at the bank for <span style="border-bottom: dashed">many years</span>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">nine</span> <u>to be exact</u>. 她在这家银行工作了很多年，确切地说是九年。
  **in other words** 换句话说
  ✎ <span style="border-bottom: dashed">He was economical with the truth</span> — <u>in other words</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">he was lying</span>. 他在事实方面非常节约，换句话说，他在撒谎。
  **to put it another way** 换句话说（L12）
  ✎ <span style="border-bottom: dashed">It’s fairly risky</span>. Or <u>to put it another way</u>, <span style="border-bottom: dashed">don’t try this at home</span>. 这相当危险。或者换句话说，不要在家里尝试。
+ **imagine 经常引导祈使句**
  ✎ <u>Imagine</u> life without hot water. 想象一下没有热水的生活吧。
  ✎ <u>Imagine</u> that you have just won a million pounds. 想象一下，你刚刚赢了一百万英镑。（+ 宾语从句）
  ✎ <u>Imagine</u> their dismay when they found a beautifully-cooked wallet and notes turned to ash!（L7）
+ **up to sth.**
  1. 多达…… as much or as many as a certain amount or number but not more
  ✎ The Olympic Stadium will hold <u>up to</u> 80,000 spectators. 奥林匹克体育场最多可容纳8万名观众。
  ✎ The temperature went <u>up to</u> 35°C. 温度上升到35°C。
  2. **= up till** 直到…… for the whole of a period until a certain time or date
  ✎ <u>Up to</u> the time of his death, Richard Colson was one of the most notable figures in our town.（L31）
  ✎ <u>Up to</u> now, historians have assumed that calendars came into being with the advent of agriculture, for then man was faced with a real need to understand something about the seasons.（L38）
+ ┏ **be capable of** 也能够
  ┗ **be able to do**
**alternatively** ad. 或者 used to introduce a suggestion or to mention sth. different to what has just been stated
  ✎ The agency will make travel arrangements for you. <u>Alternatively</u>, you can organize your own transport. 旅行社会为你安排旅行。或者，您可以自行安排交通。
  ✎ We could go to the Indian restaurant, or <u>alternatively</u>, we could try that new Italian place. 我们可以去印度餐厅，或者我们可以试试那家新开的意大利餐厅。
+ **构词法中，定语从句转化为复合形容词可使表达更简洁**
  **转化步骤：**
  **① 中心名词保留；**
  **② 动词换成分词，用连字符与中心名词连接。**（主动 → 现在分词；被动 → 过去分词）
  **life-supporting** a. 维持生命的（复合形容词）
  ↓ the planet <u>which supports life</u>（啰嗦）
  ↳ the <u>life-supporting</u> planet
  ✎ 
  ↓ animals <u>which eat insects</u> 吃昆虫的动物们
  ↳ <u>insect-eating</u> animals（B4L2）
  ✎ 
  ↓ silverware <u>which is made by hands</u> 手工制作的银餐具
  ↳ <u>hand-made</u> silverware（L28）
  ✎ 
  ↓ diseases <u>which are related to stress</u> 与压力有关的疾病
  ↳ <u>stress-related</u> diseases
  ✎ 
  ✎ <u>state-owned</u> enterprises (SOEs) 国有企业
  ✎ <u>flower-selling</u> girls 卖花姑娘
  ✎ <u>epoch-making</u> masterpieces 划时代的杰作
  ✎ <u>cancer-causing</u> substances 致癌物
+ 虚拟语气的省略
  Alternatively, if the star were small, the life-supporting planet <u>would have to</u> have a close orbit round it **and** <u>(would)</u> also <u>(have to)</u> provide the perfect conditions for life forms to develop.（原文补全）
+ for…… to do（for 引出动词不定式的逻辑主语）
  ✎ He opened a door and stood aside <u>for</u> **her** <u>to pass</u>. 他打开一扇门，站在一边让她过去。
  ✎ Her circumstances had never been good enough <u>for</u> **her hopes** <u>to be realized</u>. 她的处境从未好到足以实现她的希望。
+ 如果虚拟语气的 if 从句假设的内容，上下文可判断，则该if从句常会省略。
  ┏ But how <u>would</u> we find such a planet?（原文）
  ┗ But how <u>would</u> we find such a planet if there <u>were</u> such a planet?（原文补全）
+ **in existence** 存在（介词短语）
  ✎ The organization has been <u>in existence</u> for 25 years. 该组织已经存在了25年。（作表语）
  **come into existence** 开始存在（动词短语）
  ✎ Scientists have many theories about how the universe first <u>came into existence</u>. 科学家们对宇宙最初是如何形成的有很多理论。
+ **presence** n. 存在 the existence of sb. or sth. in a particular place
  ┏ **one’s presence** 某人/某物的存在（代词）
  ✎ <u>Her presence</u> during the crisis had a calming effect. 在危机中，她的存在起到了让人安心的效果。
  ✎ We enjoy staring at them, entranced as they go about their business, unaware (we hope) of <u>our presence</u>.（L54）
  ┗ **the presence of……** ……的存在（名词）
  ✎ Tests revealed <u>the presence of</u> poison in the blood. 检测显示血液中有毒物质的存在。
  ✎ <u>The presence of</u> pollen in the atmosphere causes hay fever in some people. 大气中花粉的存在会导致一些人出现枯草热。
  **detect the presence of……** 寻找……
  ✎ a device for <u>detecting the presence of</u> submarines 探测潜艇存在的装置
  ✎ The dogs were trained to <u>detect the presence of</u> explosives. 这些狗经过训练，可以探测爆炸物的存在。
+ **develop** v. 开发，研制 to design or make a new idea, product, system etc. over a period of time
  ✎ Scientists are <u>developing</u> new drugs to treat arthritis. 科学家们正在开发治疗关节炎的新药。
  **development** n. 开发，研制 the process of creating a new product or method
  ✎ His work is mainly in software <u>development</u>. 他的工作主要是软件开发。
  ✎ The funds will be used for product <u>development</u>. 这些资金将用于产品研发。
+ 英语中，名词表达比动词表达更正式
  ✎ <u>The resolution of</u> some problems of today is urgent and critical for the survival of a society. 解决某些现存问题对于社会的存在来说是紧迫而关键的。（GRE 范文）
  ✎ <u>Overemphasis upon</u> some existing problems could cause harmful effects. 过分地强调一些现有问题可能会造成有害影响。
  ✎ <u>The efforts</u> to solve problems of the future <u>is</u> sometimes <u>of paramount importance</u> for <u>the avoidance of</u> potential threats or even catastrophes we can anticipate. 努力解决未来的问题，有时对于避免我们可以预见的潜在威胁甚至灾难至关重要。
  ✎ <u>His acceptance of</u> bribes led to <u>his arrest</u>. 他因受贿而被捕。
  ✎ <u>My arrival</u> coincided with <u>his departure</u>. 我来的时候他正好要走。/我的到来恰逢他离开。
+ **-based**（复合形容词字根）
  1. 位于…… combines with nouns referring to places to mean sth. positioned or existing mainly in the place mentioned, or operating or organized from that place
  ✎ a <u>Washington-based</u> organization 位于华盛顿的组织
  ✎ <u>land-based</u> missiles 位于陆地上的导弹
  2. 主要成分为…… used with some names to make adjectives describing the main substance in a product
  ✎ <u>lead-based</u> paints 铅基涂料/主要成分是铅的颜料
  ✎ <u>carbon-based</u> fuels 碳基燃料/~
  ✎ <u>nitrogen-based</u> fertilizer 氮基肥料/~
  ✎ pasta and other <u>wheat-based</u> products 意大利面和其他小麦制品
+ Our own warm atmosphere and the heat generated by the telescope <u>would</u> make it impossible to detect objects as small as planets (if we <u>looked</u> for life on another planet using earth-based telescopes).（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ Even a telescope in orbit round the earth, like the very successful Hubble telescope, <u>would</u> not be suitable because of the dust particles in our solar system (if we <u>looked</u> for life using a telescope in orbit round the earth).（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ **Hubble Edwin Powell** 1889-1953.
  American astronomer who discovered (1929) that the velocities of nebulae increase with distance
  **Hubble Space Telescope (HST)**
  The Hubble Space Telescope is a telescope in orbit around the Earth.
  Its position outside the Earth’s atmosphere allows it to take extremely sharp images, and since its launch in 1990, it has become one of the most important telescopes in the history of astronomy.
  It has been responsible for many ground-breaking observations and has helped astronomers achieve a better understanding of many fundamental problems in astrophysics.
+ **particle** n. 微粒 a very small piece of sth.
  ✎ dust <u>particles</u>（本文）
  ✎ tiny <u>particles</u> of soil 微小的土壤颗粒
  **elementary particle** n. 基本粒子 one of the types of pieces of matter including **electron**s (电子), **proton**s (质子), and **neutron**s (中子) that make up **atom**s (原子)
+ A telescope <u>would</u> have to be as far away as the planet Jupiter to look for life in outer space (if we <u>looked</u> for life in outer space), because the dust becomes thinner the further we travel towards the outer edges of our own solar system.（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ **the + 比较级……，the + 比较级……。**（前半句是从句，类似于条件状语从句，先翻译，后半句是主句）（L9）
  ┏ <u>The harder</u> they worked <u>the hungrier</u> they became. 他们工作得越努力，他们就会变得越饿。
  ┗ They became <u>(the) hungrier</u> <u>the harder</u> they worked.（如果是这种语序，则前半句是主句，后半句是从句。依然先翻译从句）
  ✎ We are so familiar with the fact that man ages, that people have for years assumed that the process of losing vigour with time, of <u>becoming more likely to die</u> <u>the older we get</u>, was something self-evident, like the cooling of a hot kettle or the wearing-out of a pair of shoes.（B4L37）
+ ┏ **way of doing sth.** 做某事的方式
  ✎ a new <u>way of</u> storing information 一种新的信息存储方式
  ┗ **way to do sth.** 做某事的方式
  ✎ What is the best <u>way to</u> clean this? 最好的清洁方法是什么？
+ **blot** n. 污点，墨迹 a mark or dirty spot on sth., esp. made by ink
  ✎ ink <u>blots</u> 墨水渍
  ✎ This is a serious <u>blot</u> on your career. 这是你事业上的一个严重污点。
  v.
  **blot out** 遮住 to cover sth. so that you can no longer see it
  ✎ Dark clouds overhead had <u>blotted out</u> the sun. 头顶的乌云遮住了太阳。
+ **so (that) 作连词时，通常来说有两种用法：**（L43、L50）
  1. **引导结果状语从句**，译为“**所以、因此**”，从句谓语动词中通常没有情态动词。
  2. **引导目的状语从句**，译为“**以便于……，为了……**” = in order that……，从句谓语动词中通常会出现情态动词 can, could, may, might, should, would 等。
  ┏ We paid him immediately, <u>so (that) he left contented</u>. 我们立刻给了他钱，所以他满意地离开了。
  ┗ We paid him immediately, <u>so (that) he **would** leave contented</u>. 我们立刻给了他钱，以便于他能够满意地离开。
+ **properly** ad.(BrE) 完全地，彻底地 completely, fully, thoroughly
  ✎ Is the chicken <u>properly</u> defrosted? 这只鸡完全解冻了吗？
  ✎ He got <u>properly</u> beaten by the world champion. 他被世界冠军彻底打败了。
+ (If we <u>looked</u> for life on a planet), in the first instance, we <u>would</u> be looking for plant life, rather than ‘little green men’.（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ **in the first instance** (fml.) 首先，第一 as the first part of a series of actions
  ✎ <u>In the first instance</u>, notify the police and then contact your insurance company. 首先，通知警方，然后联系您的保险公司。
  ✎ Anyone wishing to join the society should apply <u>in the first instance</u> to the secretary. 任何希望加入该协会的人都应该首先向秘书申请。
+ **Little green men** is a popular expression used to describe extraterrestrial life.
+ The life forms most likely to develop on a planet <u>would</u> be bacteria (if the planet <u>could</u> support life).（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ **It is…… that……** 强调句句型（不管单复数，都要用 is）
+ **dweller** 居民
  ✎ The city <u>dweller</u> never experiences anxieties of this sort.（L41）
+ **cherish** v. 长期怀有某种感情（详见L34）
  英文释义：to keep hopes, memories or ideas in your mind because they are important to you and bring you pleasure
  ✎ Like a scientist bent on making a discovery, he must <u>cherish the hope</u> that one day he will be amply rewarded.（L34）
  ✎ He <u>cherished the hope</u> of winning an Olympic medal. 他一直以来都希望赢得一枚奥运奖牌。（比用have漂亮）
  ✎ He <u>cherished the memory</u> of his late wife. 他一直以来都非常怀念已故的妻子。（late放在亲属前，是“已故”的委婉表达）
  ✎ He <u>cherished the illusion</u> that the girl was in love with him. 他一直以来都怀有那个女孩爱上自己的错觉。
+ **realm(s)** 领域
  ✎ an idea that belongs in the <u>realm(s)</u> of science fiction 属于科幻小说范畴的想法
  ✎ I suppose it’s not beyond the <u>realm(s)</u> of possibility. 我想这并没有超过可能性的范畴。/我认为这还是有可能的。
  ✎ This is not really within the <u>realm(s)</u> of my experience. 这并不在我的经验范围内。
+ **science fiction** (also informal **sci-fi**) n.[U] 科学幻想（科幻）
  英文释义：a type of book, film/ movie, etc. that is based on imagined scientific discoveries of the future, and often deals with space travel and life on other planets
+ **lowly** a. 卑微的，低等的 low in rank, importance, or social class
  ✎ He was a <u>lowly</u> assistant gardener. 他是个卑微的助理园丁。
  **low** a.&ad. 低的（地）
  ✎ bow <u>low</u> to the Queen 向女王深深鞠躬（ad.）
  ✎ That plane’s flying too <u>low</u>! 那架飞机飞得太低了！（ad.）
  ✎ We were, however, worried about our nearest neighbours, whose farm was <u>low</u> lying and who were newcomers to the district.（ad.）（L56）
+ Daniel Goldin
  人物简介：Daniel Saul Goldin (born July 23, 1940) served as the 9th and longest-tenured Administrator of NASA from April 1, 1992, to November 17, 2001. He was appointed by President George H.W.Bush and served under three presidential administrations.
+ **NASA** n.（美国）国家航空航天局
  全称：National Aeronautics and Space Administration
  英文释义： a US government organization that controls space travel and the scientific study of space
+ **observe** v.(fml.)（评论）说
  英文释义：to make a written or spoken comment about someone or something
  ✎ ‘I’ve always found German cars very reliable,’ he <u>observed</u>. “我一直觉得德国汽车非常可靠，”他评论道。
  ✎ She <u>observed</u> that it would soon be time to stop for lunch. 她说很快就要停下来吃午饭了。
  **observation** n. 言论，评论
  英文释义：a spoken or written remark about something you have noticed
  ✎ A young English writer made the pertinent <u>observation</u> a year or two back that the talent goes into the first draft, and the art into the drafts that follow.（B4L46）
+ **elsewhere** ad. 在别处，到别处 in, at, or to another place
  ✎ The answer to the problem must be sought <u>elsewhere</u>. 这个问题的答案必须在别处寻找。
  ✎ Our favourite restaurant was full, so we had to go <u>elsewhere</u>. 我们最喜欢的餐厅已经客满了，所以我们不得不去别的地方。
+ Finding life elsewhere <u>would</u> change everything (if life <u>were</u> found elsewhere).（原文补全-虚拟语气）
+ (If life <u>were</u> found elsewhere), no human endeavour or thought <u>would</u> be unchanged by it.（原文补全-虚拟语气）

---

## **Lesson 56 - Our neighbour, the river**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>The river which forms the eastern boundary of our farm has always played an important part in our lives. Without it we could not make a living. There is only enough spring water to supply the needs of the house, so we have to pump from the river for farm use. We tell the river all our secrets. We know instinctively, just as beekeepers with their bees, that misfortune might overtake us if the important events of our lives were not related to it.

We have special river birthday parties in the summer. Sometimes we go upstream to a favourite backwater, sometimes we have our party at the boathouse, which a predecessor of ours at the farm built in the meadow hard by the deepest pool for swimming and diving. In a heat wave we choose a midnight birthday party and that is the most exciting of all. We welcome the seasons by the riverside, crowning the youngest girl with flowers in the spring, holding a summer festival on Midsummer Eve, giving thanks for the harvest in the autumn, and throwing a holly wreath into the current in the winter.

After a long period of rain the river may overflow its banks. This is a rare occurrence as our climate seldom goes to extremes. We are lucky in that only the lower fields, which make up a very small proportion of our farm, are affected by flooding, but other farms are less favourably sited, and flooding can sometimes spell disaster for their owners.

One bad winter we watched the river creep up the lower meadows. All the cattle had been moved into stalls and we stood to lose little. We were, however, worried about our nearest neighbours, whose farm was low lying and who were newcomers to the district. As the floods had put the telephone out of order, we could not find out how they were managing. From an attic window we could get a sweeping view of the river where their land joined ours, and at the most critical juncture we took turns in watching that point. The first sign of disaster was a dead sheep floating down. Next came a horse, swimming bravely, but we were afraid that the strength of the current would prevent its landing anywhere before it became exhausted. Suddenly a raft appeared, looking rather like Noah’s ark, carrying the whole family, a few hens, the dogs, a cat, and a bird in a cage. We realized that they must have become unduly frightened by the rising flood, for their house, which had sound foundations, would have stood stoutly even if it had been almost submerged. The men of our family waded down through our flooded meadows with boathooks, in the hope of being able to grapple a corner of the raft and pull it out of the current towards our bank. We still think it a miracle that they were able to do so.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **boundary** n. 分界线，边界 dividing line
  ◇ The river **forms a natural boundary of** our farm. 这条河形成了我们农场的自然边界。
  ◇ The fence **marks the boundary between** my property **and** hers. 栅栏标志出了我和她的地产之间的界限。
  ◇ **National boundaries** are becoming increasingly meaningless in the global economy. 在全球经济中，国界变得越来越没有意义。
  ◇ Electronic publishing is **blurring the boundaries between** dictionaries **and** encyclopedias. 电子出版正在模糊字典和百科全书之间的边界。（作比喻义）
  **border/ frontier** 国界
  ✎ the Italian <u>border/ frontier</u> 意大利边境
  ✎ the <u>border/ frontier between</u> China <u>and</u> Russia 中俄边境

+ **overtake** vt.（坏事）突然降临（一般过去式 overtook；过去分词 overtaken）
  ✎ A sudden illness <u>overtook</u> him. 他突然间得了一场病。
  近义表达（同样多指不好的事）：
  **visit/ befall** (befell - befallen) vt. **<span id="⚓befall">（🪐）</span>**
  ✎ A sudden illness <u>visited/ befell</u> him.
  **happen to**
  ✎ A sudden illness <u>happened to</u> him.
+ **predecessor** n. 前辈，前任
  **successor** 继任者
  相关词辨析：
  **ancestor(s), forefather(s), forebear(s)** [pl.] 祖宗；祖先
  **descendant** [C] 后代
  ✎ He is a direct <u>descendant</u> of Confucius. 他是孔子的直系后裔。
  **offspring** [C] 后代（单复数同形）
  ✎ the conflict between parents and their <u>offspring</u> 父母与子女之间的冲突
  **posterity** [U] 后代，子孙（泛指） **posterior** a. 在后面的；时间上发生晚一些的
  ✎ These works of art are preserved for <u>posterity</u>. 这些艺术品是为后代保存下去的。

+ **meadow** n. （河畔）草地；牧场
  相关词：
  **lawn**（家里的）草坪
  **pasture** 牧场
  **prairie** 草原（北美洲）
  **savanna(h)** 草原（热带、亚热带）
  **grassland** 草原（不限地区） ✎ the Inner Mongolian <u>Grassland</u> 内蒙古大草原
+ ┏ **occurrence** n. 事情，事件
  ┗ **occur** v. 发生
  ┏ **happening** 事件；发生的事情（常指不寻常的）
  ┗ **happen** v. 发生
  近义词 - **事件**：
  **trifle** 琐事，鸡毛蒜皮的小事
  **incident** 小事；事件
  ✎ a border <u>incident</u> 一起边境事件
  ✎ a shooting <u>incident</u> 一起枪击事件
  **affair** 公众性、政治性的事件；风流韵事
  ✎ current <u>affairs</u> 时事
  ✎ China’s internal <u>affairs</u> 中国的内部事务
  ✎ love <u>affairs</u> 桃色新闻
  **event** 重大事件
  **accident/ contingency** 意外事件
  **coincidence** 偶发事件，巧合的事
+ **proportion** n. 比例 **<span id="⚓proportion">（🪐）</span>**
  **the proportion of sth. to sth.** 前者对后者的比例
  ✎ What’s <u>the proportion of</u> boys <u>to</u> girls in your class? 你们班男生和女生的比例是多少？
  **in proportion to sth.** 成比例
  ✎ Payment will be <u>in proportion to</u> the work done, not <u>to</u> the time spent doing it. 报仇将与完成的工作量成比例，而不是与花费的时间成比例。
  **out of (all) proportion to sth.**（完全）不成比例
  ✎ They earn salaries <u>out of all proportion to</u> their ability. 他们挣的工资与他们的能力完全不成比例。
  ┏ **a <u>high/ large</u> proportion of……** 大多数……，大部分……（指人指事物都可，跟可数不可数都可）
  ┗ **a <u>small/ tiny</u> proportion of……** 少数……，一小部分……
  ┏ **a <u>high/ large</u> percentage of……** ~
  ┗ **a <u>small/ tiny</u> percentage of……** ~
  ┏ **<u>a/ the</u> majority of……** ~
  ┗ **<u>a/ the</u> minority of……** ~
  ┏ **a <u>vast/ great/ overwhelming</u> majority of……** 绝大多数
  ┗ **a <u>small/ tiny</u> minority of……** 极少数
+ **site** vt. 使位于
  **= locate = situate**
  ✎ The house <u>is sited/ located/ situated</u> on the hill.
  **site** n. 位置
  **location, situation** n.
+ **juncture** n.(fml.) 时刻，关头
  **At this juncture** 在这个时刻/关头
  ✎ <u>At this juncture</u> it’s too late to say anything. 在这个时刻，说什么都为时已晚。
  **<u>critical/ crucial</u> juncture** 关键时刻
  ✎ The battle had reached a <u>critical/ crucial juncture</u>. 战斗已到了关键时刻。
  近义词 - 时刻：
  **time, moment, point, instant**（都与介词 at 搭配，如：at this time）
+ **unduly = excessively** ad. 过分地，过度地
  ✎ The levels of pollution in this area are <u>unduly</u> high. 这个地区的污染程度过高。
  ✎ He did not sound <u>unduly</u> worried at the prospect. 他听起来对前景并不过分担心。
  **undue = excessive** a. 过分的，过度的
  ✎ The work should be carried out without <u>undue</u> delay. 这项工作不应过度地拖延。
  ✎ We did not want to put any <u>undue</u> pressure on them. 我们不想给他们施加过分的压力。
  **due** a. 适当的 proper, suitable
  ✎ After <u>due</u> consideration, we have decided to appoint Mr.Davis to the job. 经过适当的考虑，我们决定任命戴维斯先生担任这项职务。
+ ┏ **submerge** v. 淹没，潜入水中
  ┗ **emerge** v. 浮现
  **submarine** 潜水艇
  **dive** 跳水；潜水 **diver/ frogman** 潜水员；跳水者 / 蛙人
  **plunge into……** 纵身跳入水中（L10、L42）
  **<u>go down/ go under/ go to the bottom</u>**（船）沉没
  ✎ The tragic sinking of this great liner will always be remembered, for she <u>went down</u> on her first voyage with heavy loss of life.（L10）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ <u>Our neighbour</u>, the river
  同位语前置
  ✎ <u>man’s best friend</u>, the dog 狗，人类最好的朋友
  ✎ <u>God Almighty</u>, Jesus Christ 耶稣基督，全能的上帝
+ **play a……<u>role/ part</u> in……** 在……发挥……作用
  ✎ 西安市在中国历史上有至关重要的作用。
  The city of Xi’an <u>played a</u> crucial <u>role</u> in the history of China.
  ✎ 政府在促进人权方面应该发挥更显著的作用。
  The government should <u>play a</u> more prominent <u>part in</u> promoting human rights.
  ✎ Not all sounds made by animals serve as language, and we have only to turn to that extraordinary discovery of echo-location in bats to see a case <u>in</u> which the voice <u>plays a</u> strictly utilitarian <u>role</u>.（B4L7）
  ✎ The fact of first-rate importance is the predominant <u>role</u> that custom <u>plays in</u> experience and in belief, and the very great varieties it may manifest.（B4L44）
  ✎ John Dewey has said in all seriousness that the <u>part played</u> by custom <u>in</u> shaping the behavior of the individual, as against any way in which he can affect traditional custom, is as the proportion of the total vocabulary of his mother tongue against those words of his own baby talk that are taken up into the vernacular of his family.（B4L44）
+ ┏ <u>Without it</u> we <u>could</u> not make a living.（原文）
  ┗ <u>If we didn’t have it</u> we <u>could</u> not make a living.（原文补全）
  **If + S. + did/ were, S. + <u>would/ should/ could/ might</u> + do** 与现在事实相反的“if”型的虚拟语气（详见L17笔记）
  ┏ There <u>would</u> be no living things <u>without air</u>.
  ┗ There <u>would</u> be no living things <u>if there **were** no air</u>.
  ┏ <u>In his position</u>, I <u>would</u> commit suicide.
  ┗ <u>If I **were** in his position</u>, I <u>would</u> commit suicide.
+ **<u>make/ earn</u> a living** 赚钱谋生，活下去
+ **the house** 家庭
  ✎ Be quiet or you’ll wake <u>the house</u>. 安静点，不然你会吵醒全家人。
  用地方指代此地的人：
  **the village** 全村人；**the town** 全镇人；**the city** 全城人；
  **the country** 全国人；**the world** 全世界人
  ✎ entertain <u>the world</u> 娱乐全世界（某电影公司口号）
  ✎ <u>The whole country was/ were</u> shocked at the news. 全国人民对这个消息都感到震惊。
+ ┏ …… we have to pump from the river for <u>farm use</u>.（原文）
  ┗ …… we have to pump from the river for <u>irrigation</u>. 灌溉（同义表达）
  ┗ …… we have to pump from the river to <u>irrigate the fields</u>.（同义表达）
+ **instinctively = by instinct** 本能地
  ad. | prep. + n. | 汉 
  ---- | ---- | ---- 
  particularly | in particular | 尤其地，特别地
  accidentally | by accident | 偶然地，意外地
  carefully | with care | 小心地
  delightedly | with delight | 高兴地
  angrily | with anger | 愤怒地

+ ┏ …… misfortune might <u>overtake</u> us……（原文）
  ┗ …… misfortune might <u>visit/ befall</u> us……（同义替换）
  ┗ …… misfortune might <u>happen to</u> us……（同义替换）
+ **relate sth. to sb.** 把某事讲给某人听
  ✎ She <u>related</u> the events of the previous week <u>to</u> the police. 她向警方讲述了上周发生的事件。
  **relate A <u>to/ with</u> B** 把A和B联系起来
  近义表达：
  **<u>report/ recount/ relate</u> sth. to sb.** 把某事讲给某人听
  **tell sb. (about) sth.** 告诉某人（关于）某事（的情况）
  ✎ After telling several of his friends about the theft,……（L16）
  ✎ After <u>reporting</u> the theft to several of his friends……（L16课后题-10）
+ **<u>go/ row/ sail</u> upstream** 逆流而上
  ✎ Learning is like <u>rowing upstream</u>: not to advance is to drop back. 学习如逆水行舟，不进则退。
  **<u>go/ row/ sail</u> downstream** 顺流而下
+ a predecessor of ours
  = one of our predecessors
+ **hard by……** (fml.) very near to……
  ✎ The cafeteria stands <u>hard by</u> our dormitory. 食堂紧挨着我们的宿舍。
+ ┏ **heat wave** 酷暑时期，三伏天
  ┗ **cold spell** 严寒时期，三九天（spell n. 一段时间）
  ┏ It’s a **<u>boiling/ scorching/ sizzling</u> hot** day. 这真是个大热天。
  ┗ It’s a **<u>bitterly/ biting/ freezing</u> cold** day. 这真是个大冷天。
+ ┏ We welcome the seasons……（原文）
  ┗ We celebrate the arrival of the seasons.（同义表达）
+ midsummer 仲夏
  Mid-Autumn Festival 中秋节
  Dragon Boat Festival 端午节
+ **Thanksgiving Day** 感恩节 the fourth Thursday in November
  the Puritans 清教徒；the Mayflower 五月花号；Columbus 哥伦布
  <u>American Indians/ Native Americans</u> 印第安人（后者更显尊重）
  <u>the Pilgrims/ the Pilgrim Fathers</u> 朝圣者
  roast turkey 烤火鸡；apple pie 苹果派
  ✎ I <u>give thanks to</u> my mother <u>for</u> supporting me all the time. 我感谢母亲一直以来的支持。
  ✎ I <u>give thanks to</u> my math teacher <u>for</u> not flunking me. 我感谢我的数学老师没有让我不及格。
+ 【✔】This is a <u>rare</u> <u>occurrence</u> 这事很少发生（原文-名词更显正式）
  【◐】This <u>rarely/ seldom</u> <u>occurs</u>.
  **<u>a/ an</u> <u>rare/ common/ regular/ everyday</u> occurrence** 很少/经常/有规律地/每天都发生
  ✎ Laughter was <u>a rare occurrence</u> in his classroom. 笑声在他的课堂上很少见。
  ✎ Unfortunately,computer errors are <u>a common occurrence</u>. 不幸的是，计算机经常会出故障。
  ✎ Street-fights are <u>an everyday occurrence</u> in this area of the city. 街头斗殴在这个城市地区每天都会发生。
+ **go to extremes** 走极端，太过分
  ✎ Editors of newspapers and magazines often <u>go to extremes</u> to provide their reader with unimportant facts and statistics.（L5）
+ ┏ our climate seldom goes to extremes（原文）
  ┗ our climate is usually <u>moderate</u> 温和的（同义表达）
+ **spell** v. 招致，导致 to cause sth. bad to happen in the future
  **spell <u>disaster/ trouble/ danger</u> for……** 对……构成灾难/麻烦/危险
  ✎ The lack of rain could <u>spell disaster for</u> farmers. 缺少雨水可能会给农民带来灾难。
  ✎ This cold weather could <u>spell trouble for</u> gardeners. 这种寒冷的天气可能会给园丁们带来麻烦。
+ **creep** v. 蹑手蹑脚地走
  ✎ Nevertheless, I managed to <u>creep</u> down into the living room for two days before anyone found me out.（L50）
  拟人举例：
  ✎ Curiosity <u>swallowed</u> him. 好奇心吞噬了他。
  ✎ A gentle breeze <u>caressed</u> my cheeks and <u>soothed</u> my heart. 一阵微风拂过我的脸颊，抚慰了我的心。
+ **stall** n. 牲口棚，马厩，牛棚 an enclosed area in a building for an animal such as a horse or cow
+ **stand to do sth.** 可能…… to be likely to do or have something
  **stand to <u>gain/ lose/ win</u>……** 可能获得/损失/赢
  ✎ Many small companies <u>stand to lose</u> financially if the new law is introduced. 如果推行新法律，许多小公司可能将在经济上遭受损失。
+ **low** ad.（地势）很低地
  ✎ The plane flew <u>low</u>. 飞机在很低地飞行。
  **lowly** a. 卑微的，低等的 humble
  ✎ a <u>lowly</u> servant 一个地位卑微的仆人
+ **put…… out of order** 使出故障
  **put…… in order = put…… right** 修好
  ✎ When lights fuse, furniture gets rickety, pipes get clogged, or vacuum cleaners fail to operate, some women assume that their husbands will somehow <u>put things right</u>.（L46）
  **be out of order** 坏了
  ✎ The bell had <u>been out of order</u> for many years. 这个大钟已经坏了很多年了。
  **put sb. out of business** 使破产
  **put sb. out of work** 使失业
  **out of……** 在……之外
  ✎ I am <u>out of</u> patience. 我现在没有耐心了。
  ✎ I am <u>out of</u> anger. 我生气了。
  ✎ The TV is <u>out of</u> repair. 这台电视坏了。
  **out of + n.** 出于……
  ✎ <u>out of</u> <u>sympathy/ pity</u> 出于同情
  ✎ <u>out of</u> interest 出于兴趣
  ✎ <u>out of</u> respect 出于敬意
  ✎ <u>out of</u> conscience 出于良心
  ✎ <u>out of</u> necessity 出于必要
  ✎ <u>out of</u> desperation 出于绝望
  ✎ So let us begin anew — remembering on both sides that civility is not a sign of weakness, and sincerity is always subject to proof. Let us never negotiate <u>out of fear</u>, but let us never fear to negotiate.
  所以，让我们重新开始——双方都要记住，谦恭不是懦弱的表现，真诚永远取决于证据。让我们绝不要出于恐惧而去谈判，但让我们绝不要恐惧谈判。（主语不是人）（回文修辞）（小肯尼迪就职演说）
+ ┏ …… find out how they were managing.（原文）
  ┗ …… find out how they were managing <u>to deal with it</u>.（原文补全）
+ ┏ …… get a <u>sweeping view</u> 俯瞰，鸟瞰
  ┗ …… get a <u>bird’s eye view</u>
+ ┏ …… at the most critical juncture……（原文）
  ┗ ……, when the flood <u>was at its height</u>…… 洪水最猛烈的时候（近义表达）
  ┗ ……, <u>at the height of</u> the flood……
  **the height of……** ……的极限/巅峰状态
  ✎ August is <u>the height of</u> summer. 八月正是盛夏时节。
  ✎ The storm <u>is at its height</u>. 暴风雨正处在最猛烈的时候。
  ✎ — and <u>when the flood was at its height</u> we took turns in watching that point.（课后题-10）
+ ┏ **take turns (in) doing sth.** 轮流
  ┗ **take turns to do sth.**
  ┏ There is only one computer, so we have to <u>take turns (in) using</u> it.
  ┗ There is only one computer, so we have to <u>take turns to use</u> it.
  我们这里只有一台电脑，我们只能轮流使用。
+ **sign** 迹象，征兆，兆头
  **= indication = omen**
  ┏ a good <u>omen</u> 吉兆
  ┗ a bad <u>omen</u> 凶兆

#### 👾 **全部倒装 / 完全倒装（复制自L10） <span id="⚓全部倒装">（🪐）</span>**
即把全部谓语置于主语之前。
1. **表示位置或次序的状语置于句首，只要满足两个条件，要用全部倒装：**
  **① 主语不是代词；**
  **② 谓语动词不是及物动词。**
  **这种倒装主要目的是为了突出句末的主语。**
  + 表**位置**的例句
    ✎ <u>In **came**</u> Miss Green. 格林小姐走了进来。
    ┏ <u>On the hill **stands**</u> a temple. 山上有座庙。
    ┗ A temple stands on the hill. （正常语序）
    ┏ <u>There **are**</u> two people. （there be 句型其实就是全部倒装）
    ┗ Two people are there.（正常语序）
    ✎ <u>There</u> once <u>**stood**</u> a little village.（there be 句型的变型）
  + 表**次序**的例句
    ✎ <u>Now **comes**</u> your turn. 现在该你了。（now 表示次序）
    ✎ <u>Next **came**</u> a horse, ……（L56）（next 表示次序）
  + 无法倒装情况举例
    ✎ Off <u>he</u> went. 他出去了。（off表位置）（he 是代词，故无法倒装）
    ✎ On the hill John <u>saw</u> Marry. （see 是及物动词，故无法倒装）
2. **表语置于句首。**
  **这种倒装主要目的是为了避免头重脚轻（主语较长）。（非强制，不倒装也行）**
  ┏ Happy is <u>he who has a sound mind in a sound body</u>.（倒装语序）
  ┏ <u>He who has a sound mind in a sound body</u> is happy.（正常语序）
  ┗ 一个身心健康的人是快乐的。
  ✎ Gone are <u>the days when my heart was young and gay</u>. 我的心是年轻和快乐的日子一去不复返了。
3. **更多用法，后续补充……**
+ ┏ …… prevent its landing anywhere……（原文 - 动名词 + 属格）
  ┗ …… <u>prevent</u> it <u>from</u> landing anywhere……（近义表达：prevent…… from…… 阻止某人做某事）
  ✎ He always <u>insisted on its being written out</u> in full.（L22课后题-5）
+ Noah’s ark 诺亚方舟
  the Genesis 《创世纪》（圣经旧约的第一章）
  the New Testament (Christians) 新约
  the Old Testament (Jews) 旧约
  deluge 大洪水
+ **sound** a. 完好的 in good condition and not damaged in any way
  ✎ The floor was completely <u>sound</u>. 地板完全完好无损。
  ✎ Is the building structurally <u>sound</u>? 这座建筑结构还完好吗？
+ **stout = sturdy** a. 粗壮的，结实的 strong and thick
  ✎ <u>stout</u> boots for climbing 用于登山的结实的靴子
  ✎ a <u>stout</u> walking-stick 粗壮的手杖
+ **wade** 趟水
  **trek** 跋涉，（尤指在山中）徒步旅行
+ **in the hope <u>of/ that</u>……**（常作状语）
  ┏ …… <u>in the hope of</u> being able to……（原文）
  ┗ …… <u>in the hope that</u> they would be able to……（同义替换）
  ✎ Police are carrying out a house-to-house search <u>in the hope of</u> finding the missing girl. 警方正在挨家挨户搜查，希望找到失踪的女孩。
  **in + n. 作状语，相当于原因状语从句**（L53）
  ✎ The men of our family waded down through our flooded meadows with boathooks, <u>in the hope of being (= because they hope to be)</u> able to grapple a corner of the raft and pull it out of the current towards our bank.（本文）
  ✎ The Swedes were the first to recognize that public officials like civil servants, police officers, health inspectors or tax-collectors can make mistakes or act over-zealously <u>in the belief (= because they believe)</u> that they are serving the public.（L53）
  ✎ In the lift her thoughts were on lunch and a good rest; but when she got out at her own floor, both were forgotten <u>in her sudden discovery (= because she suddenly discovered)</u> that her front door was open.（L58）
  ✎ They leave unwanted objects in drawers, cupboards and attics for years, <u>in the belief that (= because they believe that)</u> they may one day need just those very things.（L59）
  ✎ Young men who have reason to fear that they will be killed in battle may justifiably feel bitter <u>in the thought (= because they think)</u> that they have been cheated of the best things that life has to offer.（B4L11）
+ **grapple** v. 紧紧抓住，扭住，扭打 to take a firm hold of sb./sth. and struggle with them
  ✎ They managed to <u>grapple</u> him to the ground. 他们设法扭住他并将他摁倒在地。
+ 【✔】We still think it a miracle <u>that they were able to do so</u>.（原文-形式宾语）
  【◐】We still think that it was a miracle that they were able to do so.（双重复合句-啰嗦）

---

## **Lesson 57 - Back in the old country**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>I stopped to let the car cool off and to study the map. I had expected to be near my objective by now, but everything still seemed alien to me. I was only five when my father had taken me abroad, and that was eighteen years ago. When my mother had died after a tragic accident, he did not quickly recover from the shock and loneliness. Everything around him was full of her presence, continually reopening the wound. So he decided to emigrate. In the new country he became absorbed in making a new life for the two of us, so that he gradually ceased to grieve. He did not marry again and I was brought up without a woman’s care; but I lacked for nothing, for he was both father and mother to me. He always meant to go back one day, but not to stay. His roots and mine had become too firmly embedded in the new land. But he wanted to see the old folk again and to visit my mother’s grave. He became mortally ill a few months before we had planned to go and, when he knew that he was dying, he made me promise to go on my own.

I hired a car the day after landing and bought a comprehensive book of maps, which I found most helpful on the cross-country journey, but which I did not think I should need on the last stage. It was not that I actually remembered anything at all. But my father had described over and over again what we should see at every milestone, after leaving the nearest town, so that I was positive I should recognize it as familiar territory. Well, I had been wrong, for I was now lost.

I looked at the map and then at the milometer. I had come ten miles since leaving the town, and at this point, according to my father, I should be looking at farms and cottages in a valley, with the spire of the church of our village showing in the far distance. I could see no valley, no farms, no cottages and no church spire — only a lake. I decided that I must have taken a wrong turning somewhere. So I drove back to the town and began to retrace the route, taking frequent glances at the map. I landed up at the same corner. The curious thing was that the lake was not marked on the map. I felt as if I had stumbled into a nightmare country, as you sometimes do in dreams. And, as in a nightmare, there was nobody in sight to help me. Fortunately for me, as I was wondering what to do next, there appeared on the horizon a man on horseback, riding in my direction. I waited till he came near, then I asked him the way to our old village. He said that there was now no village. I thought he must have misunderstood me, so I repeated its name. This time he pointed to the lake. The village no longer existed because it had been submerged, and all the valley too. The lake was not a natural one, but a man-made reservoir.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **alien** a. 外国的；外星的
  ✎ <u>alien</u> cultures 外国文化
  ✎ <u>alien</u> beings 外星人
  **be alien to……** 对……来说是陌生的/格格不入的（作表语）
  ✎ The idea <u>is alien to</u> our religion. 这个想法与我们的宗教格格不入。
  ✎ Luxury <u>is alien to</u> her nature. 奢侈与她的天性格格不入。
  同义表达：
  **be foreign to……**
  ✎ Jealousy <u>is foreign to</u> his nature. 嫉妒与他的本性格格不入。/他绝对不是一个会嫉妒别人的人。
  近义词：
  **exotic** a.外国的；新奇漂亮的（褒义）
  ✎ <u>exotic</u> tropical plants 来自异域的热带植物
  ✎ I am charmed with her <u>exotic</u> beauty. 我被她异国情调的美丽迷住了。
+ ┏ **emigrate** v. 移居国外（仅指人）
  ┗ **migrate** 迁移；迁徙（不一定是国外，指人指动物）
  ┗ **immigrate** 移民，（从外地）移居
  **migrate to** 迁移到
  ✎ People <u>migrate to</u> cities in search of work. 人们迁移到城市寻找工作。
  ✎ Swallows <u>migrate</u> south in winter. 燕子在冬天时会迁徙到南方。
  **emigrate from**
  **immigrate to**
  ✎ Europeans <u>emigrating from</u> their homelands after World War Ⅱ were encouraged to <u>immigrate to</u> Australia. 二战后，从祖国移民出去的欧洲人被鼓励移民到澳大利亚去。
  词性变化：
  v. | n.（行为） | n.（对象）
  ---- | ---- | ----
  migrate | migration | migrant
  immigrate | immigration | immigrant
  emigrate | emigration | emigrant

+ **absorb** v. 使全神贯注（使役动词）
  ┏ **be <u>absorb</u>ed in……** 全神贯注于……
  ┗ **be <u>engross</u>ed in……**
  ┗ **be <u>wrap</u>ped up in……**
  ┗ **be <u>immerse</u>d in……**
  ✎ He <u>is</u> totally <u>immersed in</u> the novel. 他完全沉浸在了小说中。
  近义表达 - 忙碌（L6）：
  **be busy (in) doing** 忙于做某事
  **be up to one’s <u>neck/ ears/ eyes</u> in……** 忙于……（口语习语）
  ✎ M: Can you come over for dinner tonight?
  W: I<u>’m up to my ears in</u> work, so I’ll have to take a rain check.（take a rain check 改日，择期(习语)）
  Q: What does the woman mean?
  Answer: She’d enjoy coming to dinner another time.（托福听力真题）
+ **embedded** a. 嵌入的
  **embed** v. 把……嵌入/放入/埋入/插入
  ┏ **be (firmly) <u>embed</u>ded in……** 深深地扎根/陷于……中
  ┗ **be (firmly) <u>root</u>ed in……**
  ┗ **be (firmly) <u>entrench</u>ed in……**
  ┗ **be (firmly) <u>ingrain</u>ed in……**
  ✎ His roots and mine had <u>become</u> too <u>firmly embedded in</u> the new land.（本文）
  ✎ He had lived in it as a child when it was already disappearing, and his hero <u>was firmly rooted in</u> his memories and experiences, and in both the history and the mythology of the vanished frontier.（B4L21）
  相关表达（L50）：
  **deep-seated/ deep-rooted** 根深蒂固的（中性，通常指事物）
  ✎ a <u>deep-seated/ deep-rooted</u> <u>bad habit/ faith in god</u> 一个根深蒂固的坏习惯/坚定的对上帝的信仰
  **inveterate** a. 根深蒂固的，积习难改的（多贬义，指人、指事物都可）
  ✎ <u>inveterate</u> <u>hatred/ prejudice/ distrust</u> 深深的仇恨/偏见/不信任
  ✎ an <u>inveterate</u> <u>smoker/ drinker/ gambler/ liar</u> 一个老烟鬼/老酒鬼/赌棍/撒谎成性的人
+ **milestone** n. 里程碑；划时代事件
  **milestone in……** ……的里程碑
  ✎ October 1^st^, 1949 was a <u>milestone in</u> the history of China. 1949年10月1日是中国历史上的一个里程碑。
  **mark a milestone in……** 标志着……的里程碑
  ✎ This voyage <u>marked an</u> important <u>milestone in</u> the history of exploration. 这次航行标志着探险史上的一个重要里程碑。
  **a milestone <u>on/ along</u> the road to……** 在通往……道路上的一个里程碑
  ✎ We believe that what we have agreed today will be <u>a milestone on the road to</u> true peace and prosperity in our country. 我们相信，我们今天达成的协议将是我国实现真正和平与繁荣道路上的一个里程碑。
  **crossroads** n. 十字路口；抉择关头（单复数同形）
  **at a crossroads** 处在十字路口
  ✎ He was <u>at a crossroads</u> in his career. 他正处于职业生涯的十字路口。
+ **territory**
  + n1.[U]&[C] 领土，地盘
    ✎ <u>enemy/ disputed/ foreign</u> <u>territory</u> 敌占区/有争议的地区/外国领土
    ✎ occupied <u>territories</u> 被占领的领土
    ✎ They refused to allow UN troops to be stationed in their <u>territory</u>. 他们拒绝允许联合国部队驻扎在他们的领土上。
    ✎ A tiger has a large <u>territory</u> to defend. 老虎有广阔的领地需要捍卫。
    ✎ A dog uses urine to <u>mark</u> its <u>territory</u>. 狗用尿液标记自己的领地。
  + n2.[U]（知识或经验的）领域
    **<u>familiar/ unfamiliar</u> <u>territory</u>** 熟悉/不熟悉（的领域）
    ✎ The company is moving into <u>unfamiliar territory</u> with this new software. 该公司正借助这款新软件进入一个陌生的领域。
    ✎ Social work is <u>familiar territory</u> to her. 社会工作对她来说是熟悉的领域。
+ **stumble** v. 绊脚 **= trip**
  英文释义：strike one’s foot against sth. and almost fall
  ✎ In her hurry she <u>stumbled</u> and spilled the milk all over the floor. 匆忙中，她被绊了一下，把牛奶洒得满地都是。
  **stumble <u>over/ on</u>…… = trip <u>over/ on</u>……** 在……上绊了一下
  ✎ Vic <u>stumbled over</u> the step as he came in. 维克进来时在台阶上绊了一下。
  ✎ Running along the beach, she <u>stumbled on</u> a log and fell on the sand. 当她沿着海滩跑时，在一根木头上绊了一下，摔倒在了沙滩上。
  **stumble <u>across/ on/ upon</u>……** 偶然发现或遇到…… to find sth. or meet sb. by accident
  **= come across……**
  ✎ We <u>stumbled across</u> him at the mall. 我们在商场偶然遇见了他。
  ✎ Police investigating tax fraud <u>stumbled across</u> a drugs ring. 调查税务欺诈的警方偶然发现了一个贩毒集团。
  ✎ History relates that they <u>stumbled on</u> a magnificent waterfall. 历史记载，他们偶然发现了一座壮观的瀑布。
  **stumble into……** 偶然卷入、参与或陷入…… to become involved in sth. by chance
  ✎ I <u>stumbled into acting</u> when I left college. 我从大学出来后偶然地进了演艺界。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **cool off** v. 冷却下来，凉爽下来 to return to a normal temperature after being hot
  ✎ <u>Cool off</u> with an iced drink. 喝一杯冰饮料凉快一下。
  ✎ By late autumn Mediterranean islands have <u>cooled off</u>, and can have rainy days. 到深秋，地中海岛屿已经凉爽下来，可能会有雨天。
  **study** v. 仔细察看（某事物） examine (sth.) very carefully
  ✎ <u>study</u> the <u>map/ menu/ ……</u> 仔细地察看地图/菜单……
  ✎ Scientists are <u>studying</u> the photographs of Mars for signs of life. 科学家们正在仔细地察看火星的照片，以寻找生命的迹象。
+ **expect (sb.) to do** 以为；料想
  ✎ He didn’t <u>expect to</u> see me. 他没想到会见到我。
  ✎ We <u>expected</u> him <u>to</u> arrive yesterday. 我们本以为他昨天就到。
+ **objective** n. 目标，目的 **= goal**
  ✎ Everest is the climber’s next <u>objective</u>. 珠穆朗玛峰是登山者的下一个目标。
  ✎ Let justice be our <u>objective</u>. 让正义成为我们的目标。
+ **by now**（L25）
  相当于 by then，用 by now 更有代入感。
  ✎ After crossing the Equator, the captain called in at a port to have a new rudder fitted, but <u>by now</u> the *Thermopylae* was over five hundred miles ahead.（L25）
+ **be alien to……** 对……来说是陌生的/格格不入的
  ✎ a way of life that <u>is</u> totally <u>alien to</u> us 一种对我们来说完全陌生的生活方式
  ✎ The idea <u>is alien to</u> our religion. 这个想法与我们的宗教格格不入。
  ✎ Luxury <u>is alien to</u> her nature. 奢侈与她的天性格格不入。
+ **recover from……** 从……恢复（L43、L44）
  ✎ You will not have to spend the next few days <u>recovering from</u> a long and arduous journey.（L44）
  **recover sth.**
  1. 恢复…… **= <u>restore sth./ regain sth.</u>**
    **recover, restore, regain** vt. 恢复了（下文以“r3”指代）
    ✎ <u>r3</u> one’s health 恢复了健康
    ✎ <u>r3</u> one’s sight 恢复了视力
    ✎ <u>r3</u> one’s consciousness 恢复了意识
    ✎ <u>r3</u> one’s balance 恢复了平衡
    ✎ <u>r3</u> one’s composure 恢复了镇静
  2. vt. 重新获得，找回，赚回，补偿
    ✎ Four paintings stolen from the gallery have <u>been recovered</u>. 画廊失窃的四幅画已被追回。
    ✎ We <u>recovered</u> lost time by setting out early. 我们通过提早出发，弥补了损失的时间。
    ✎ But the claim made by a local authority to <u>recover</u> the cost of salvaging a sunken pie dish must surely be unique.（L43）
+ **presence**（L54、L55）
  + n1. 出席，在场，存在
    ✎ We enjoy staring at them, entranced as they go about their business, unaware (we hope) of our <u>presence</u>.（L54）
    ✎ At present, there is no telescope in existence that is capable of detecting the <u>presence</u> of life.（L55）
    ┏ **in the presence of sb.** 在某人在场的情况下
    ┗ **in sb.’s presence** （代词情况）
    ✎ Harry is very thrifty, but <u>in the presence of</u> his friends he never shows this side of his life. 哈里非常节约，但在朋友面前，他从不展现自己生活的这方面。
    ✎ I asked you not to smoke <u>in my presence</u>. 我请求你在我在场时别抽烟。
  + n2. 似乎在场，感觉在附近的人（或鬼魂）
    英文释义：a person or spirit that you cannot see but that you feel is with you in a place
    ✎ His daughter’s <u>presence</u> seemed to fill her empty bedroom. 他女儿的身影似乎充满了她空荡荡的卧室。
+ **continually** 总是（有中断，强调频繁发生，且多指不愉快的事情） **<a href="#⚓continually">（🚀L54）</a>**
  **continuously** 连续不断地（不中断）（L18）
  ✎ Everything around me is full of <u>his/ her</u> <u>presence</u>, <u>continually</u> reopening the wound. 我周围的一切都充满了他/她的印记，不断地揭开伤口。
+ **make a new life for sb.** 为某人开创新生活
  ✎ I was determined to <u>make a new life for myself</u> in Australia. 我决心在澳大利亚为自己创开创新的生活。
  ✎ After the divorce she moved to Buckingham to <u>make a new life for herself</u>. 离婚后，她搬到了白金汉，开始了新的生活。
  辨：
  **turn over a new leaf** 弃恶从善，洗心革面重做人
  ✎ The thief was determined to <u>turn over a new leaf</u> once he was released from prison. 这个小偷决心出狱后改过自新。
+ **cease to do** 不再……（L35）
  ✎ There are rare instances when justice almost <u>ceases to be</u> an abstract concept.（L35）
+ **grieve** v. 悲伤（多用于亲人故去）to feel extremely sad, especially because someone you love has died
  **grieve <u>over/ for</u>……** 为了……而悲伤
  ✎ They are still <u>grieving over/ for</u> their dead child. 他们仍在为死去的孩子悲伤。（不及物）
  ✎ She <u>grieved</u> the death of her husband. 她为丈夫的去世感到悲痛。（及物）
  **grievance** n. 委屈，不平，不满，牢骚 **<a href="#⚓grievance">（🚀L53）</a>**
  ✎ A parliamentary committee representing all political parties appoints a person who is suitably qualified to investigate private <u>grievances</u> against the State.（L53）
+ **bring up sb.** 把某人抚养成人
+ **lack sth.** 缺乏……
  辨：
  **lack for sth.** (fml.) = **need sth.** 需要……
  **lack for nothing** 应有尽有
+ **语义相对的名词并列，常省略冠词**
  ✎ <u>Father and son</u> went to New York by a morning train. 父子俩乘早班火车去了纽约。
  ✎ We are <u>brother and sister</u>. 我们俩是兄妹。
  ✎ <u>Husband and wife</u> are talking about the boy’s future. 夫妻俩正在谈论男孩的未来。
  ✎ Please pass me <u>pencil and paper</u>. 请把铅笔和纸递给我。
+ **mean to do sth.** 打算做某事，~~意味着做某事~~
  ✎ Whoops! I didn’t <u>mean to</u> step on your toe. 哇！我不是故意踩到你的脚趾的。
  ✎ I <u>mean to</u> leave that meeting with a new contract. 我打算带着一份新合同离开那次会议。
+ **folk** (BrE)/ **folks** (AmE)n. 人们 people
  ✎ ordinary working-class <u>folk</u> 普通工人阶级
  ✎ I’d like a job working with old <u>folk</u> or kids. 我想找一份和老人或孩子在一起的工作。
  ✎ Young <u>folk</u> these days don’t know the meaning of work. 现在的年轻人不知道工作的意义。
+ **visit one’s grave** 扫墓，拜访某人的墓地
**mortally = fatally** ad. 致命地
  ✎ <u>mortally/ fatally</u> <u>ill/ injured/ wounded</u> 致命地疾病/受伤/受伤
  **mortal = fatal** a.
  ✎ a <u>mortal/ fatal</u> <u>illness/ injury/ wound</u> 致命的疾病/伤口/伤口
  **immortal** a. 不朽的
  ✎ Though Verrazano is by no means considered to be a great explorer, his name will probably remain <u>immortal</u>, for on November 21st, 1964, the longest suspension bridge in the world was named after him.（L17）
+ **make sb. do** 让某人做某事
+ **alone = on one’s own = by oneself** 独自地，单独地，无人陪伴地（L22）
  ✎ She was sitting <u>alone</u> on a park bench. 她独自坐在公园的长椅上。
  ✎ I don’t like walking home <u>on my own</u> at night. 我不喜欢晚上独自走回家。
  ✎ Do you share the apartment or do you live <u>by yourself</u>? 你是合住公寓还是一个人住？
  **all + <u>alone/ on one’s own/ by oneself</u>**（加副词all，以强化语气）
  ✎ Wendy was frightened, <u>all alone</u> in that big old house. 温蒂一个人待在那座大房子里，吓坏了。

#### 👾 **双重定语从句**
1. **同一层次上的双重定语从句**
  两个定语从句修饰同一个名词或短语中间用并列连词（and, or 或 but）连接此时关系词往往不可省去。
  ✎ This book is intended for foreign students <u>who have already mastered the elements of English</u>, and <u>who now want to use their knowledge of language to read books on their own subjects</u>.
  这本书是为那些已经掌握了英语基础知识，现在想用他们的语言知识阅读自己学科书籍的外国学生准备的。
  ✎ The past progressive is chiefly used for past actions <u>which continued for some time</u> but <u>whose exact limits are not known</u>.
  过去进行时主要用于过去的动作，即延续了一段时间，但延续的起止时间点不明的动作。
1. **不在同一层次上的双重定语从句**
  第一个定语从句修饰前面的名词或短语，第二个定语从句修饰“名词或短语 + 第一个定语从句”两个定语从句之间没有并列连词连接。第一个定语从句的关系词（一般是关系代词作宾语）可省略。
  ✎ The only person <u>^①^(who/ whom) I know</u> <u>^②^who has a skeleton in the cupboard</u> is George Carlton, and he is very pound of the fact.（L24）

#### 👾 **嵌入式定语从句（Embedded Attributive Clause） <span id="⚓嵌入式定语从句3">（🪐）</span><a href="#⚓嵌入式定语从句">（🚀L42</a> <a href="#⚓嵌入式定语从句2">🚀L48）</a>**
**既是先行词的后置定语，又是另一个分句结构的宾语**
✎ ……, but <u>which **I did not think** I should need on the last stage</u>.（原文）
✎ In this part of the cave, they could hear an insistent booming sound <u>which **they found** was caused by a small waterspout shooting down into a pool from the roof of the cave</u>.（L42）
↳ 解析：划线部分一方面修饰水声，另一方面作加粗部分的宾语。
✎ Turning back down the main street, we quickened our pace and made our way rapidly towards the stream <u>where **we hoped** the boatman was waiting</u>.（L48）

+ **It <u>is/ was</u> not that……, but (that)……** 不是因为……，而是因为……
  ┏ It was not that Bruce always underestimated difficulties. He simply had no sense of danger at all.（L39）
  ┗ <u>It was not that</u> Bruce always underestimated difficulties, <u>but (that)</u> he simply had no sense of danger at all.（合并为一句）
  **not that……, but that……** 不是因为……，而是因为……（L23）
  ✎ <u>Not that</u> I love Caesar less, <u>but that</u> I love Rome more. 不是我不爱凯撒，而是我更爱罗马。/ 不是因为我爱凯撒爱得更少，而是因为我爱罗马爱得更多。（Shakespeare ‘Julius Caesar’）
+ **over and over (again)** 一再地，屡次地，三番五次地
  ✎ I’ve told you <u>over and over (again)</u> not to do that. 我一再告诉你不要那样做。
  同义替换：
  **again and again**
  **time after time**
  **time and (time) again**
  **many times**
  **repeatedly**
+ **be positive (that)……** 对……确定/肯定
  ✎ <u>Are</u> you absolutely <u>positive</u> you locked the door? 你确定你把门锁上了吗？
  同义替换：
  **I was <u>sure/ certain/ confident/ convinced</u> (that)……**
  **I had no doubt (that)……**
  **I bet (that)……**
+ **<u>familiar/ unfamiliar</u> territory** 熟悉/ 不熟悉（的领域）
  ✎ Social work is <u>familiar territory</u> to her. 社会工作对她来说是熟悉的领域。
  ✎ All this is <u>familiar territory</u> to readers of her recent novels. 对读过她新近几本小说的读者来说，这一切都是很熟悉的。
+ **well** interj. 哎呦（表达怀疑、惊讶或愤怒等感情）used for expressing a feeling such as doubt, surprise, or anger
  ✎ <u>Well</u>, they have a lot of nerve! 哎呦呵，他们很有胆量嘛！
  ✎ <u>Well</u>, she could at least have phoned to say she wasn’t coming! 哎呀，她至少可以打电话说她不来了呀！
+ **metre [英] / meter [美]** n. 仪器，仪表（L13）
  作词根：
  ✎ thermo<u>meter</u> 温度表，温度计
  ✎ baro<u>meter</u> 气压表，气压计
  ✎ odo<u>meter</u>/ milo<u>meter</u> 里程表
  ✎ speedo<u>meter</u> 速度表
+ **come = travel** 走过了多远距离
  ✎ Some of the birds have <u>come</u> thousands of miles to winter here. 有些鸟千里迢迢来到这里过冬。

#### 👾 **独立主格结构（L6）**
**(with) + n.（逻辑主语） + 非谓语（doing/ done/ to do。其中being常省略）**，在句中常作状语或定语。
独立主格其实就是加上了本身逻辑主语的非谓语动词。
✎ The silence was suddenly broken when a large car, <u>**with** its headlights (being) on</u> and <u>its horn blaring</u>, roared down the arcade.（L6）
✎ It is possible that upon such an occasion a battle ensued, <u>**with** the sharks being driven away or killed</u>.（B4L18）

+ **decide** 不一定译为“决定”，而常常译为“**（在考虑之后）确定，断定，认为**”，尤其是其后加 that 引导的宾语从句时。（L43、L52）
  ✎ The pie committee <u>decided</u> <u>that the best way to transport the dish would be by canal</u>, so they insured it for the trip.（L43）
  ✎ From then on, Harry <u>decided</u> <u>that this little game he had invented might prove to be expensive</u>.（L52）
+ **turning** (BrE) / **turn** (AmE) n. 道路转弯处
  ◇ He must have **taken a wrong turning** in the dark. 他一定是在黑暗中转错了弯。
  ◇ **Take the first turning** on the left. 在第一个路口左转。
+ **retrace**
  + v1. 折返 to go back exactly the way you have come
    ✎ After a few minutes, he turned around and began to <u>retrace his steps</u>. 几分钟后，他转过身，开始往回走。
  + v2. 重走 repeat (a journey, route, etc.) exactly
    ✎ We shall be <u>retracing the route</u> taken by Marco Polo. 我们将沿着马可波罗的路线走。
    ✎ They are hoping to <u>retrace the epic voyage</u> of Christopher Columbus. 他们希望沿着克里斯托弗·哥伦布的史诗般的航行路线再走一遍。
+ **<u>take/ shoot/ throw/ cast</u> a glance at……** 扫视……
  ✎ The couple at the next table <u>cast quick glances at</u> us. 邻桌的那对夫妇快速地瞥了我们几眼。
  ✎ The other people <u>shot sidelong glances at</u> me. 其他人斜眼一再地扫视我。
+ **land up = end up = finish up** 最终；最后…… to finally be in a particular place or situation
  ✎ He’ll <u>land/ end/ finish up in hospital</u> if he carries on drinking like that. 如果他继续这样喝酒，他最终会住院的。
  **<u>land up/ end up/ finish up</u> doing** 最终；最后……
  ✎ Instead of becoming a doctor, however, he <u>landed up/ ended up/ finished up becoming</u> a successful writer of detective stories.（L24改写）
+ **<u>as if/ as though</u> 从句中表达与事实相反或可能性很小的事情时，可以用虚拟语气。**（L33）
  **与现在事实相反用一般过去时（be 动词一般用 were）；**
  **与过去事实相反用过去完成时；**
  **与未来趋势相反用 <u>would/ should/ could/ might</u> + 动词原形。**
  ✎ It is <u>as if</u> a single unimportant event <u>set</u> up a chain of reactions.（L33）
  ✎ <u>As if</u> this <u>were</u> not enough to reduce you to tears, your husband arrives, unexpectedly bringing three guests to dinner.（L33）
  ✎ It looks <u>as if</u> it <u>might</u> rain. 看起来好像要下雨。
  **注意：<u>as if/ as though</u> 从句中虚拟语气为进行时的时候，一般都用 were doing 的形式。**
  ✎ ‘Oh, that,’ he said with a smile <u>as if</u> he <u>were talking</u> about an old friend.（L24）
  ✎ Suddenly, the knocking turned to a forceful banging, <u>as if</u> someone <u>were hitting</u> the door with a metal rod. 突然，敲门声变成了强烈的砰砰声，仿佛有人在用金属棒敲门。 (《The Da Vinci Code》)
  ✎ It looks <u>as if</u> he <u>were talking</u> to someone invisible. 他好像在和一个看不见的人说话。
+ ┏ I felt as if I had stumbled into a nightmare country, as you sometimes <u>do</u> in dreams.（原文）
  ┗ I felt as if I had stumbled into a nightmare country, as you sometimes <u>stumble into a nightmare country</u> in dreams.（原文展开）
+ **“as + 状语”结构**
  连词 as 引导的方式状语从句中常省略主句中出现过的成分而只残存“as + 状语”结构。
  ↓ And, <u>as in a nightmare</u>, there was nobody in sight to help me.（原文）
  ↳ And, <u>as there is nobody in sight to help me in a nightmare</u>, there was nobody in sight to help me.
  ↓ In New York, <u>as in some other cities</u>, environmental pollution is becoming more and more serious. 在纽约，正如在其他一些城市一样，环境污染正在变得越来越严重。（考研阅读真题）
  ↳ In New York, <u>as environmental pollution is becoming more and more serious in some other cities</u>, environmental pollution is becoming more and more serious.

#### 👾 **全部倒装 / 完全倒装（L10 <a href="#⚓全部倒装">🚀L56</a>）**
┏ ……, there <u>appeared</u> on the horizon a man on horseback,……（原文-倒装语序）
┗ ……, a man on horseback <u>appeared</u> there on the horizon,……（正常语序）

+ **on horseback** 在马背上（horseback 前面不可加冠词，类似举例：by car）
  ✎ a soldier <u>on horseback</u> 一个骑马的士兵
  ✎ They travelled over the mountains <u>on horseback</u>. 他们骑马翻山越岭。
+ **in sb.’s direction** 向某人的方向
  ✎ Tony glanced <u>in her direction</u> and their eyes met. 托尼朝她的方向瞥了一眼，他们的目光相遇了。
+ **<u>ask/ tell/ show</u> sb. the way to……** 向某人问去某地的路
  ✎ He <u>asked</u> me <u>the way to</u> London. 他问我去伦敦的路。
  ✎ Could you <u>tell</u> me <u>the way to</u> the station? 你能告诉我去车站的路吗？
  ✎ Could you please <u>show</u> me <u>the way to</u> the temple? 你能给我指一下去寺庙的路吗？
+ 并列句中，重复的谓语动词常省略
  ┏ The village no longer existed because it <u>had been submerged</u>, **and** all the valley too.（原文-省略）
  ┗ The village no longer existed because it <u>had been submerged</u>, **and** all the valley <u>had been submerged</u> too.（不省略）

---

## **Lesson 58 - A spot of bother**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>The old lady was glad to be back at the block of flats where she lived. Her shopping had tired her and her basket had grown heavier with every step of the way home. In the lift her thoughts were on lunch and a good rest; but when she got out at her own floor, both were forgotten in her sudden discovery that her front door was open. She was thinking that she must reprimand her home help the next morning for such a monstrous piece of negligence, when she remembered that she had gone shopping after the home help had left and she knew that she had turned both keys in their locks. She walked slowly into the hall and at once noticed that all the room doors were open, yet following her regular practice she had shut them before going out. Looking into the drawing room, she saw a scene of confusion over by her writing desk. It was as clear as daylight then that burglars had forced an entry during her absence. Her first impulse was to go round all the rooms looking for the thieves, but then she decided that at her age it might be more prudent to have someone with her, so she went to fetch the porter from his basement. By this time her legs were beginning to tremble, so she sat down and accepted a cup of very strong tea, while he telephoned the police. Then, her composure regained, she was ready to set off with the porter’s assistance to search for any intruders who might still be lurking in her flat.

They went through the rooms, being careful to touch nothing, as they did not want to hinder the police in their search for fingerprints. The chaos was inconceivable. She had lived in the flat for thirty years and was a veritable magpie at hoarding; and it seemed as though everything she possessed had been tossed out and turned over and over. At least sorting out the things she should have discarded years ago was now being made easier for her. Then a police inspector arrived with a constable and she told them of her discovery of the ransacked flat. The inspector began to look for fingerprints, while the constable checked that the front door locks had not been forced, thereby proving that the burglars had either used skeleton keys or entered over the balcony. There was no trace of fingerprints, but the inspector found a dirty red bundle that contained jewellery which the old lady said was not hers. So their entry into this flat was apparently not the burglars’ first job that day and they must have been disturbed. The inspector then asked the old lady to try to check what was missing by the next day and advised her not to stay alone in the flat for a few nights. The old lady thought he was a fussy creature, but since the porter agreed with him, she rang up her daughter and asked for her help in what she described as a little spot of bother.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **composure** n. 镇静，沉着 **<span id="⚓composure">（🪐）</span>**
  **<u>keep/ maintain</u> one’s composure** 保持镇静
  **lose one’s composure** 失去镇静
  **<u>recover/ regain</u> one’s composure** 恢复镇静
  **compose** v. 使镇静
  **<u>compose/ collect</u> oneself** 使某人镇静
  ✎ He took a deep breath to <u>compose/ collect himself</u>. 他深吸一口气，让自己镇定下来。
  **composed/ collected** v. 镇静的，平静的
  ✎ He appeared <u>composed/ collected</u> despite the stress. 尽管有压力，他看上去还是表现得镇定自若。
+ **hinder** v. 妨碍，阻碍
  英文释义：to make it difficult for sth. to develop or succeed
  ✎ a political situation that <u>hinders</u> economic growth 一个阻碍经济增长的政治局面
  ✎ They went through the rooms, being careful to touch nothing, as they did not want to <u>hinder</u> the police in their search for fingerprints.（本文）
  同义词-妨碍（L46）：
  **hamper, impede**
  ✎ Higher interest rates could <u>hinder/ hamper/ impede</u> economic growth. 更高的利率可能会阻碍经济增长。
  ✎ Social unrest will <u>hinder/ hamper/ impede</u> economic development. 社会动荡将阻碍经济发展。
  近义习语：
  **put sand in the wheels of……** 妨碍/阻碍……
  **put obstacles in the way of……**
  **stand in the way of……**
  ✎ These days, it is differences in national regulations, far more than tariffs, that <u>put sand in the wheels of</u> trade between rich countries.（B4L8）
  ✎ The tax <u>puts obstacles in the way of</u> companies trying to develop trade overseas. 这项税收给试图发展海外贸易的公司设置了障碍。
  ✎ The British government would not <u>stand in the way of</u> such a proposal. 英国政府不会阻止这样的提议。
+ **inconceivable** a. 难以置信的，无法想象的
  英文释义：too strange or unusual to be thought real or possible
  ✎ The chaos was <u>inconceivable</u>.（本文）
  ✎ <u>It is inconceivable that</u> a man in such a powerful position could act so unwisely. 令人难以置信的是，一个处于如此强大地位的人竟然会做出如此不明智的行为。
  **conceive** v.(fml.) 设想，想象
  英文释义：to imagine a particular situation or to think about sth. in a particular way
  **conceive of sth.** 设想/想象某事物
  ✎ Many people can’t <u>conceive of</u> a dinner without meat or fish. 许多人无法想象一顿没有肉或鱼的晚餐。
  **conceive of A as B** 把A想象成B（详见L12）
  ✎ The ancients <u>conceived of</u> the world <u>as</u> (being) flat. 古人认为世界是平的。 
  **conceive + 宾语从句**
  ✎ I cannot <u>conceive</u> <u>that he would wish to harm us</u>. 我无法想象他会想伤害我们。
  ✎ I cannot <u>conceive</u> <u>why you allowed the child to go alone</u>. 我无法理解你为什么让孩子一个人去。
  同义词/搭配：
  **incredible, unbelievable, unimaginable, unthinkable**
  **beyond belief**（习语）
+ **veritable** a. 真正的，货真价实的 **= real**
  英文释义：a word used to emphasize a description of sb. or sth.
  ✎ The area is a <u>veritable</u> paradise for those who love walking and swimming. 对于那些喜欢散步和游泳的人来说，这个地区是一个名副其实的天堂。（褒义）
  ✎ My garden had become a <u>veritable</u> jungle by the time I came back from holiday. 到我度假回来时，我的花园已经变成了名副其实的丛林。（贬义）
  + 字根 **ver = true**
    **<u>ver</u>y** a. 正是的
    ✎ He died in this <u>very</u> room. 他就是在这个房间里死的。
    ✎ At that <u>very</u> moment the phone rang. 就在那一刻，电话铃响了。
    **<u>ver</u>ify** v. 证实，核实
    ✎ His story has <u>been verified</u> by other witnesses. 他的故事已被其他目击者证实。
    ✎ Please <u>verify</u> that there is sufficient memory available before loading the program. 请在加载程序之前核实是否有足够的可用内存。
    **<u>ver</u>dict** n.（陪审团的）裁决
    ✎ After a week the jury had still not reached a <u>verdict</u>. 一周后，陪审团仍未作出裁决。
    **<u>ver</u>acity** n. = truth 真实，真实性
    ✎ Some people questioned the <u>veracity</u> of her story. 有些人质疑她的故事的真实性。

+ **magpie**
  n1. 喜鹊
  n2. 爱饶舌的人 person who chatters a lot
  n3. 爱收集或贮藏东西的人 person who collects or hoards things
  ✎ She had lived in the flat for thirty years and was a veritable <u>magpie</u> at hoarding; ……（本文）
  用动物指代某类人：
  ◇ He is a <u>bear</u>. 他是一个粗鲁的人
  ◇ He is a <u>beast</u>. ~野蛮的人
  ◇ He is a <u>fox</u>. ~狡猾的人
  ◇ He is a <u>snake</u>. ~阴险的人
  ◇ He is a <u>stupid ass</u>. ~缺心眼的人
  ◇ He is a <u>dark horse</u>. ~意外取得成功的人
  ◇ He is a <u>lucky dog</u>. ~幸运的人
  ◇ He is a <u>big fish</u>. ~显赫的人/大人物
  ◇ He is a <u>lame duck</u>. ~任期将满的统治者
  ◇ He is an <u>old goat</u>. ~老色鬼
  ◇ He is an <u>eager beaver</u>. ~勤奋刻苦的人
  用动物指代某类事：
  ✦ black swan 黑天鹅（提出者：Nassim Nicholas Taleb）
  ✦ gray rhino 灰犀牛（提出者：Michele Wucker）
  ✦ 独角兽
+ **toss** v. 抛掷，扔
  英文释义：to throw sth., esp. sth. light, with a quick gentle movement of your hand
  ✎ She crumpled the letter and <u>tossed</u> it into the fire. 她把信揉成一团扔进了火里。
  ✎ …… it seemed as though everything she possessed had <u>been tossed out</u> and turned over and over.（本文）
  ✎ <u>Toss</u> the carrots in some butter before serving. 上菜前把胡萝卜放进黄油里拌一下。
  ✎ <u>tossed</u> green salad 拌好了（调料）的蔬菜沙拉
  **toss and turn** 辗转反侧
  ✎ I was <u>tossing and turning</u> all night.
+ **fussy** a. 神经过敏的，小题大做的；挑剔的
  + a1.（对小事）神经过敏的，小题大做的 nervously active or excited about small things
    ✎ <u>fussy</u> parents 神经过敏的/过分操心的父母
    ✎ The old lady thought he was a <u>fussy</u> creature,……（本文）
  + a2. 挑剔的 giving too much close attention to detail, etc. and therefore difficult to please
    ✎ A lot of small children are <u>fussy</u> eaters. 许多小孩子都挑食。
    **be <u>fussy/ picky/ choosy/ particular</u> about……** 对……很挑剔（作表语）
    ✎ He <u>is</u> very <u>fussy/ picky/ choosy/ particular about</u> the clothes he buys. 他对买的衣服很挑剔。


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **a spot of……** [英] = a small amount of…… 有一点……
  ✎ Shall we stop for <u>a spot of</u> lunch? 我们停下来吃一点午饭好吗？
  **a spot of bother** = some trouble
  ✎ I’m <u>having a spot of</u> bother <u>with</u> <u>my car/ one of my teeth</u>. 我的车/我的一颗牙齿出了点问题。
+ **block** n. 大楼 a large building divided into separate parts
  ◇ a block of flats 公寓楼
  ◇ an office block 办公楼
  ◇ an apartment block [美] 公寓楼
  ✎ Once he landed on the roof of a <u>block of flats</u> and on another occasion, he landed in a deserted car park.（B2L29）
+ **tire** vt. 使疲劳
+ **grow** linking-v. 慢慢变得…… become different quite slowly
  ✎ 我对英语的兴趣随着每一堂课慢慢增长。
  My interest in English grew stronger with every class of the course.
  ✎ 他的自信心随着每一次取得的成功渐渐增长。
  His self-confidence grew greater with every success he achieved.
+ **lift** (BrE.) = **elevator** (AmE) n. 电梯
+ **one’s thoughts <u>are/ were</u> on……** 某人在想着某事，某人的想法/心思都在某事上
  【✔】In the lift her thoughts were on lunch and a good rest; ……（原文）
  【◐】In the lift she <u>was thinking about</u> lunch and a good rest.（较平庸）
  ✎ On my way to the school, <u>my thoughts were on</u> the final examinations. 在去学校的路上，我的思绪都集中在期末考试上。
+ **“in the + 表示感觉的名词” 在句中多作原因状语** 意为：因为……。较正式。 **（<a href="#⚓in the + 表示感觉的名词">🚀L53</a> L56）**
  ✎ In the lift her thoughts were on lunch and a good rest; but when she got out at her own floor, both were forgotten <u>in her sudden discovery (= because she suddenly discovered)</u> that her front door was open.（本文）
  ✎ The Swedes were the first to recognize that public officials like civil servants, police officers, health inspectors or tax-collectors can make mistakes or act over-zealously <u>in the belief (= because they believe)</u> that they are serving the public.（L53）
  ✎ The men of our family waded down through our flooded meadows with boathooks, <u>in the hope of being (= because they hope to be)</u> able to grapple a corner of the raft and pull it out of the current towards our bank.（L56）
  ✎ They leave unwanted objects in drawers, cupboards and attics for years, <u>in the belief (= because they believe)</u> that they may one day need just those very things.（L59）
  ✎ Young men who have reason to fear that they will be killed in battle may justifiably feel bitter <u>in the thought (= because they think)</u> that they have been cheated of the best things that life has to offer.（B4L11）
+ **reprimand…… (for……)** 因为某事而批评某人（多用于上下级之间） **（L31 <a href="#⚓reprimand">🚀L53</a>）**
  ✎ Recognizing who the customer was, the manager was most apologetic and <u>reprimanded</u> the assistant severely.（L31）
  ✎ He may gently <u>reprimand</u> an official or even suggest to parliament that a law be altered.（L53）
  ✎ She was thinking that she must <u>reprimand</u> her home help the next morning <u>for</u> such a monstrous piece of negligence,……（本文）
+ **home help** n.(BrE.) 家务助手 someone who helps ill or old people in their homes with cleaning, cooking etc.
+ **monstrous** a. 巨大的；骇人的 **monster** 怪兽
+ **negligence** n.[U] 疏忽，粗心大意
  ✎ The accident was due to her <u>negligence</u>. 事故是由于她的疏忽（造成的）。
  **negligent** a. 疏忽的，粗心大意的
  **neglect** v. 忽视；疏忽 
+ key
  ◇ **turn** the key in the lock 拧/转钥匙
  ◇ **insert** the key in the lock 插钥匙
  ◇ **<u>remove/ take out</u>** the key from the lock 拔钥匙
+ **follow one’s regular practice** 按照某人习惯性的做法
  ✎ <u>Following my regular practice</u> I write once a month to my son in the States. 按照惯例，我每月都会给在美国的儿子写一封信。
+ **look into sth.** 调查或仔细查看某物 investigate or examine sth.
  ✎ I wrote a letter of complaint and the airline has promised to <u>look into</u> the matter. 我写了一封投诉信，航空公司已答应调查此事。
  ✎ The police are <u>looking into</u> the records of all those involved in the crime. 警方正在调查所有卷入这起犯罪的人的记录。
+ **drawing room** n.(formal or old-fashioned) 客厅，起居室 a room in a large house in which people relax and guests are entertained
  + **室内** 相关词汇（复制自L13）
    **hall** 门厅；衣帽厅（L23）
    **<u>living room/ sitting room/ drawing room</u>** 客厅；起居室 （drawing room 多表示大宅院的豪华的客厅（L58））
    **dining room** 餐厅
    **kitchen** 厨房
    **bathroom** 浴室（也可以表示自己家里的厕所）
    **guestroom** 客房（L24）
    **study** 书房（L52）
    **bedroom** 卧室 **master bedroom** 主卧室
    **storeroom** 储藏室；储物间
    **attic/ loft** 阁楼；顶楼（L59）
    **basement/ cellar** 地下室；地窖（basement 用途广（L58），通常可住人；cellar 多指地窖，多用于窖藏酒、煤等（L49））
    **balcony** 阳台；露台（L58）
+ **confusion** n. 混乱 mess; disorder; chaos
  ✎ Only two stray dogs benefited from all this <u>confusion</u>, for they greedily devoured what was left of the cake.（L33）
+ **over** ad. 在那边 across a distance in a particular direction or at a location
  ✎ He lives <u>over</u> in England. 他住在英国那边。
+ **as clear as <u>day/ daylight/ crystal</u>** 很明显（固定比喻）
  【◐】It was <u>very clear</u> then that……
  【✔】It was <u>as clear as daylight</u> then that……
  相关比喻-像……一样：
  **as clear as mud** 非常不明显
  **as dark as pitch** 一团漆黑
  **as easy as ABC** 非常容易
  **as swift as lightning** 像闪电一般迅捷
  **as cold as ice** 冷冰冰的
  **as straight as an arrow** 像箭一样直（类似中文：笔直的）
  **as strong as a horse** 像马一样强壮（类似中文：壮如牛）
  **as brave as a lion** 像狮子一样勇敢（类似中文：猛如虎）
  **as cunning as a fox** 像狐狸一样狡猾
  **as greedy as a wolf** 像狼一样贪婪
  **as stubborn as a mule** 像骡子一样倔（类似中文：倔驴）
  **as poor as a church mouse** 穷得像教堂里的老鼠一样（穷得叮当响）
+ **force an entry = break in** 强行闯入（固定搭配）
  ✎ The police <u>forced an entry</u> into the building. 警察强行闯入了大楼。
  ✎ There is no signs of <u>forced entry</u>. 没有强行闯入的迹象。（作名词）
+ ┏ **<u>in/ during</u> one’s absence** 某人不在场（代词）
  ┏ **<u>in/ during</u> the absence of sb.**（名词）
  ┗ **in one’s presence** 某人在场
  ┗ **in the presence of sb.**
  【✔】during her absence
  【◐】while she was away
+ 主语要做而未做，用“**to do**”，不用“doing”
  **one’s <u>aim/ purpose</u> is to……** 某人的目标/目的是……
  **one’s dream is to……** 某人的梦想是……
  **one’s plan is to……** 某人的计划是去……
  **one’s <u>hope/ wish</u> is to……** 某人的希望是……
  **one’s <u>advice/ suggestion</u> is to……** 某人的建议是……
  **one’s first <u>impulse/ reaction</u> is to……** 某人的第一个冲动/反应是……
+ **decide + that从句** 多表示：（在考虑之后）认为，断定，~~决定~~
+ **prudent** a. 审慎的，明智的 sensible and careful, esp. by trying to avoid unnecessary risks
  ✎ <u>prudent</u> house buyers 谨慎的购房者
  **it is prudent (for sb.) to do sth.** （对某人来说）做某事是很审慎的
  ✎ <u>It would be prudent to</u> save some of the money. 节省一些钱是审慎的。
  ✎ <u>It might be prudent to</u> get some expert advice first. 首先征求一些专家的意见可能是明智的。
  反义词：
  **rash** a. 轻率的，鲁莽的，不计后果的（L8）
  ✎ Don’t make <u>rash</u> promises. 不要许下轻率的诺言。
  ✎ Despite the new tunnel, there are still a few people who <u>rashly</u> attempt to cross the Pass on foot.（L8）
+ **have (got) sb. with you** 某人与自己在一起 if you have someone with you, they are present with you
  ✎ Luckily I <u>had a friend with me</u> who spoke German. 幸运的是，我有一个会说德语的朋友。
+ **fetch sb. from sth.** 从……把某人接来、叫来或找来
  ✎ Would you mind going to <u>fetch</u> the kids <u>from</u> school? 你介意去学校接孩子们吗？
  ✎ I have to <u>fetch</u> my mother <u>from</u> the railway station. 我得去火车站接我妈妈。
+ **porter**
  + n1.(BrE.) = **doorman** (AmE.) 门房，看门人
    英文释义：someone whose job is to take care of a building and be present at its entrance in order to help visitors
  + n2. 脚夫，搬运工（多见于机场、火车站）
    英文释义：a person whose job is to carry things, especially traveler’s bags at railway stations, airports, etc.
    ✎ She gave her luggage to a <u>porter</u> and showed him her ticket.（L60）
+ **be beginning to do** 渐渐开始
  ✎ It <u>was beginning to</u> get dark. 天慢慢开始变黑了。
  ✎ By now we <u>were beginning to</u> get tired and the rain was falling heavily. 那时我们开始累了，雨下得很大。
  ✎ During the summer, I noticed that the leaves of the tree <u>were beginning to</u> wither.（L54）
+ **tremble** v. 震颤，颤抖（指人指物都可）（L10）
  ✎ Suddenly, there was a slight <u>trembling</u> sound from below, and the captain went down to see what had happened.（L10）
+ **strong** a.（饮料、酒等）浓的，烈性的
  ✎ <u>strong</u> <u>coffee/ tea/ beer/ ……</u> 浓咖啡/浓茶/高度啤酒……
  反义：
  **weak** a.（饮料、酒等）淡的
  ✎ <u>weak</u> <u>coffee/ tea/ beer/ ……</u> 淡咖啡/淡茶/低度啤酒……
+ **<u>keep/ maintain</u> one’s composure** 保持镇静（详见本课单词讲解 <a href="#⚓composure">🚀</a>）
  **lose one’s composure** 失去镇静
  **<u>recover/ regain</u> one’s composure** 恢复镇静
+ 独立主格结构
  【◐】Then, her composure <u>was</u> regained, <u>and</u> she was ready to……（完整句子，其后需用连词连接并列句）
  【✔】Then, her composure regained, she was ready to……（独立主格-突出主句又更简洁）
+ **set <u>out/ off</u> = start <u>out/ off</u>** 动身，出发（不强调出行方式）（L10、L20）
  ✎ Four days after <u>setting out</u>, while the *Titanic* was sailing across the icy waters of the North Atlantic, a huge iceberg was suddenly spotted by a lookout.（L10）
+ **intruder** n. 非法入侵者（尤指为行窃）
  英文释义：someone who illegally enters a building or area, usually in order to steal sth. 
  ✎ The police think the <u>intruder</u> got in through an unlocked window. 警方认为闯入者是通过一扇未上锁的窗户进入的。
  **intrude** v. 打扰，侵扰，干涉（隐私等）
  英文释义：to interrupt someone or become involved in their private affairs in an annoying and unwanted way
  ✎ I don’t wish to <u>intrude</u>, but could I talk to you for a moment? 我无意打扰你，但我能和你谈一下吗？
  **intrude <u>into/ on/ upon</u>……** 侵扰……
  ✎ Employers should not <u>intrude into</u> the private lives of their employees. 雇主不应干涉雇员的私人生活。
  ✎ Civil Rights campaigners say the new laws will <u>intrude on</u> people’s personal freedom. 民权运动领袖表示，新法律将侵犯人们的人身自由。
+ **lurk** v. 潜伏 to wait somewhere quietly and secretly, usually because you are going to do sth. wrong
  ✎ She didn’t see the figure <u>lurking</u> behind the bushes. 她没有看到那个潜伏在灌木丛后面的身影。
+ **go through sth.** 搜寻 to search sth. in order to find sth. in particular（详见L11）
  ✎ The Officer <u>went through</u> the case with great care.（L11）
+ **search for + 搜寻目标** 搜寻……
  **in the search for + 搜寻目标** 在搜寻……的过程中
  ✎ Bad weather is hampering <u>the search for</u> survivors. 恶劣的天气阻碍了对幸存者的搜寻。
  辨：
  **in search of…… = searching for……**
  ✎ go <u>in search of</u> a cheap hotel 去找一家便宜的旅馆
  ✎ Soon the hobby leads to travel, perhaps to a meeting in another town, possibly a trip abroad <u>in search of</u> a rare specimen, for collectors are not confined to any one country.（L59）
+ The chaos was **<u>incredible/ unbelievable/ unimaginable/ unthinkable/ beyond belief</u>**.
+ **sort out**
  1. 从……中挑出来 to separate one type of thing from another
  ✎ I’ve <u>sorted out</u> the papers that can be thrown away. 我已经把可以扔掉的报纸挑出来了。
  1. 将……分类整理好 to arrange or organize sth. that is mixed up or untidy, so that it is ready to be used
  ✎ We need to <u>sort out</u> our camping gear before we go away. 我们需要在出发前分类整理好露营装备。
+ **should have done** 应该做的却没有做（详见L11）
  ✎ You <u>should have declared</u> that. Perfume is not exempt from import duty.（L11）
+ **police inspector** n. 巡官 a police officer of middle rank
  **constable** n. 警察 a British police officer of the lowest rank
+ **tell sb. of sth.** (fml.) 向某人讲述某事 describe an event to sb.
  ✎ He <u>told</u> us <u>of</u> his extraordinary childhood. 他跟我们讲了他不同寻常的童年。
+ **ransack** v. 洗劫 to search a place, making it untidy and causing damage, usually because you are looking for sth.
