  ✎ The house had <u>been ransacked</u> by burglars. 这房子遭到了盗贼的洗劫。
+ **while** 而
  ✎ One man stayed at the wheel <u>while</u> two others with black stockings over their faces jumped out and smashed the window of the shop with iron bars.（L6）
+ **check** v.（用检查或调查的方法）印证、确认
  英文释义：make sure of sth. by examining or investigating it
  **check (that)……** 印证、确认某事物
  ✎ Go and <u>check (that)</u> I’ve locked the windows. 去确认一下我是不是把窗户锁上了。
+ **<u>force/ pick/ break</u>** a lock 撬锁
+ **thereby** ad.(fml.) 因此，由此 with the result that sth. else happens
  **thereby doing sth.** 因此/由此，某事发生了（作结果状语）
  ✎ He became a citizen in 1978, <u>thereby gaining</u> the right to vote. 他于1978年成为公民，从而获得了投票权。
  ✎ Regular exercise strengthens the heart, <u>thereby reducing</u> the risk of heart attack. 定期锻炼可以增强心脏，从而降低心脏病发作的风险。
  **= thus doing**（更通俗）
  ✎ The universities have expanded, <u>thus allowing</u> many more people the chance of higher education. 大学已经扩招，从而让更多的人有机会接受高等教育。
  ✎ They diluted the drug, <u>thus reducing</u> its effectiveness. 他们稀释了药物，从而降低了药效。
  ✎ The merchants began to import corn, <u>thus forcing</u> farmers to cut their prices. 商人开始进口玉米/谷物，迫使农民降价。
+ **<u>skeleton key/ passkey</u>** 万能钥匙
+ **trace** n. 痕迹，踪迹，迹象 a small sign that shows that sb. or sth. was present or existed
  **there is no trace of……** 没有……的痕迹/迹象
  ✎ <u>There was no trace of</u> anyone having entered the room since then. 从那以后就没有人进过房间的痕迹。
+ **bundle** n. 包裹 parcel, package

#### 👾 嵌入式定语从句(Embedded Attributive Clause)  **<a href="#⚓嵌入式定语从句">（🚀L42</a> <a href="#⚓嵌入式定语从句2">🚀L48</a> <a href="#⚓嵌入式定语从句3">🚀L57）</a>**
**既是先行词的后置定语，又是另一个分句结构的宾语**
✎ In this part of the cave, they could hear an insistent booming sound <u>which **they found** was caused by a small waterspout shooting down into a pool from the roof of the cave</u>.（L42）
✎ Turning back down the main street, we quickened our pace and made our way rapidly towards the stream <u>where **we hoped** the boatman was waiting</u>.（L48）
✎ I hired a car the day after landing and bought a comprehensive book of maps, which I found most helpful on the cross-country journey, but <u>which **I did not think** I should need on the last stage</u>.（L57）

+ **entry (into……)** 进入（……）**= entering**（动名词）
  ✎ 老师突然进来把孩子们吓了一跳。
  The children were surprised by the sudden <u>entry</u> of their teacher.
  ✎ 夜色昏暗，谁也没有注意到他们进入了军营。
  It was dark and their <u>entry into</u> the camp had gone unnoticed.
+ **job** n.(infml.) 作案，罪行 a crime, esp. stealing
  ✎ an inside <u>job</u> 内鬼作案
  ✎ He got six months for that last <u>job</u> he did. 他因为最后一桩罪行被判六个月监禁。
+ **creature** 有某种特点的人（尤其用于形容词后）
  英文释义：a person, considered in a particular way (esp. following an adjective)
  ✎ a <u>fussy/ strange/ pathetic/ ……</u> <u>creature</u> 一个小题大做的/奇怪的/可怜的/……家伙
+ **ring <u>sb.🗘up</u>** 给某人打电话
  ✎ As the cry was repeated several times, she ran to tell the manager who promptly <u>rang up</u> the fire brigade.（L35）
  给某人打电话：
  ◇ **<u>ring/ phone</u> <u>sb.🗘up</u>** (BrE.) = **call <u>sb.🗘up</u>** (AmE)
  ◇ **<u>telephone/ phone/ call</u> sb.**
  ◇ **give sb. a call** = **give sb. a ring** (BrE.)
+ **help in sth.** 在某方面帮助
  ✎ Local teachers provided invaluable <u>help in</u> developing the material. 当地教师在编写材料方面提供了宝贵的帮助。
+ **describe…… as……** 把（前者）描述成为是（后者）**<span id="⚓describe2">（🪐）</span>（L10 L17 <a href="#⚓describe">🚀L51</a>）**
  ✎ He <u>described</u> it <u>as</u> ‘a very agreeable situation located within two small hills in the midst of which flowed a great river.’（L17）

---

## **Lesson 59 - Collecting**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>People tend to amass possessions, sometimes without being aware of doing so. Indeed they can have a delightful surprise when they find something useful which they did not know they owned. Those who never have to move house become indiscriminate collectors of what can only be described as clutter. They leave unwanted objects in drawers, cupboards and attics for years, in the belief that they may one day need just those very things. As they grow old, people also accumulate belongings for two other reasons, lack of physical and mental energy, both of which are essential in turning out and throwing away, and sentiment. Things owned for a long time are full of associations with the past, perhaps with relatives who are dead, and so they gradually acquire a value beyond their true worth.

Some things are collected deliberately in the home in an attempt to avoid waste. Among these I would list string and brown paper, kept by thrifty people when a parcel has been opened, to save buying these two requisites. Collecting small items can easily become a mania. I know someone who always cuts sketches out from newspapers of model clothes that she would like to buy if she had the money. As she is not rich, the chances that she will ever be able to afford such purchases are remote; but she is never sufficiently strong-minded to be able to stop the practice. It is a harmless habit, but it litters up her desk to such an extent that every time she opens it, loose bits of paper fall out in every direction.

Collecting as a serious hobby is quite different and has many advantages. It provides relaxation for leisure hours, as just looking at one’s treasures is always a joy. One does not have to go outside for amusement, since the collection is housed at home. Whatever it consists of, stamps, records, first editions of books china, glass, antique furniture, pictures, model cars, stuffed birds, toy animals, there is always something to do in connection with it, from finding the right place for the latest addition, to verifying facts in reference books. This hobby educates one not only in the chosen subject, but also in general matters which have some bearing on it. There are also other benefits. One wants to meet like-minded collectors, to get advice, to compare notes, to exchange articles, to show off the latest find. So one’s circle of friends grows. Soon the hobby leads to travel, perhaps to a meeting in another town, possibly a trip abroad in search of a rare specimen, for collectors are not confined to any one country. Over the years, one may well become an authority on one’s hobby and will very probably be asked to give informal talks to little gatherings and then, if successful, to larger audiences. In this way self-confidence grows, first from mastering a subject, then from being able to talk about it. Collecting, by occupying spare time so constructively, makes a person contented, with no time for boredom.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **amass** vt. 积累，积聚
  ✎ How had he <u>amassed</u> his fortune? 他是如何积累起财富的？
  ✎ For 25 years, Darwin <u>amassed</u> evidence to support his theories. 25年来，达尔文积累了大量证据来支持他的理论。
  **accumulate** vt.&vi. 积累，积聚（L1）
  ✎ <u>accumulate/ amass</u> <u>knowledge/ possessions</u> 积累知识/财富（及物）
  ✎ Debts began to <u>accumulate</u>. 债务开始越积越多。（不及物）
  ✎ However, as the evidence began to <u>accumulate</u>, experts from the Zoo felt obliged to investigate,……（L1）（不及物）
  近义词 - 积累，积聚：
  **collect/ gather**（指物指人都可，及物不及物都可）
  ✎ Dust had <u>collected</u> on the window-sill. 窗台上积满了灰尘。（不及物）
  ✎ I didn’t know what to do with it, so it just sat there <u>collecting</u> dust. 我不知道该怎么办，所以它只是坐在那里积灰。（及物）
  ✎ The darkness is <u>gathering</u>. 夜色渐浓。（不及物）
  ✎ You may as well take these books — they’re just <u>gathering</u> dust on the shelf. 你不妨把这些书拿走——它们一直在书架上积灰。（及物）
  **<u>pile up/ build up</u>**（L33）
  ✎ Meanwhile, the traffic <u>piled up</u> behind.（不及物）（L33）
  ✎ He <u>piled up</u> huge debts. 他背负了巨额的债务。（及物）
  ✎ Traffic is <u>building up</u> on roads into the city. 进城的道路上车子越积越多。
  ✎ The gallery has <u>built up</u> a fine collection of contemporary art. 这家画廊收藏了大量精美的当代艺术品。
+ **indiscriminate** a. 不加选择的
  **be indiscriminate in……** 在某方面不加选择
  ✎ He <u>is indiscriminate in</u> his choice of friends. 他在择友方面不加选择。
  **discriminate** v. 分辨，辨别；歧视
  **discriminate against……** 歧视……
  ✎ <u>discriminate against</u> women 歧视妇女
  ✎ <u>discriminate against</u> ethnic minorities 歧视少数民族
  **discrimination** n. 辨别力；歧视
  ✎ racial <u>discrimination</u> 种族歧视
  ✎ sexual <u>discrimination</u> 性别歧视
  ✎ religious <u>discrimination</u> 宗教歧视
+ **requisite** n. 必需品
  同义词：
  **necessity**
  ✎ daily <u>necessities</u> 日用品
  相关词：
  **prerequisite** 先决条件，前提
+ **mania** n. 狂热，癖好；躁狂症
  **= craze**（crazy 疯狂的）
  ✎ soccer <u>mania/ craze</u> 对足球的狂热
  ✎ fitness <u>mania/ craze</u> 健身热潮
  **maniac** n. 对某方面过分狂热的人，疯子
  ✎ a sex <u>maniac</u> 大色狼，色情狂
  字根 **-mania-**
  **klepto<u>mania</u>** 盗窃癖，盗窃狂
  **pyro<u>mania</u>** 纵火狂
  **megalo<u>mania</u>** 自大狂
  **dipso<u>mania</u>** 酒鬼
  **biblio<u>mania</u>** 书痴（**bibliography** 参考书目，字根 **-bibl(i)- = book 书**）
+ **remote** a. 遥远的；（可能性）微小的（指位置、时间都可）
  ✎ in the <u>remote</u> <u>past/ future</u> 在遥远的过去/未来
  ✎ <u>remote</u> control 遥控器
  ┏ The chances are <u>remote/ slight/ slim/ small</u>. 可能性很小
  ┗ The chances are <u>high/ good</u>. 可能性很大
  ✎ The following day, however, the doctor consoled him by telling him that his <u>chances</u> of being able to leave hospital in time for New Year celebrations <u>were good</u>.（L29）
+ **strong-minded** a. 意志坚强的
  同/近义词：
  **iron-willed** 钢铁般意志力的
  **resolute, determined**
  **stubborn, obstinate** 固执的，倔强的（L41）
  反义词：
  **hesitant** 犹豫不决的，优柔寡断的（**hesitate** 犹豫，迟疑）
+ **verify** v. 证实，核实
  ✎ <u>verify</u> <u>data/ details</u> 证实/核实数据/细节
  近义词辨析：
  **testify** 呈堂作证
  **testify <u>against sb./ in favor of sb.</u>** 出庭作不利于/有利于某人的证词
  **justify** vt. 证明……是正确的/合理的
  ✎ The end <u>justifies</u> the means. 只要目的正确，可以不择手段。（谚语）
+ **contented** a. 心满意足的（作定语、表语皆可）
  ✎ a <u>contented</u> heart 知足的心（定语）
  ✎ a <u>contented</u> smile 满意的微笑（定语）
  ✎ Whenever he returns to this place he is happy and <u>contented</u>. 每当他回到这个地方，他都会感到快乐和满足。（表语）
  **content** a. 满足的，满意的（仅可作表语）
  **be content with…… = be satisfied with……** 对……满意
  **be content to do…… = be satisfied to do……** 做某事很满意
  ┏ He <u>is content with</u> his present job. 他对目前的工作很满意。
  ┗ He <u>is content to</u> stay in his present job. 他满足于继续做现在的工作。
  **satisfied** 满意的；满足的（作定语、表语皆可，无场合限制，不如 content 正式）


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ ┏ **collecting** 强调收藏这种行为
  ┗ **collection** 多表示收藏的东西
+ **tend to do** 往往……，常常……，倾向于……
  同义搭配：
  **have a tendency to do**
  **be inclined to do**
  **be apt to do**
  辨（L13）：
  **intend to do** 打算
  **mean to do**
  **be going to do**
  **plan to do**
  ┏ **have every intention of doing**
  ┗ **have no intention of doing**（反义）（L28）
  ✎ I <u>had no intention of buying</u> one, but I could not conceal the fact that I was impressed by the size of the diamonds.（L28）
+ amass possessions 积累财产（泛指财产）（“财产”详见L32）
  accumulate belongings 积累财产（动产）（本文）
+ ┏ …… <u>without being aware of</u> doing so.（原文）
  ┗ …… <u>without being conscious of</u> doing so.（同义替换）
  ✎ They disregard social conventions <u>without being conscious that</u> they are doing anything extraordinary.（L31）
+ 不知道
  …… **without knowing** so.
  …… **without realizing** so.
  …… **(being) <u>unaware/ unconscious</u> of** doing so.（being 在非谓语动词和独立主格中可省略）
  ✎ He used to sleep during the day and work at night, <u>quite unaware of</u> the fact that he had become the ghost of Endley.（非谓语动词）（L30）
> 仿写第1句
  人们变老时往往睡得更少，有时候自己都没有意识到。
  People tend to sleep less when they get older, sometimes without being aware of doing so.
+ delightful surprise 惊喜交加
  painful joy 苦乐交织
  sweet sorrow 甜蜜的忧伤
  hating love 爱恨交织
  ↳ mixed <u>feelings/ emotions</u> 杂糅的情绪
+ **定语从句的先行词，要用指示代词，不能用人称代词。**（古英语、谚语偶有例外）
+ **move <u>house/ home</u>** [BrE] 搬家
  ✎ We’re <u>moving house/ home</u> next week. 我们下周就要搬家了。
  **move** [AmE] 搬家
  ✎ We’re <u>moving</u> next week. ~
  相关表达：
  **move to……** 搬到……
  ✎ We’re <u>moving to</u> Shanghai. 我们打算搬到上海。（进行时表将来）
  **move in** 搬进来
  ✎ They’ve bought a new house, but it will need a lot of work before they can <u>move in</u>. 他们买了一栋新房子，但在搬进来之前需要做很多工作。
  **move out** 搬出去
  ✎ Her landlord has given her a week to <u>move out</u>. 她的房东给她一星期时间搬出去。
  **<u>up sticks** [英] / **pull up stakes** [美]</u> [口] 搬家（up 作动词）
  ✎ This is the fourth time in five years that we’ve had to <u>up sticks/ pull up stakes</u>. 这是五年来我们第四次不得已的搬家。
+ 被描述为……（被动）
  **be described…… as……** 把（前者）描述成为是（后者） **<a href="#⚓describe">（🚀L51</a> <a href="#⚓describe2">🚀L58）</a>**
  **be called……**
  **be regarded as……** 被看待成……
  **be classified as……** 被归类到……（L27）
  **be branded as……** 被贴上……的标签/烙印（贬义）
+ **unwanted** 不想要的，不需要的
  近义替换：
  **undesirable/ unwelcome**
+ **“in the + 表示感觉的名词” 在句中多作原因状语** **（<a href="#⚓in the + 表示感觉的名词">🚀L53</a> L56 L58）**
  **in the belief** that…… = **because they believe** that……
  ✎ The Swedes were the first to recognize that public officials like civil servants, police officers, health inspectors or tax-collectors can make mistakes or act over-zealously <u>in the belief (= because they believe)</u> that they are serving the public.（L53）
  ✎ The men of our family waded down through our flooded meadows with boathooks, <u>in the hope of being (= because they hope to be)</u> able to grapple a corner of the raft and pull it out of the current towards our bank.（L56）
  ✎ Young men who have reason to fear that they will be killed in battle may justifiably feel bitter <u>in the thought (= because they think)</u> that they have been cheated of the best things that life has to offer.（B4L11）
> 仿写第4句 - “in the + 表示感觉的名词”
  他每天都吃维生素药丸，相信这样对健康有好处。
  He takes vitamin pills every day <u>in the belief that</u> they may benefit his health.
  他给这个女孩子写了一封又一封信希望能赢得芳心。
  He wrote to the girl one letter after another <u>in the hope of</u> winning her heart.
+ **just** ad. 正是
  **very** a. 正是
  ┏ 他正是被警方通缉的那个人。（**wanted** 详见L26）
  ┗ He is <u>just</u> the man wanted by the police.
  ┗ He is the <u>very</u> man wanted by the police.
  ┗ He is <u>just</u> the <u>very</u> man wanted by the police.（两个都用，语气更强）

#### 👾 **“名词+介词+关系代词”引导非限定性定语从句（L32）**
适用情况：定语从句修饰的不是先行词本身，而是先行词相关的东西或先行词的一部分。
✎ 他有两个儿子，其中的一个死于战火。
He has two sons, <u>one of whom</u> died in the war.（比并列句简洁）
✎ She hurried home to feed her cats, <u>one of which</u> had just had kittens. 她匆匆回家喂猫，其中一只刚刚生了小猫。
✎ The most valuable find of all was the ship’s log book, <u>parts of which</u> it was still possible to read.（L32）

+ **sentiment** n.[U] (usu. derog. 通常作贬义) （对怜悯、怀旧等的）情感，多愁善感，感情用事（尤与理智相对）
  英文释义：tender feelings of pity, nostalgia, etc. which may be exaggerated or wrongly directed (contrasted esp. with reason)
  ✎ There’s no room for <u>sentiment</u> in business. 做生意容不得感情用事。
  **sentimentally** ad. 感情方面地，非理智地；多愁善感地；煽情地 **<a href="#⚓sentimentally">（🚀L54）</a>**
  **be sentimentally attached to……** 在感情上对……有依恋
  ✎ She <u>was sentimentally attached to</u> this house, for even though it was far too big for her needs, she persisted in living there long after her husband’s death.（L49）
+ ┏ Things **<u>owned</u> for a long time**…… 被拥有了很长时间（原文）
  ┗ Things **<u>kept/ possessed</u> for a longtime**……（同义替换）
+ ┏ …… full of <u>associations with</u> the past,…… 联系（原文）
  ┗ …… full of <u>connections with</u> the past,……（同义替换）
+ **relative** [C] 亲属
  a close <u>relative</u> 近亲
  a distant <u>relative</u> 远亲
  a <u>direct/ straight</u> <u>relative</u> 直系亲属
  a blood <u>relative</u> 血亲
  one’s own flesh and blood 至亲骨肉
+ **nostalgia** n. 怀旧
+ **gradually, slowly, little by little, bit by bit, by degrees** 逐渐地，慢慢地，一点一点地（L50）
+ ┏ <u>beyond</u> their true worth 超过
  ┗ <u>above/ over</u> their true worth
  ┗ <u>more than</u> their true worth
  ┗ <u>greater than</u> their true value
  ┗ <u>in excess of</u> their true value
  ┏ **appreciate** v. 增值
  ┗ **depreciate** v. 贬值
  ┏ The value of our house has <u>appreciated</u> by 50%. 我们房子的价值已经增值了50%。
  ┗ The value of our house has <u>depreciated</u> by 50%. ~ 贬值 ~
+ **deliberately** ad. 故意地（L27）
  同义词：
  **intentionally, on purpose**
  （intention 目的，意图；intentional 有意的）
  反义词（意外地，偶然地，无预谋地）：
  **accidentally, by accident, by chance, unintentionally, fortuitously**
+ **in an attempt to…… = in order to……** 为了做某事
  ✎ They closed the road <u>in an attempt to</u> reduce traffic in the city. 他们封锁了道路，为了减少城市的车流量。
+ brown paper 牛皮纸
+ list v. 列清单；列举，列数
  ✎ The actors are <u>listed</u> in order of appearance. 演员已经按出场顺序列成了名单。
  ✎ <u>list</u> one’s faults 列举某人的过失
  ✎ <u>list</u> one’s achievements 列举某人的成就
+ **save = avoid** 避免
  **save <u>sth./ doing</u>**
  ✎ Setting down clear rules from the start will <u>save</u> arguments later on. 从一开始就制定清晰的规则将会避免日后的争论。
  ✎ A stitch in time <u>saves</u> nine. 小洞不补，大洞吃苦。（直译：及时缝一针，可避免日后缝九针）（谚语）
  **save sb. <u>sth./ doing sth.</u>** 使某人免于某事/做某事（不愿做的事）（L41）
  ✎ If you lend me some money, it will <u>save</u> me <u>a trip to the bank</u>. 如果你借给我一些钱，我就省得去银行了。
  ✎ If you tell her the news, it will <u>save</u> me <u>calling her</u>. 如果你告诉她这个消息，我就省得给她打电话了。
  ✎ They could <u>be saved</u> <u>so much misery and expense</u> if they chose to live in the city where they rightly belong.（L41）
+ **know** vt. 认识
  ┏ **know <u>of/ about</u>……** 听说……
  ┗ **hear <u>of/ about</u>……**
  ┗ **learn <u>of/ about</u>……**
  ✎ Verrazano, an Italian <u>about whom little is known</u>, sailed into New York Harbour in 1524 and named it Angoulême.（L17）
+ ┏ …… if she <u>had the money</u>.（原文）
  ┗ …… if she could <u>afford them</u>.（近义表达）
  ┗ …… if she could <u>afford such purchases</u>.（**purchases** 要买的东西）（近义表达）
+ ┏ **chances <u>that……/ of……</u> are <u>remote/ slight/ slim/ small</u>** 可能性很小
  ┗ **chances <u>that……/ of……</u> are <u>high/ good</u>** 可能性很大
  **there is little chance of……** 机会很小（chance 不可数）
  ✎ <u>There is little chance of</u> her being able to afford such purchases.（原文同义替换）
+ strong-minded <u>enough</u>（enough 修饰形容词要后置）
+ **practice** 惯例，习惯，习俗，通常的做法，惯常做的事
  ✎ On the other hand, your stomach would turn at the idea of frying potatoes in animal fat — the normally accepted <u>practice</u> in many northern countries.（L23）
+ **litter (up)……** 杂乱地堆满某地（up 强调堆满）
  **be <u>littered/ cluttered</u> with……** 杂乱地堆满了……（L28？，L39，L46）
  ✎ The garden <u>was</u> soon <u>littered with</u> chunks of metal which had once made up a lawn mower.（L46）
+ **in all directions = in every direction** 向四面八方
+ **quite**（L8）
  + ad. 相当地，颇为（程度副词）
  + ad. 完全，截然，彻底 **= completely = totally**
    ✎ In winter, however, life at the monastery is <u>quite different</u>.（L8）
+ **one** 可泛指“人们”，但毕竟是形式是单数，注意与谓语动词对应。
+ **house**
  + v. 为某人提供住处
    ✎ The refugees <u>have been fed, clothed</u> and <u>housed by</u> welfare organizations around the world. 世界各地的福利组织为难民提供了食物、衣服和住所。
    **= accommodate** v. 为某人提供住处，容纳
    ✎ The hotel can <u>accommodate</u> 600 guests. 这家酒店可容纳600位客人。
  + v. 储存，收藏（派生义）
    ✎ The Palace Museum <u>houses</u> the biggest collection of antiques in China. 故宫博物院收藏了中国最大量的古董。
+ ┏ Whatever it <u>consists of</u>,…… 由……构成（原文）
  ┗ Whatever it <u>is made up of</u>,……
  ┗ Whatever it <u>is composed of</u>,……
  ┗ Whatever it <u>comprises</u>,……
+ **in connection with……** (fml.) 关于……（类似 about）
  同义替换 (fml.)：
  **concerning……**
  **regarding……**
  **respecting……**
  **relating to……**
  ✎ I am writing to you <u>in connection with</u> your job application. 关于你最近工作申请，我正为此写信给你。
+ **reference book** [C] 参考书
  **bibliography** 参考书目（字根 **-bibl(i)- = book 书**；**-graph- = to write (写) 或 writing (记录)**）
+ **have…… bearing on……** 与……有某种关系
  ✎ Exercise <u>has a direct bearing on</u> how healthy you are. 锻炼身体跟你的健康状况有直接关系。
  ✎ What he said <u>had not much bearing on</u> the problem. 他的话与这个问题没有多大关系。
  ✎ His private life <u>has no bearing on</u> his competence as a manager. 他的私生活与他作为经理的能力无关。
  ┏ …… which <u>have some bearing on</u> it.（原文）
  ┗ …… which <u>have some connection with</u> it.（同义替换）
  ┗ …… which <u>have some relationship with</u> it.（同义替换）
+ **meet** v. 结识……
  英文释义：get to know, get acquainted with
  ✎ I’d like you to <u>meet</u> one of my best friends, Peter. 我想让你结识一下我最好的朋友之一，彼得。
  ✎ You can stretch your legs on the spacious decks, play games, <u>meet</u> interesting people and enjoy good food……（L44）
+ **compare notes (with sb.)** 交换意见、交换观点、交流心得 exchange ideas or opinions
  ✎ We saw the play separately and <u>compared notes</u> afterwards. 我们分开看了这出戏，然后交换了意见。
  ✎ Leading scientists got together in Paris to <u>compare notes</u> on current research. 顶尖科学家齐聚巴黎，就当前的研究交换意见。
+ **show off** 炫耀
  ✎ She raised her wrist, <u>showing off</u> a sparkling diamond bracelet. 她抬起手腕，炫耀着一只闪闪发光的钻石手镯。
+ **find** 被发现的人或物，~~发现~~（褒义）（L32）
  ✎ The restaurant was a real <u>find</u>. 这家餐馆真是个好去处。
  ✎ My new secretary was a marvelous <u>find</u>. 我的新秘书是个了不起的发现。
  ✎ The most valuable <u>find</u> of all was the ship’s log book, parts of which it was still possible to read.（L32）
+ **circle** 圈子，圈层，阶层，界
  ✎ in political <u>circles</u> 政界
  ✎ in legal <u>circles</u> 法律界
  ✎ in literary <u>circles</u> 文艺界
+ **in search of…… = searching for……** 寻找
  ✎ Scientists are <u>in search of</u> a cure for the disease. 科学家们正在寻找治疗这种疾病的方法。
+ **<u>may/ might/ could</u> well** 可能（well 加强语气）
  英文释义：used to say that sth. is likely to happen or is likely to be true
  ✎ What you say <u>may well</u> be true. 你说的很可能是真的。
  ✎ You could try the drugstore, but it <u>might well</u> be closed by now. 你可以试试杂货店，但现在很可能已经关门了。
+ **authority <u>on</u>……** 某方面的权威
  ✎ Yuan Longping is a leading authority <u>on</u> hybrid rice. 在杂交水稻方面袁隆平是首屈一指的权威。
  同义表达：
  **expert <u>in/ on</u>**
+ **gathering** n. 人群，聚会 a group of people meeting together
  ✎ a <u>social/ family</u> <u>gathering</u> 社交/家庭聚会
  ✎ a <u>gathering</u> of religious leaders 宗教领袖的聚会
+ Over the years, <u>one^主句主语^</u> may well become an authority on one’s hobby and will very probably be asked to give informal talks to little gatherings and then, <u>if (he/ one is) successful</u>, to larger audiences.（原文补全-状语从句中，主语和be动词同时省略）

---

## **Lesson 60 - Too early and too late**
### **课文原文** [🌏](#第三册目录)
<font color=gray size=4>Punctuality is a necessary habit in all public affairs in civilized society. Without it, nothing could ever be brought to a conclusion; everything would be in a state of chaos. Only in a sparsely-populated rural community is it possible to disregard it. In ordinary living, there can be some tolerance of unpunctuality. The intellectual, who is working on some abstruse problem, has everything coordinated and organized for the matter in hand. He is therefore forgiven if late for a dinner party. But people are often reproached for unpunctuality when their only fault is cutting things fine. It is hard for energetic, quick-minded people to waste time, so they are often tempted to finish a job before setting out to keep an appointment. If no accidents occur on the way, like punctured tyres, diversions of traffic, sudden descent of fog, they will be on time. They are often more industrious, useful citizens than those who are never late. The over-punctual can be as much a trial to others as the unpunctual. The guest who arrives half an hour too soon is the greatest nuisance. Some friends of my family had this irritating habit. The only thing to do was ask them to come half an hour later than the other guests. Then they arrived just when we wanted them.

If you are catching a train, it is always better to be comfortably early than even a fraction of a minute too late. Although being early may mean wasting a little time, this will be less than if you miss the train and have to wait an hour or more for the next one; and you avoid the frustration of arriving at the very moment when the train is drawing out of the station and being unable to get on it. An even harder situation is to be on the platform in good time for a train and still to see it go off without you. Such an experience befell a certain young girl the first time she was travelling alone.

She entered the station twenty minutes before the train was due, since her parents had impressed upon her that it would be unforgivable to miss it and cause the friends with whom she was going to stay to make two journeys to meet her. She gave her luggage to a porter and showed him her ticket. To her horror he said that she was two hours too soon. She felt in her handbag for the piece of paper on which her father had written down all the details of the journey and gave it to the porter. He agreed that a train did come into the station at the time on the paper and that it did stop, but only to take on mail, not passengers. The girl asked to see a timetable, feeling sure that her father could not have made such a mistake. The porter went to fetch one and arrived back with the station master, who produced it with a flourish and pointed out a microscopic ‘o’ beside the time of the arrival of the train at his station; this little ‘o’ indicated that the train only stopped for mail. Just as that moment the train came into the station. The girl, tears streaming down her face, begged to be allowed to slip into the guard’s van. But the station master was adamant: rules could not be broken. And she had to watch that train disappear towards her destination while she was left behind.</font>


### 🌻 **单词讲解**
+ **punctuality** n.[U] 守时，准时
  ✎ <u>Punctuality</u> is the soul of business. 守时是做事的灵魂。（谚语）
  反义词：
  **procrastination** n.[U] 拖延
  ✎ <u>Procrastination</u> is the thief of time. 拖延是时间的窃贼。（谚语）
  **punctual** a. 准时的
  **punctually** ad. 准时地
  ✎ We have learnt to expect that trains will be <u>punctual</u>.（L37）
  ✎ Sure enough, Rastus arrived <u>punctually</u> at seven o’clock that evening.（L19）
  字根 **-punct- = point**
  **puncture** vt.&vi. 把某物扎破
  **acupuncture** 针灸
  **punctuate** vt.&vi. 给句子加标点
  ✎ The <u>tyre [英]/ tire [美]</u> <u>punctured</u>. 车胎被扎了。（不及物）
  ✎ A nail <u>punctured</u> our <u>tyre/ tire</u>. 一个钉子扎破了我们的轮胎。（及物）
  ✎ a <u>flat/ burst/ punctured</u> <u>tyre/ tire</u> 一个没气的/爆了的/被扎了的车胎（作形容词）
  ✎ The children have not yet learned to <u>punctuate</u> correctly. 孩子们还没有学会正确地加标点。（不及物）
  ✎ The transcription of his speech must <u>be punctuated</u>. 他的演讲抄写稿必须被加上标点符号。（及物）
+ **rural** a. 农村的（中性）
  英文释义：connected with or like the countryside
  <u>rural</u> <u>areas/ accents</u> 农村地区/口音
  ✎ Only in a sparsely-populated <u>rural</u> community is it possible to disregard it.（本文）
  **pastoral** a. 田园的（褒义）（L41）
  英文释义：showing country life or the countryside, especially in a romantic way
  ✎ a <u>pastoral</u> <u>scene/ poem/ painting</u> 一幅田园风光/诗/画
  ✎ This idyllic <u>pastoral</u> scene is only part of the picture.（L41）
  相关词：
  **urban** 城市的
  **suburban** 郊区的；**suburb** 郊区
  **metropolitan** a. 大城市的，大都会的；**metropolis** n. 大城市，大都会
  **cosmopolitan** a. 国际性大都市的；**cosmopolis** n. 国际性大都市
+ **intellectual** n. 知识分子；a. 智力的（L27）
  相关词辨析：
  **intellectual** 智力方面的 ✎ <u>intellectual</u> development 智力的发展
  **intelligent** 聪明的，智商高的 ✎ <u>intelligent</u> beings 智慧生物
  **mental** 脑力上的 ✎ <u>mental</u> work 脑力工作
  **spiritual** 精神的 ✎ <u>spiritual</u> civilization 精神文明 
+ **reproach** v. 责备
  英文释义：criticize sb. or oneself, esp. for failing to do sth.
  **reproach sb. for sth.** 强调因为没有做该做的事而指责（偏文言）（L31）
  ✎ The General <u>was reproached</u> by his allies <u>for</u> failing to inform them of his plans. 将军因未将其计划告知盟友而受到指责。
  ✎ I have nothing to <u>reproach</u> myself <u>for</u>. 我没有什么可自责的。
  ✎ But people <u>are</u> often <u>reproached for</u> unpunctuality when their only fault is cutting things fine.（本文）
  相关搭配回顾-批评（L16、L31）：
  **criticize sb. for sth.** 因为某事而批评某人（正式地，无感情色彩）
  **censure sb. for sth.** 严厉地批评某人（措辞重，不一定有感情色彩）
  **<u>reprimand/ rebuke</u> sb. for sth.** 因为某事而批评某人（多用于上下级之间的责备）（L31）
  **accuse sb. of sth.** 指控，控告/（愤怒地）指责某人（L16）
  **scold sb. for sth.** 因为某事指责某人（多用于长辈对晚辈）
  **<u>blame sb. for sth. / blame sth. on sb.</u>** 强调把某事归咎于某人，强调某人应该为此负责
  **condemn A <u>for/ as</u> B** 因为B而谴责A / 把A谴责为是B（大家一致地批评）
+ **fraction** n. 分数；一小部分，些微
  **a fraction of……** ……的一小部分
  ✎ I bought these shoes at <u>a fraction of</u> its original price. 我以原价的一小部分买了这双鞋。
  **a fraction of <u>a second/ a minute/ an inch/ ……</u>**
  不到一秒钟/一分钟/一英寸/……（固定搭配）
  ✎ She hesitated for <u>a fraction of a second</u> before answering. 她犹豫了不到一秒钟就回答了。
  ✎ The car stopped within <u>a fraction of an inch</u> of the wall. 汽车在离墙不到一英寸的地方停了下来。
  ✎ If you are catching a train, it is always better to be comfortably early than even <u>a fraction of a minute</u> too late.（本文）
  **proportion** n. 比例 **<a href="#⚓proportion">（🚀L54）</a>**
  ┏ **a <u>high/ large</u> proportion of……** 大多数……，大部分……（指人指事物都可，跟可数不可数都可）
  ┗ **a <u>small/ tiny</u> proportion of……** 少数……，一小部分……
  ┏ **a <u>high/ large</u> percentage of……** ~
  ┗ **a <u>small/ tiny</u> percentage of……** ~


### 🕹️ **课文讲解**
+ **public affairs** n. 公众事务
  英文释义：issues and questions about social, economic, political or business activities, etc. that affect ordinary people in general
+ **civilized** 文明的
  civilized society 文明社会
  civilized world 文明世界
  ✎ Terrorism is a threat to the <u>civilized world</u>. 恐怖主义是对文明世界的一种威胁。
> 仿写第1句
  礼节（politeness/ courtesy）是文明社会所有公众事务中一个必备的习惯。
  <u>Politeness/ Courtesy</u> is a necessary habit in all public affairs in civilized society.

+ ┏ <u>Without it</u>, nothing <u>could</u> ever be brought to a conclusion; everything <u>would</u> be in a state of chaos.（原文-介词短语）
  ┗ <u>If we didn’t have it</u> nothing <u>could</u> ever be brought to a conclusion; everything <u>would</u> be in state of chaos.（if从句）
  介词短语替换if从句：
  ┏ <u>Without it</u> we <u>could</u> not make a living.（L56）
  ┗ <u>If we didn’t have it</u> we <u>could</u> not make a living.
+ ever 常放在否定句中，加强语气
  ✎ Nothing <u>ever</u> seems to upset him. 从来没有任何事情能让他心烦意乱。
+ **bring sth. to a conclusion** 使某事结束，~~得出结论~~（L36）
  ✎ In the nineteenth century, a novelist would <u>bring his story to a conclusion</u> by presenting his readers with a series of coincidences — most of them wildly improbable.（L36）
  **<u>draw/ come to/ reach</u> a conclusion** 得出结论
  ✎ This trend began during the Second World War, when several governments <u>came to the conclusion</u> that the specific demands that a government wants to make of its scientific establishment cannot generally be foreseen in detail.（考研英译汉）
  这种趋势始于第二次世界大战期间，当时一些国家的政府得出结论：政府要向科研机构提出的具体要求通常是无法详尽预见的。
+ **chaos** 混乱状态（L33） **disorder; mess; confusion**
  ✎ Only two stray dogs benefited from all this <u>confusion</u>, for they greedily devoured what was left of the cake.（L33）
  **in (a state of) chaos** 处于一片混乱（状态）
  ✎ 在老师不在的时候，班里处于一片混乱状态。
  In the absence of the teacher, the class was <u>in a state of chaos</u>.
+ **“only + 状语”位于句首，引起部分倒装**（详见L5、L37）
  意为：只有……才……（非时间状语）；直到……才……（时间状语）
+ **populate** v. （人口）生活于，居住于（L47）
  ┏ <u>densely/ thickly</u> populated 人口稀少的
  ┗ <u>sparsely/ thinly</u> populated 人口稠密的
+ **disregard** v. 漠视，不顾，不理睬（详见L31）
  ✎ They <u>disregard</u> social conventions without being conscious that they are doing anything extraordinary.（L31）
+ **living** 
  n1. 生计 ✎ <u>make/ earn</u> a <u>living</u> 谋生活
  n2. 生活；生活方式 ✎ <u>plain/ luxurious</u> <u>living</u> 简朴/奢侈的生活 ✎ the art of <u>living</u> 生活的艺术
+ 无灵主语的翻译
  There can’t be any tolerance of this brutality.
  【✔】没有任何人能够容忍这种暴行。（人称主语）
  【✘】不会有任何的对这种残忍行为的容忍。
+ **单数名词 + 定冠词 the**：既可能是特指，也可能是类指。
  类指 **<a href="#⚓类指">（🚀L42）</a>**
+ **work on <u>sth./ doing</u>** 致力于……
  ✎ John is still <u>working on</u> the new book. 约翰还在致力于写这本新书。
  ✎ The couple need to <u>work on</u> improving their relationship. 这对夫妇需要努力改善他们的关系。
+ abstruse a. 深奥的；难理解的 difficult to understand
+ some 的翻译
  ┏ some + 可数名词复数/不可数名词：**一些……**
  ┗ some + 单数名词：**某个……**
+ **have sth. done**（L2）
  ① 请某人做某事
  ✎ I’m going to <u>have my hair cut</u> this weekend. 我周末要去理发。
  ② 表示某种(不愉快的)遭遇/经历
  ✎ He <u>had his watch stolen</u>. 他的表被人偷了。
  ③ 主语本身做某事（本文）（需根据上下文判断）
  ✎ By this time, a Lancaster bomber in reasonable condition was rare and worth rescuing. The French authorities <u>had the plane packaged and moved ^含义①^</u> in parts back to France. Now a group of enthusiasts are going to <u>have the plane restored ^含义③^</u>.（B2L66）
+ **the <u>job/ task/ matter</u> in hand** 手头的工作/任务/事情（固定搭配）
  ✎ Could you just concentrate on <u>the job in hand</u>? 你能集中精力做手头的工作吗？
  ✎ As <u>the matter in hand</u> was urgent, we dealt with it at once. 由于手头的事情很紧急，我们立即处理了。
  **prep. + hand** 固定搭配（hand 通常作不可数）：
  **at hand** 在手边；某个日期快到了
  ✎ I always keep a dictionary close <u>at hand</u>. 我总是把字典放在手边。
  ✎ My birthday is near <u>at hand</u>. 我的生日快到了。
  **by hand** 用手
  ✎ The signature must be made <u>by hand</u>. 签名必须亲笔签名。
  **on hand** 可以得到的，有空的，有时间的 **= available**
  ✎ They are always <u>on hand</u> whenever you need them. 只要你需要，它们总是有空。
  **off hand** 立刻，立即，马上 **= immediately**
  ✎ I can’t remember his phone number <u>off hand</u>. 我记不起他的电话号码了。

#### 👾 **状语从句的省略（L5）**
**状语从句中如果同时满足以下两个条件，则可同时省略状语从句的主语和其后的 be 动词。**
**1. 状语从句的主语与主句主语一致。**
**2. 状语从句的谓语包含 be 动词。**
↓ <u>He</u> is therefore forgiven if <u>he is</u> late for a dinner party.（条件状语从句）
↳ <u>He</u> is therefore forgiven if late for a dinner party.（原文）
✎ 
↓ <u>Metals</u> expand when <u>they</u> <u>are</u> heated and contract when <u>they</u> <u>are</u> cooled.（时间状语从句）
↳ <u>Metals</u> expand when heated and contract when cooled.
金属当被加热时会膨胀，当被冷却时会收缩。
✎ 
↓ <u>Francis Preston Blair Jr.</u>, although <u>he</u> <u>was</u> born in Kentucky, lived and practiced in Missouri.（让步状语从句）（托福真题）
↳ <u>Francis Preston Blair Jr.</u>, although born in Kentucky, lived and practiced in Missouri.
小弗朗西斯尽管出生于肯塔基州，但生活和工作于密苏里州。（practice 指律师或医生持执照工作，而非“练习”）
✎ 
↓ <u>Judges</u>, however wise or eminent <u>they are</u>, are human and can make mistakes.
↳ <u>Judges</u>, however wise or eminent, are human and can make mistakes.（L35）
✎ 
↓ While <u>he was</u> on a walking tour with his wife, <u>he</u> stopped to talk to a workman.
↳ While on a walking tour with his wife, <u>he</u> stooped to talk to a workman.（L36）

**<font color=red>例外：</font>** 状语从句的主语是虚指的主语 **it** 时，那么 it 和其后的 be 动词可省略，**主语可不与主句主语统一**。
✎ We’ll resolve the Taiwan issue with peaceful means <u>when (it is) ever possible</u>, with force <u>when (it is) necessary</u>. 我们将尽可能以和平手段解决台湾问题，必要时以武力解决。（百度翻译不给翻😶）
+ **cut things fine** 时间不留余地，掐钟点
  ✎ He <u>cut things fine</u> by reaching the classroom only 20 seconds before the bell rang. 他在铃响前20秒掐点到了教室。
+ **<u>be/ feel</u> tempted to do** 很想……
  ✎ I <u>feel tempted to</u> take a day off. 我很想请一天假。
  ✎ Several times since, she has <u>been tempted to</u> ring him up. Her pride, however, would not let her to do so. 从那以后，她几次想给他打电话。然而，她的自尊心不允许她这样做。
+ **appointment** 约会（通常指公事；**date** 通常指情人）
  ◇ have an <u>appointment</u> 有约
  ◇ make an <u>appointment</u> 订约
  ◇ keep an <u>appointment</u> 赴约
  ◇ cancel an <u>appointment</u> 取消约会
  ◇ break an <u>appointment</u> 爽约
+ a <u>flat/ burst/ punctured</u> <u>tyre/ tire</u> 一个没气的/爆了的/被扎了的车胎
+ **diversion** n.[BrE] = detour [AmE]（交通）改道
  英文释义：a different way that traffic is sent when the usual roads are closed
  ✎ They turned back because of traffic <u>diversions</u>. 他们因为交通改道而折返。
+ ┏ **<u>come down/ descend</u>** v. 下雾 **descent** n.
  ✎ A dense fog <u>came down/ descended</u> in the afternoon. 下午下起了浓雾。
  ┗ **<u>lift/ clear/ disperse</u>** v. 雾散
  ✎ The fog had <u>lifted/ cleared/ dispersed</u> by late morning. 临近中午，大雾散了。
+ …… **those** who are never late.
  **当代英语中，定语从句的先行词，通常用指示代词，而非人称代词。**
+ **be a trail to sb.** 令某人头疼讨厌
✎ She <u>was a trail to</u> her parents when she was younger. 她年轻时挺让父母讨厌/头疼的。
+ **as much as……** 和……一样；就等于……
  ✎ That is <u>as much as</u> to say I am a liar. 这就等于说我是个骗子。
  ✎ I hope you have <u>as much</u> fun <u>as</u> I did. 我希望你和我一样开心。
  ✎ He is <u>as much</u> a bore <u>as</u> his father. 他和他父亲一样令人厌烦。
  ✎ She is <u>as much</u> a beauty <u>as</u> her mother. 她和她妈妈一样漂亮。
+ ┏ **…… too <u>early/ soon</u>** 早了……
  ✎ He arrived <u>ten minutes too early</u>. 他早到了十分钟。
  ┗ **…… too late** 晚了……
  ✎ He arrived <u>ten minutes too late</u>. 他晚到了十分钟。
+ **nuisance** n. 令人讨厌的人或事
  英文释义：a thing, person or situation that is annoying or causes trouble or problems
  ✎ I don’t want to be a <u>nuisance</u> so tell me if you want to be alone. 我不想成为一个令人讨厌的家伙，所以你要是想一个人呆着你就告诉我。
+ **动词不定式作表语时，若前面出现了实义动词“do”，则常去掉“to”**
  ✎ All I have to <u>do</u> is <u>(to) dream</u>. 只有寻梦去/我所要做的就是做梦。（歌曲名）
  ✎ The best thing you can <u>do</u> now is <u>(to) write</u> her an apology. 你现在能做的最好的事情就是给她写一封道歉信。
  ✎ All I wanted was <u>to help</u> him. 我所有想做的就是去帮助他。
  ✎ The only way that they can preserve their history is <u>to recount</u> it as sagas — legends handed down from one generation of story-tellers to another.（B4L1）
  **动词不定式作“except/but”的宾语时，若前面出现了实义动词“do”，则常去掉“to”**
  ✎ They <u>did</u> nothing <u>but/ except</u> <u>(to) complain</u>. 他们除了抱怨什么也没做。
  ✎ I’ve <u>done</u> everything you wanted <u>but/ except</u> <u>(to) make</u> the beds. 除了铺床，我已经做了你要求的所有事。
  ✎ We have no choice <u>but/ except</u> <u>to wait</u> here. 我们除了在这里等待，别无选择。
+ catch a <u>train/ bus/ plane</u> 赶火车/公交/飞机
+ **a fraction of <u>a second/ a minute/ an inch/ ……</u>**
  不到一秒钟/一分钟/一英寸/……（固定搭配）（详见本课单词讲解）
+ **比较状语从句的省略**
  Although being early may mean wasting a little time, <u>this will be</u> less than <u>(it will be)</u> if you miss the train and have to wait an hour or more for the next one; ……（原文补全）
  ✎ 
  ↓ <u>He’s</u> never more annoying than <u>(he is)</u> when he’s trying to help.
  ↳ <u>He’s</u> never more annoying than when he’s trying to help.
  他没有比试图帮忙时更令人烦的了。
  ✎ 
  ↓ Sometimes <u>patients are</u> more depressed six months later than <u>(they are)</u> when they first hear the bad news.
  ↳ Sometimes <u>patients are</u> more depressed six months later than when they first hear the bad news.
  有时患者在六个月后比第一次听到坏消息时更抑郁。
+ ┏ **<u>pull/ draw</u> out of the station** 出站（L28）
  ┗ **<u>pull/ draw</u> <u>in/ into the station</u>** 进站
  ✎ The train slowly <u>drew in/ drew into the station</u>. 火车慢慢地进站了。
+ **in good time (for sth.)** [BrE] （为了某事）早早就……
  ✎ There wasn’t much traffic so we got there <u>in good time</u>. 路上车不多，所以我们早早就到了那里。
  ✎ He arrived <u>in good time for dinner</u>. 他早早就来吃晚饭了。
+ **befall** (befell - befallen) 不幸的事降临到…… **<a href="#⚓befall">（🚀L56）</a>**
  **= overtake/ happen to** 
  ✎ A great misfortune <u>befell</u> him. 他遭遇了巨大的不幸。
  ✎ We know instinctively, just as beekeepers with their bees, that misfortune might <u>overtake</u> us if the important events of our lives were not related to it.（L56）
+ **due**
  + a1. 到期的，到时间的
    ✎ When is your baby <u>due</u>? 你的孩子什么时候出生？
    ✎ The train is <u>due (in)</u> at 8:00. 火车八点钟进站。
    ✎ M: It says here the next train <u>is due in</u> at 6:30.
    W: I know, but I don’t know whether I can make that one. I’d rather call you from the station than have you waiting around for an hour.
    Q: What does the woman imply?
    Answer: She isn’t sure which train she’ll be on.（托福听力真题）
  + a2. 适当的
    ✎ after <u>due</u> consideration 经过适当考虑
    反义词：
    **undue/ unduly** 过度的/过度地
    ✎ They are either unduly optimistic or <u>unduly</u> pessimistic.（L12课后题-1c）
    ✎ While the quality of legal journalism varies greatly, there is an <u>undue</u> reliance amongst many journalists on interpretations supplied to them by lawyers. While comment and reaction from lawyers may enhance stories, it is preferable for journalists to rely on their own notions of significance and make their own judgments. 
    尽管有关法律方面的新闻报道的质量差异很大，很多记者过分地依赖于律师提供给他们的解释。尽管来自于律师的评论和反馈可能会改善新闻报道的质量，但是记者应该依赖于自己对于重要性的理解以及亲自做出判断。（2007考研-英译汉）
+ ┏ **impress sth. <u>on/ upon</u> sb.** 让某人铭记某事
  ┗ **impress <u>on/ upon</u> sb. sth.**
  ✎ Father <u>impressed on</u> me the importance of hard work. 父亲让我牢记了努力工作的重要性。（Father 作不可数，首字母大写，表示对家庭成员的称谓，无属格和单复数变化）
  ✎ I had always <u>impressed upon</u> the children that if they worked hard they would succeed in life. 我总是让孩子们牢记，如果他们努力工作，他们就会在生活中取得成功。
+ the friends <u>with **whom** she was going to stay</u>
  **在书面语中，如果关系代词作介词的宾语，通常把介词放到关系代词前面而非句中。**
+ **cause sb. to do** 使得某人做某事
+ **make a journey** 到某地去（未必指旅行）
+ **to one’s + 感官词** 使某人……的是
  ✎ To her horror…… 让她惊恐的是……（本文）
+ **feel for……** 摸着找……
  ✎ She <u>felt</u> in her bag <u>for</u> a pencil. 她在包里摸索着找铅笔。
  ✎ I <u>felt for</u> the switch on the wall and turned it on. 我摸着找墙上的开关，并把它打开。
+ **助动词 do/does/did + 谓语动词**：加强语气
+ **take on……** 上（货/乘客等）
  ✎ The bus stopped to <u>take on</u> more passengers. 公共汽车停下来以搭载更多的乘客。
  ✎ The ship <u>took on</u> more fuel here. 船在这里加上了更多的燃料。
+ **timetable [BrE], schedule [AmE]** 时间表，日程表，课程表，行程表（L37）
  ✎ <u>train/ railway[BrE]/ railroad[AmE]</u> ~ 列车时刻表
  ✎ <u>college/ school</u> ~ 大学/学校课程表
  ✎ <u>exam/ examination</u> ~ 考试日程
+ **do sth. with a flourish** 为了引起注意而用较大的动作自信地潇酒地做某事
  ✎ The waiter handed me the menu <u>with a flourish</u>. 服务员自信潇洒地把菜单递给了我。
+ **<u>break/ violate</u> rules** 打破/违反规则
  **<u>ignore/ disregard</u> rules** 漠视规则
  **<u>make/ formulate/ establish/ lay down</u> rules** 制定规则
  **<u>obey/ comply with/ abide by/ observe</u> rules** 服从/遵守规则
+ **leave <u>sb./ sth. 🗘 behind</u>** 留下（不带走）
  ✎ Don’t <u>leave me behind</u>! 别丢下我！


## 结束
